# NPC Deep Lore


# Rulers and Major Leaders
---

## King Aldric IV Thandris
**"The mountain bows to no one—neither shall we."**

### Basic Information
- **Race:** Human
- **Age:** 52
- **Location:** Kaer Thandros, The Iron Palace
- **Role:** High King of Thaldros (Western Continent)
- **Alignment:** Lawful Neutral
- **Class:** Fighter 15 / Noble Background

### Physical Description
Tall and powerfully built (6'4", 220 lbs), with broad shoulders and a commanding presence. Steel-gray hair cut short, kept beard neat and trimmed. Deep-set brown eyes that miss nothing. Weathered face with a scar across his left cheek from a border skirmish in his youth. Always stands with perfect military posture.

### Stat Block
```
Medium Humanoid (Human), Lawful Neutral

Armor Class: 20 (plate armor +2, shield +2, defense fighting style)
Hit Points: 165 (15d10 + 75)
Speed: 30 ft.

STR: 18 (+4)  DEX: 12 (+1)  CON: 20 (+5)
INT: 14 (+2)  WIS: 16 (+3)  CHA: 16 (+3)

Saving Throws: Str +9, Con +10, Wis +8
Skills: Athletics +9, History +7, Insight +8, Intimidation +8, Perception +8, Persuasion +8
Damage Resistances: Bludgeoning, piercing, slashing from nonmagical attacks (indomitable)
Senses: Passive Perception 18
Languages: Common, Dwarvish, Draconic, Elvish
Challenge Rating: 15 (13,000 XP)

ABILITIES:
Action Surge (2/Rest): Can take one additional action on his turn.
Second Wind (1/Rest): Bonus action to regain 1d10+15 hit points.
Indomitable (3/Rest): Can reroll a failed saving throw.
Extra Attack (3): Can attack three times when taking the Attack action.

SPECIAL FEATURES:
The King's Authority: Has advantage on Intimidation and Persuasion checks when acting in official capacity.
Mountain's Endurance: Has advantage on saving throws against exhaustion and environmental hazards.
Veteran Commander: Allies within 30 feet gain +2 to attack rolls and saving throws against being frightened.

LEGENDARY RESISTANCE (3/Day): If he fails a saving throw, he can choose to succeed instead.

ACTIONS:
Multiattack: Makes three melee attacks or two ranged attacks.

Thrandil's Edge (Longsword +3): Melee Weapon Attack: +12 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d8+10 slashing damage (1d10+10 versatile), plus 2d6 radiant damage. 
Special: Glows in presence of betrayers. Once per day can cast Zone of Truth (DC 16).

Shield Bash: Melee Weapon Attack: +9 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d4+4 bludgeoning damage, target must succeed DC 17 Strength save or be knocked prone.

Heavy Crossbow: Ranged Weapon Attack: +6 to hit, range 100/400 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d10+1 piercing damage.

REACTIONS:
Parry: Adds +4 to AC against one melee attack that would hit him.
Protect the Realm: When an ally within 5 feet is hit by an attack, can impose disadvantage on the attack roll.

LEGENDARY ACTIONS (3/Turn):
- Move: Moves up to his speed without provoking opportunity attacks.
- Command: Issues an order; one ally within 60 feet can use their reaction to make one weapon attack.
- Intimidating Presence (Costs 2): Each enemy within 30 feet must succeed DC 16 Wisdom save or be frightened until end of his next turn.
```

### Equipment
- **Armor:** Plate Armor +2 (Mythril-forged, black iron finish, Thandris family crest)
- **Shield:** Tower Shield +2 (Iron-bound, bears the mountain sigil)
- **Primary Weapon:** Thrandil's Edge (Legendary longsword, see above)
- **Secondary:** Heavy crossbow (masterwork), 20 bolts
- **Crown:** Iron Crown of Thaldros (counts as +2 circlet of intellect for official duties)
- **Ring:** Ring of Protection +1
- **Cloak:** Cloak of Protection (heavy fur-lined, royal purple)
- **Other:** Royal seal, ceremonial regalia worth 5,000 gp

### Personality
**Traits:**
- Speaks in clipped, military tones; every word has purpose
- Stands when others enter the room out of respect and dominance
- Constantly assesses threats and tactical situations
- Values loyalty above all other virtues

**Ideals:**
- **Duty:** "The crown is a burden I bear for my people, not a treasure I enjoy."
- **Strength:** "Only through strength can we protect what matters."
- **Legacy:** "My ancestors built this kingdom; I will not be the one to lose it."

**Bonds:**
- Kaer Thandros and its people are his sacred charge
- His claim to the title of High King (of the unified realm) is legitimate and must be proven
- The memory of his father, who died defending the northern pass
- His daughter Princess Eira, whom he's grooming as heir

**Flaws:**
- Stubbornly refuses to admit mistakes once a decision is made
- Views compromise as weakness, especially with House Aethermere
- So focused on external threats that he misses internal corruption
- Secret fear that he's not worthy of the High King title

### Background & History
Born in 1200 CR, third in line for the throne. Never expected to rule—his older brothers were the heirs. Changed when his eldest brother died in the Dragon Wars (1215), and his second brother died of plague (1222). At age 28, he became heir apparent.

Crowned in 1230 after his father's death defending Ironhold from giant raids. His first decade was spent consolidating power and rebuilding the military. Known for the "Iron Reforms"—modernizing the army, improving fortifications, and establishing the Northern Guard as an elite force.

Married Queen Mara of House Ironforge in 1225 (political alliance). They have three children:
- **Princess Eira** (age 20) - Heir, brilliant tactician
- **Prince Gareth** (age 17) - Second son, training as knight
- **Princess Lyanna** (age 14) - Youngest, scholar interested in magic

His reign has been marked by stability and strength, but also by increased tensions with Aethoria over the "High King" title. He genuinely believes his claim is legitimate and that reunification under Thandris rule would benefit both continents.

### Connections
- **Ally:** Lord Commander Thrain Ironoak (trusts completely)
- **Advisor:** Sage Thelmar Runescribe (values his counsel)
- **Rival:** High Queen Aelindra Aethermere (political opponent)
- **Secret Contact:** Has a spy in the Aethorian court (unknown to others)
- **Enemy:** The Syndicate (they once tried to assassinate him)

### Secrets
1. **The Succession Document:** Privately possesses evidence suggesting neither Thandris nor Aethermere has clear claim to High King title—a third bloodline might exist. Keeps this hidden.
2. **The Northern Pact:** Made a secret treaty with the frost giants—they stay in high peaks, humans stay below. Publicly denies this.
3. **His Youngest:** Princess Lyanna shows signs of sorcerous power. In public, he encourages her scholarly pursuits. Privately, he's arranging for secret training.
4. **The Black Budget:** Maintains a secret treasury for "special operations" funded by seizing Syndicate assets. Not all council members know about it.
5. **Health Concern:** Has recurring nightmares about the Worldrend. Consulted diviner secretly; told he'll face a choice between crown and realm.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The High King's Quest:** Hires party to find the legendary proof of succession—the High King's Sword or crown jewels from the Sundered Palace.
2. **Assassination Plot:** The Syndicate makes another attempt. Party must protect him or investigate who hired the killers.
3. **Northern Crisis:** Giants are pushing boundaries of the secret treaty. King needs deniable agents to resolve situation.
4. **The Lost Heir:** Evidence surfaces of a third bloodline. King wants party to investigate quietly.
5. **Dragon's Return:** A dragon attacks the border. King needs heroes to deal with it—but secretly, it might be tied to his family's past.
6. **Princess in Danger:** One of his children is kidnapped or threatened. King will pay anything for their safe return.
7. **The Unity Summit:** King arranges a summit with Queen Aelindra. Needs party to ensure security and perhaps influence negotiations.

### Roleplaying Notes
**Voice:** Deep, commanding, formal. Uses "we" when speaking officially. Short sentences.
**Mannerisms:** 
- Taps fingers on sword pommel when thinking
- Stands with weight on both feet, ready for combat
- Makes direct eye contact—holds it until others look away
- Adjusts armor straps when stressed

**In Combat:** Fights from the front. Protects weaker allies. Never retreats unless tactical. Uses Intimidating Presence to break enemy morale.

**Social Situations:** Formal, proper, expects respect. Will relax slightly with trusted advisors. Enjoys strategic discussions. Has dry sense of humor that catches people off-guard.

**Goals:**
- Short-term: Secure the northern border, maintain stability
- Medium-term: Prove his claim to High King title
- Long-term: Reunify the realms under Thandris rule (but only if truly best for everyone)

### Notes for DMs
- Use him as quest-giver for high-level parties
- Can be ally or obstacle depending on party's goals
- Not evil—genuinely believes he's doing right thing
- Complex character—military pragmatist with hidden depths
- His stubbornness can create problems even when he's right
- Good for political intrigue campaigns
- Can be redeemed if shown he's wrong about something important

---

## High Queen Aelindra Aethermere
**"The stars remember what mortals forget. We are their keepers."**

### Basic Information
- **Race:** High Elf
- **Age:** 487 (appears mid-30s)
- **Location:** Aethermere, The Starlight Palace
- **Role:** High Queen of Aethoria (Eastern Continent)
- **Alignment:** Lawful Good
- **Class:** Wizard 16 (School of Divination) / Noble Background

### Physical Description
Graceful and ethereal (5'8", 120 lbs), with the timeless beauty of high elves. Silver hair that seems to shimmer with starlight, worn long and unbound. Eyes are violet-blue, seem to see through you. Pale skin with faint silver patterns (natural elf marking, not tattoos). Moves with liquid grace. Always appears serene and in control.

### Stat Block
```
Medium Humanoid (High Elf), Lawful Good

Armor Class: 17 (Robes of the Archmagi, ring of protection)
Hit Points: 105 (16d6 + 48)
Speed: 30 ft.

STR: 8 (-1)  DEX: 14 (+2)  CON: 16 (+3)
INT: 22 (+6)  WIS: 18 (+4)  CHA: 20 (+5)

Saving Throws: Int +12, Wis +10
Skills: Arcana +12, History +12, Insight +10, Perception +10, Persuasion +11
Damage Resistances: Force (from protective spells)
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft., Passive Perception 20
Languages: Common, Elvish, Celestial, Draconic, Sylvan, Deep Speech, Primordial
Challenge Rating: 16 (15,000 XP)

ABILITIES:
Spellcasting: 16th-level wizard. Spell save DC 20, +12 to hit with spell attacks.

Spells Prepared (Daily):
Cantrips (at will): Mage Hand, Message, Minor Illusion, Prestidigitation, Ray of Frost
1st level (4 slots): Detect Magic, Identify, Mage Armor*, Shield
2nd level (3 slots): Detect Thoughts, Mirror Image, See Invisibility
3rd level (3 slots): Clairvoyance, Counterspell, Dispel Magic
4th level (3 slots): Arcane Eye, Banishment, Greater Invisibility
5th level (2 slots): Scrying, Teleportation Circle, Wall of Force
6th level (1 slot): True Seeing, Globe of Invulnerability
7th level (1 slot): Teleport, Plane Shift
8th level (1 slot): Maze, Mind Blank*
9th level (1 slot): Foresight*, Time Stop

*Usually active

DIVINATION SCHOOL FEATURES:
Portent (2/Day): After a long rest, roll 2d20. Can replace any attack roll, save, or check with one of these rolls.
Expert Divination: Regains a spell slot (up to 5th level) when casting divination spell of 2nd level or higher.
The Third Eye (1/Rest): Can see invisible creatures, read any language, see into Ethereal Plane, or gain darkvision 60 ft. for 1 hour.

SPECIAL FEATURES:
Fey Ancestry: Advantage against being charmed, immune to magical sleep.
Trance: Meditates for 4 hours instead of sleeping.
Queen's Wisdom: Has advantage on Insight and Persuasion checks when in her realm.
Starlight Blessing: Once per day, can cast Lesser Restoration or Remove Curse without expending a spell slot.

LEGENDARY RESISTANCE (3/Day): If she fails a saving throw, she can choose to succeed instead.

ACTIONS:
Multiattack: Casts a cantrip and uses her Star Staff, or casts two cantrips.

Star Staff (Quarterstaff +3): Melee Weapon Attack: +8 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d6+2 bludgeoning damage (1d8+2 versatile), plus 2d8 force damage.
Special: Can cast a wizard spell through the staff as a bonus action once per turn.

Spellcasting: Casts a spell from her prepared list.

REACTIONS:
Shield: Casts Shield to increase AC by 5 until start of next turn.
Counterspell: Automatically counters spells of 6th level or lower, or makes check for higher levels.
Precognitive Defense: Using Portent, can change an enemy's attack roll to one of her portent rolls.

LEGENDARY ACTIONS (3/Turn):
- Cantrip: Casts a cantrip.
- Detect: Makes a Wisdom (Perception) or Intelligence (Investigation) check.
- Spell (Costs 2): Casts a spell of 3rd level or lower.
- Foresight (Costs 3): Uses her divination to grant one ally within 60 feet advantage on their next attack roll, save, or check.
```

### Equipment
- **Armor:** Robes of the Archmagi (white with silver stars, AC 15 + Dex modifier)
- **Staff:** Star Staff (legendary quarterstaff, see above, acts as Rod of Absorption)
- **Crown:** Crown of Stars (silvery circlet, functions as Headband of Intellect +2 but already included in stats)
- **Ring:** Ring of Protection +1
- **Cloak:** Cloak of Displacement (appears as flowing starlight)
- **Amulet:** Amulet of Proof Against Detection and Location
- **Spellbook:** The Chronicle of Stars (contains all wizard spells up to 7th level, some 8th-9th)
- **Other:** Crystal focus, royal seal, several spell scrolls, potions of greater healing (3)

### Personality
**Traits:**
- Speaks slowly and deliberately, as if each word has been foreseen and chosen
- Makes eye contact that seems to see your past, present, and future
- Often pauses mid-conversation, as if listening to something others can't hear
- Smiles knowingly, which can be comforting or unnerving

**Ideals:**
- **Knowledge:** "The future is not set, but neither is it unknown. Wisdom lies in seeing all paths."
- **Duty:** "The crown is a lens through which I see my people's needs and guide them forward."
- **Peace:** "Violence is the choice of those who cannot see beyond the moment."

**Bonds:**
- Aethermere and the elven people are her sacred trust
- The ancient traditions and wisdom of the pre-Worldrend elves must be preserved
- Her son, Prince Eldrin, whom she's carefully preparing to rule
- The stars themselves, which she believes hold the answers to all questions

**Flaws:**
- Sometimes so focused on long-term future that she misses immediate crises
- Can appear cold or detached because she's seen so many possible futures
- Trusts her divinations absolutely—sometimes to her detriment when magic fails
- Secret guilt over her role (however small) in the Worldrend

### Background & History
Born in 760 CR, long before the Worldrend. Trained at the University of Arcane Studies in Silverpine (when it was one continent). Witnessed the Worldrend at age 247—one of the few elves alive who remembers the world before.

Ascended to the throne in 1180 CR after her mother's death. Her reign has been marked by wisdom, peace, and prosperity—but also by the shadow of the Worldrend and the question of succession.

Married Prince Consort Thaelon Starlight (another high elf, age 600+). They have one child:
- **Prince Eldrin** (age 95, still considered young for elves) - Heir, wizard like his mother

She genuinely believes her claim to High Queen (of the unified realm) is legitimate. Unlike King Aldric IV, she doesn't seek reunification through force—she believes it will happen naturally when the time is right, guided by the stars.

### Connections
- **Closest Advisor:** Council Elder Thaelon (her husband, also chief advisor)
- **Magical Mentor:** Archmage Veridian Starweaver (University)
- **Spiritual Guide:** Archdruid Silvaris Oakenheart
- **Rival:** King Aldric IV Thandris (political opponent, but respects him)
- **Concern:** The growing power of the Syndicate in both continents
- **Secret:** Has regular visions of a potential Second Worldrend

### Secrets
1. **The Vision:** Has foreseen multiple possible futures, several involving catastrophe. Working quietly to prevent them without revealing the full scope of danger (might cause panic).
2. **The Lost Sister:** Had a twin sister who died in the Worldrend. Consults her spirit through magic (others don't know). Sister's advice is sometimes... questionable.
3. **The True Heir:** Her divinations show that neither Thandris nor Aethermere is the "true" heir—but also show three different people who could be. Trying to identify them.
4. **The Stars' Warning:** The stars have gone "quiet" in recent years. Her divination magic still works, but there's a sense that something is blocking or changing fate itself. This terrifies her.
5. **Mother's Death:** Officially died of old age. Truth: sacrificed herself in a ritual to prevent something terrible. Aelindra continues the ritual monthly in secret.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Prophecy Quest:** Hires party to investigate a prophecy that promises revelation but requires dangerous journey.
2. **Stolen Future:** Her Portent ability stops working—someone or something is blocking divination magic. Party must find out why.
3. **The Lost Prince:** Prince Eldrin goes missing while researching ancient magic. Queen needs discreet heroes to find him.
4. **Diplomatic Mission:** Sends party as emissaries to Thaldros to discuss potential peace. They might represent her at crucial negotiations.
5. **The Third Heir:** Party finds evidence of the mysterious third bloodline. Queen wants them to investigate without alerting the other houses.
6. **Worldrend Anniversary:** On the anniversary of the Worldrend, reality starts weakening again. Queen knows how to stop it but needs components/help.
7. **Star's Going Out:** A star literally goes out in the sky. Queen's divination says this is connected to a ancient evil awakening. Party must stop it.

### Roleplaying Notes
**Voice:** Soft, melodious, measured. Speaks in complete sentences with formal grammar. Often references fate, stars, or time.
**Mannerisms:**
- Gazes into distance as if seeing beyond present moment
- Touches her crown when receiving visions
- Speaks of future events in present tense sometimes
- Tilts head when listening to something others can't hear

**In Combat:** Avoids melee. Stays at range. Uses Portent to turn enemy crits into misses or ally misses into hits. Prefers control spells over damage. Will Teleport to safety if seriously threatened.

**Social Situations:** Gracious host, excellent listener, gives impression she knows more than she says. Diplomatic but firm. Uses divination to anticipate arguments and prepare responses.

**Goals:**
- Short-term: Maintain peace and prosperity in Aethoria
- Medium-term: Prevent the catastrophes she's foreseen
- Long-term: Guide the realms toward reunification when the time is right (but not forced)

### Notes for DMs
- Use her as patron for parties working for greater good
- Excellent quest-giver for mysteries and prophecies
- Her Portent ability means she might know party is coming
- Can serve as deus ex machina but use sparingly
- Interesting moral conflict: she knows terrible futures but can't prevent all of them—which does she choose?
- Good foil to King Aldric IV—wisdom vs. strength, patience vs. action
- Her visions can seed future campaigns
- Not infallible—divination can be wrong or misinterpreted

---

## Merchant Prince Davos Goldshore
**"Gold opens doors that armies cannot breach, and silence is the most profitable investment."**

### Basic Information
- **Race:** Half-Elf
- **Age:** 157 (appears early 40s)
- **Location:** Goldreach, Goldshore Manor
- **Role:** Ruler of Goldreach, Head of House Goldshore, Trade Council Leader
- **Alignment:** Lawful Neutral (leans toward Evil)
- **Class:** Rogue 12 (Mastermind) / Bard 4 (College of Whispers)

### Physical Description
Distinguished and handsome (5'11", 165 lbs), with the ageless quality of half-elves. Dark hair streaked with silver, kept impeccably groomed. Green eyes that seem to calculate your worth when they look at you. Always impeccably dressed in the finest clothes (worth 500+ gp per outfit). Wears expensive jewelry but tastefully—shows wealth without being gaudy.

### Stat Block
```
Medium Humanoid (Half-Elf), Lawful Neutral

Armor Class: 17 (studded leather +2, ring of protection, defensive style)
Hit Points: 120 (12d8 + 4d8 + 48)
Speed: 30 ft.

STR: 10 (+0)  DEX: 18 (+4)  CON: 14 (+2)
INT: 16 (+3)  WIS: 14 (+2)  CHA: 20 (+5)

Saving Throws: Dex +9, Int +8, Wis +7, Cha +10
Skills: Deception +15, Insight +12, Intimidation +10, Investigation +8, Perception +7, Persuasion +15, Sleight of Hand +9, Stealth +9
Damage Resistances: Psychic (from Words of Terror feature)
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft., Passive Perception 17
Languages: Common, Elvish, Dwarvish, Halfling, Thieves' Cant, Draconic
Challenge Rating: 13 (10,000 XP)

ABILITIES:
Sneak Attack (6d6): Once per turn, deals extra damage when he has advantage or an ally is within 5 feet of target.

Cunning Action: Can take bonus action to Dash, Disengage, or Hide.

Expertise: Double proficiency in Deception, Insight, Persuasion, Investigation.

Master of Intrigue: Can mimic speech patterns and accents. Can unerringly mimic another person's speech, writing, and behavior if studied for at least 1 hour.

Master of Tactics: Can use Help action as bonus action. When using Help, ally also gains advantage on their next attack against the target.

Insightful Manipulator: If he spends 1 minute observing or interacting with someone, can learn if target is his equal, superior, or inferior in:
- Intelligence score
- Wisdom score
- Charisma score
- Class levels (if any)

Misdirection: When targeted by attack while a creature within 5 feet is also within reach of attacker, he can use reaction to have attack target that creature instead.

BARDIC INSPIRATION (d6): Can inspire allies 5 times per long rest. Lasts 10 minutes.

SPELLCASTING (Bard): 4th-level bard. Spell save DC 15, +7 to hit with spell attacks.
Cantrips: Message, Vicious Mockery, Minor Illusion
1st level (4 slots): Charm Person, Disguise Self, Detect Thoughts
2nd level (3 slots): Detect Thoughts, Suggestion, Zone of Truth

WORDS OF TERROR: Can whisper to a creature during conversation (at least 1 minute). Target must succeed DC 15 Wisdom save or be frightened of him or another creature for 1 hour. Doesn't realize it was magically induced.

PSYCHIC BLADES: Can expend Bardic Inspiration when dealing Sneak Attack damage to add psychic damage equal to inspiration die.

SPECIAL FEATURES:
Fey Ancestry: Advantage against being charmed, immune to magical sleep.
Merchant's Fortune: Has advantage on Charisma checks when negotiating trade deals.
Network of Informants: Can make Intelligence check (DC 15) to know information about any notable person or organization in Goldreach or major trade cities.

ACTIONS:
Multiattack: Makes two rapier attacks or one rapier attack and uses a bonus action.

Goldvein (Rapier +2): Melee Weapon Attack: +11 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d8+6 piercing damage plus 6d6 sneak attack (if conditions met).
Special: On a critical hit, target must succeed DC 15 Constitution save or be poisoned for 1 minute (coated in subtle toxin).

Hand Crossbow +1: Ranged Weapon Attack: +10 to hit, range 30/120 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d6+5 piercing damage plus 6d6 sneak attack (if conditions met).

Spellcasting: Casts a bard spell.

REACTIONS:
Uncanny Dodge: Halves damage from an attack he can see.
Misdirection: Redirects attack to another creature (see above).
Counteroffer: When someone makes a request or demand, can use Persuasion or Deception to completely change the terms of negotiation.

LEGENDARY ACTIONS (3/Turn):
- Move: Moves up to his speed.
- Assess: Makes an Insight check.
- Attack: Makes one weapon attack.
- Whisper (Costs 2): Uses Words of Terror on a creature within 5 feet.
- Manipulate (Costs 2): Uses Bardic Inspiration or casts a 1st-level spell.
```

### Equipment
- **Armor:** Studded Leather +2 (black leather, gold studs, elegant)
- **Primary Weapon:** Goldvein (Rapier +2, golden blade with emerald pommel, poisoned)
- **Secondary:** Hand Crossbow +1 (concealed, decorated with gold inlay), 20 bolts
- **Ring:** Ring of Protection +1
- **Cloak:** Cloak of Elvenkind (appears as fine merchant's cloak)
- **Amulet:** Amulet of Proof Against Detection and Location (hides from scrying)
- **Other:** Multiple sets of fine clothing (500 gp each), signet ring (House Goldshore), ledgers, various documents, bag of holding with 10,000 gp in gems

### Personality
**Traits:**
- Everything is a negotiation—every conversation has an angle
- Smiles constantly, even when discussing violence (especially then)
- Remembers everyone's name and details about them
- Never shows anger, even when furious inside

**Ideals:**
- **Profit:** "Gold is freedom. Everything else is negotiable."
- **Control:** "Information is more valuable than gold, and I collect both."
- **Legacy:** "House Goldshore will outlast kingdoms and crowns."

**Bonds:**
- House Goldshore's reputation and wealth
- His daughter Serina, whom he's grooming as his heir
- The city of Goldreach—he built it into what it is
- His network of informants and agents across both continents

**Flaws:**
- Believes everything and everyone can be bought
- So focused on profit that he misses emotional motivations
- Paranoid—trusts almost no one completely
- Ruthless when betrayed—holds grudges forever

### Background & History
Born in 1090 CR to a minor merchant family in Goldreach. Half-elf heritage from his elvish mother. Showed talent for trade and manipulation from youth. Built family business into trading empire through combination of shrewd deals and ruthless elimination of competitors.

Became leader of House Goldshore at age 50 (1140 CR) when his uncle died (officially natural causes, but Davos was involved). Transformed House Goldshore from wealthy merchants into de facto rulers of Goldreach.

Currently the richest individual in Tirvandor (excepting maybe dragons). Worth estimated 8-10 million gold pieces. Controls approximately 40% of maritime trade between continents.

Married twice (both wives died of "illness"). Currently widowed. Has one legitimate child:
- **Lady Serina Goldshore** (age 45, half-elf) - His heir and trade minister

Rumored to have several illegitimate children across both continents. Uses them as agents sometimes.

### Connections
- **Business Partner:** Captain Sylara Windchaser (merchant fleet)
- **Ally:** Sultan Rashid Al-Sahir (trade agreements)
- **Rival:** Trade Prince Lucian Goldfingers (Merchant League)
- **Tool:** Master Crimson (criminal syndicate—Davos uses them, they don't know)
- **Curiosity:** High Queen Aelindra (wants trade deal with Aethoria)
- **Problem:** House Crystalborn (old naval rivalry)

### Secrets
1. **The Salvage Operation:** Has secret expeditions searching sunken palace for treasures. Found several artifacts, kept quiet. One might be the Crown Jewels.
2. **The Poison Prince:** Maintains a poisoner on permanent staff. Has eliminated at least seven business rivals. Never caught.
3. **The Lost Heir:** Knows the identity (or thinks he does) of Lord Aldris's fourth daughter Marina. Keeping information for leverage.
4. **The Syndicate Connection:** While he publicly opposes the Syndicate, he secretly funds certain operations and gets cut of profits. Uses them for deniable operations.
5. **The Will:** Has a forged copy of Lord Aldris's will. Real enough to fool most experts. Plans to "discover" it at strategically perfect time.
6. **Hidden Assets:** His declared wealth is 8-10 million. His actual wealth is closer to 20 million. Half is hidden in various accounts, fake names, shell companies.
7. **The Insurance Policy:** Has compromising information on dozens of nobles, merchants, and officials. Files hidden in several locations. If he dies, they're released.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Salvage Job:** Hires party to recover something from the sunken palace. Pays extremely well but mission is dangerous and possibly illegal.
2. **Corporate Espionage:** Needs party to infiltrate rival's operations and steal trade secrets or sabotage operations.
3. **The Blackmail:** Someone is blackmailing him (rare!). Needs party to find out who and eliminate the problem quietly.
4. **Protect the Shipment:** High-value cargo needs protection from pirates/monsters/rivals. Simple job that becomes complicated.
5. **The Daughter's Suitor:** Lady Serina has attracted unwanted attention. Davos wants party to make the problem go away without obvious connection to him.
6. **The Missing Agent:** One of his informants disappeared with sensitive information. Find them, retrieve the information, ensure silence.
7. **The Hostile Takeover:** Davos is trying to acquire a company/property. Owner won't sell. Party might be hired by Davos... or by the owner to stop him.

### Roleplaying Notes
**Voice:** Smooth, cultured, friendly. Uses people's names frequently. Asks questions that seem casual but gather information. Never raises voice.
**Mannerisms:**
- Steeples fingers when thinking
- Smiles that doesn't reach eyes
- Touches jewelry when calculating
- Leans back when he's won a negotiation

**In Combat:** Avoids if possible. If fighting, uses minions, traps, and poison. Fights dirty. Uses Cunning Action to escape. Only fights if escape is impossible.

**Social Situations:** Charming host, excellent conversationalist, remembers everything said. Appears to give ground in negotiations but ends up with what he wanted. Makes people feel clever for accepting his terms.

**Goals:**
- Short-term: Increase wealth and market share
- Medium-term: Control majority of cross-continental trade
- Long-term: House Goldshore becomes indispensable to both continents' economies

### Notes for DMs
- Excellent recurring patron for mercenary-type parties
- Can be ally or antagonist depending on party's actions
- Not obviously evil—just ruthlessly practical
- Good source of morally gray quests
- His resources mean he can bail out or screw over the party
- Use as example of "rich getting richer" and systemic corruption
- Can be redeemed if he suffers genuine loss that teaches him value of things beyond gold
- Excellent for intrigue and investigation campaigns

---

*Continued in next section with Sultan Rashid Al-Sahir and Council Mistress Elara Silverleaf...*

# Rulers Continued
---

## Sultan Rashid Al-Sahir
"The Twice-Blessed"

**"The desert teaches patience. Water comes to those who wait, death to those who rush."**

### Basic Information
- **Race:** Human
- **Age:** 68
- **Location:** Sundara, The Oasis Palace
- **Role:** Sultan of Sundara, Elder Council Leader, Spiritual Guide
- **Alignment:** Lawful Good
- **Class:** Cleric 14 (Life Domain) / Monk 2

### Physical Description
Elderly but vigorous (5'9", 160 lbs), with dark skin weathered by desert sun. Long white beard, braided with golden rings. Deep brown eyes filled with wisdom and kindness. Bald head covered with white turban adorned with sapphire. Moves with surprising grace for his age. Always dressed in white robes with gold trim.

### Stat Block
```
Medium Humanoid (Human), Lawful Good

Armor Class: 18 (Bracers of Defense, Wisdom modifier, no armor)
Hit Points: 126 (14d8 + 2d8 + 48)
Speed: 40 ft.

STR: 12 (+1)  DEX: 16 (+3)  CON: 16 (+3)
INT: 14 (+2)  WIS: 20 (+5)  CHA: 16 (+3)

Saving Throws: Wis +11, Cha +9
Skills: History +8, Insight +11, Medicine +11, Perception +11, Religion +8
Damage Resistances: None
Senses: Passive Perception 21
Languages: Common, Celestial, Primordial, Draconic
Challenge Rating: 14 (11,500 XP)

ABILITIES:
Spellcasting: 14th-level cleric. Spell save DC 19, +11 to hit with spell attacks.

Spells Prepared (Daily):
Cantrips (at will): Light, Mending, Resistance, Sacred Flame, Thaumaturgy
1st level (4 slots): Bless, Cure Wounds, Detect Evil and Good, Sanctuary
2nd level (3 slots): Aid, Lesser Restoration, Prayer of Healing, Spiritual Weapon
3rd level (3 slots): Beacon of Hope, Dispel Magic, Mass Healing Word, Revivify
4th level (3 slots): Death Ward, Divination, Guardian of Faith
5th level (2 slots): Greater Restoration, Mass Cure Wounds, Raise Dead
6th level (1 slot): Heal, Heroes' Feast
7th level (1 slot): Divine Word, Resurrection

DOMAIN SPELLS (Always Prepared):
1st: Bless, Cure Wounds
2nd: Lesser Restoration, Spiritual Weapon
3rd: Beacon of Hope, Revivify
4th: Death Ward, Guardian of Faith
5th: Mass Cure Wounds, Raise Dead
6th: Heal
7th: Resurrection

CHANNEL DIVINITY (3/Rest):
- Turn Undead (DC 19 Wisdom save)
- Preserve Life: Restore 70 hit points, divided among creatures within 30 feet

DIVINE INTERVENTION: Can call upon his deity for aid. 14% chance of success. If successful, cannot use again for 7 days.

MONK FEATURES:
Unarmored Defense: AC = 10 + Dex + Wis (already calculated)
Martial Arts (1d4): Unarmed strikes deal 1d4 + Dex damage, can use as bonus action
Ki Points (2/Rest): Can use for Flurry of Blows, Patient Defense, or Step of the Wind

SPECIAL FEATURES:
Blessed Healer: When he casts a spell that restores hit points to someone else, he regains 2 + spell level hit points.
Supreme Healing: When restoring hit points with a 1st level or higher spell, target regains additional 5 hit points.
Twice-Blessed: Has survived two lethal situations through divine intervention (actual game mechanic activated both times). Considered a living miracle.
Desert Wisdom: Has advantage on Wisdom checks related to survival, weather, or desert phenomena.

ACTIONS:
Multiattack: Makes two unarmed strikes or one staff attack, or casts a spell.

Sun Staff (Quarterstaff): Melee Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d6+1 bludgeoning damage (1d8+1 versatile), plus 2d6 radiant damage.
Special: Once per day, can cast Daylight as bonus action.

Unarmed Strike: Melee Weapon Attack: +9 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d4+3 bludgeoning damage.

Sacred Flame: Target makes DC 19 Dexterity save or takes 3d8 radiant damage (no cover bonus).

Spellcasting: Casts a cleric spell.

REACTIONS:
Patient Defense: Can spend 1 ki point to take Dodge action as bonus action.
Shield of Faith (Pre-cast): +2 AC to self or ally within 60 feet.

LEGENDARY ACTIONS (3/Turn):
- Move: Moves up to his speed.
- Heal: Touches a creature and restores 2d8 + 5 hit points.
- Bless (Costs 2): Casts Bless without expending a spell slot (if not already active).
- Channel Divinity (Costs 3): Uses Channel Divinity ability.
```

### Equipment
- **Armor:** None (Bracers of Defense, AC from Wisdom)
- **Weapon:** Sun Staff (quarterstaff, see above, golden wood that glows faintly)
- **Robes:** White silk robes with gold thread (worth 200 gp, no AC bonus)
- **Turban:** Turban of Wisdom (functions as Headband of Intellect but for Wisdom, already in stats)
- **Bracers:** Bracers of Defense (+2 AC while unarmored)
- **Amulet:** Holy Symbol of Pelor (sun disc made of gold)
- **Ring:** Ring of Feather Falling
- **Other:** Pouch with 10 diamonds (300 gp each for Revivify), waterskin (always full—Create Water), prayer beads

### Personality
**Traits:**
- Speaks in parables and desert wisdom—everything has a lesson
- Genuinely kind and patient with everyone, even enemies
- Pauses to pray/meditate multiple times daily, even mid-conversation
- Touches people's hands or shoulders when speaking—physical connection matters

**Ideals:**
- **Life:** "Every soul is precious. Every death diminishes us all."
- **Wisdom:** "The desert teaches: water sustains, shade protects, community survives."
- **Peace:** "Violence is the last resort of the unimaginative."

**Bonds:**
- Sundara and its people are his sacred charge from Pelor
- The Great Oasis—if it fails, the city dies
- His students and spiritual children (he's trained dozens of clerics)
- The memory of his wife, who died twenty years ago

**Flaws:**
- Pacifistic to a fault—sometimes won't act when action is needed
- Trusts too easily—believes in the good in everyone
- So focused on spiritual matters that practical governance suffers
- Secret fear that he's not worthy of being "Twice-Blessed"

### Background & History
Born in Sundara in 1179 CR to a merchant family. Experienced divine vision at age 16—saw Pelor in the sun and dedicated his life to service. Trained as cleric, became respected spiritual leader by age 30.

Elected Sultan at age 45 (1224 CR) after previous Sultan died. Leadership is spiritual and administrative—he guides more than rules. The city functions through council system he established.

**The Two Blessings:**
1. **First Blessing (Age 22):** During plague, he healed hundreds until he collapsed from exhaustion. Should have died. Divine Intervention activated—Pelor himself appeared and restored him. Earned title "The Blessed."
2. **Second Blessing (Age 50):** During sandstorm, went into desert to rescue lost child. Caught in storm, nearly died of dehydration. Divine Intervention activated again. Pelor sent rain (in the desert!). Saved both. Became "Twice-Blessed."

These two miracles make him living legend. Many pilgrims come to Sundara just to meet him. He's humble about it, insists he's just a servant.

Wife (Aisha) died 20 years ago. Never remarried. They had no children. Considers his students his children.

### Connections
- **Student:** Master Glasswright Zara (he taught her, she reveres him)
- **Ally:** Merchant Prince Davos (trade partnership, but Rashid doesn't fully trust him)
- **Friend:** Archdruid Silvaris Oakenheart (mutual respect between clerics and druids)
- **Concern:** Desert Ranger Khalid (capable but vengeful—Rashid tries to teach mercy)
- **Mysterious:** The Sand Prophet (oracle in desert, sometimes agrees, sometimes contradicts Rashid's visions)

### Secrets
1. **The Third Blessing:** Rashid knows he can call Divine Intervention one more time before he dies. Pelor told him so. Saving it for the moment of greatest need. Terrified of choosing wrong moment.
2. **The Oasis Curse:** The Great Oasis is slowly dying. Not natural—someone cursed it. Rashid knows but hasn't told anyone (would cause panic). Working on solution privately.
3. **The Doubts:** Despite being "Twice-Blessed," he has moments of deep doubt. Wonders if he misunderstood Pelor's will. Hasn't told anyone.
4. **The Dark Prayer:** Once, in moment of rage when his wife died, he prayed for vengeance instead of peace. Pelor didn't answer. Rashid considers this his greatest sin.
5. **The Successor:** Has no biological heir. Secretly training three possible successors, but hasn't chosen which one. One of them isn't who they claim to be.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Dying Oasis:** The Great Oasis is failing. Rashid reveals the curse and needs party to find the source and break it.
2. **The False Heir:** One of his spiritual successors is actually a Syndicate plant. Rashid suspects but can't prove it. Needs investigation.
3. **The Third Blessing:** Rashid receives vision that the moment for his final Divine Intervention is coming. Party must help him reach the place where it must be used.
4. **The Plague Returns:** Disease strikes Sundara again. Rashid heals everyone he can, but it's not enough. Party must find the source/cure.
5. **The Sand Prophet:** The mysterious oracle in the desert has gone silent. Rashid is concerned—needs party to check on them.
6. **The Pilgrimage:** Rashid must make pilgrimage to sacred site, but assassins have been hired to kill him on the road. Party provides protection.
7. **The Doubt:** Rashid's faith wavers after a terrible tragedy. His powers weaken. Party must help him find his faith again.

### Roleplaying Notes
**Voice:** Gentle, slow, grandfatherly. Uses metaphors and desert imagery. Calls people "my child" regardless of age. Laughs warmly.
**Mannerisms:**
- Closes eyes when praying (several times daily)
- Touches forehead, lips, heart when blessing people
- Offers water to everyone (symbolic and practical)
- Smiles even when discussing sad topics

**In Combat:** Avoids combat if possible. If fighting, focuses on healing allies and protecting innocents. Uses non-lethal methods when possible. Will use lethal force only to save lives.

**Social Situations:** Extremely approachable. Listens more than talks. Gives advice when asked, never forces it. Treats everyone with equal respect—beggar and king alike.

**Goals:**
- Short-term: Keep Sundara safe and prosperous
- Medium-term: Solve the Oasis problem before it becomes crisis
- Long-term: Find worthy successor and ensure spiritual tradition continues

### Notes for DMs
- Excellent quest-giver for good-aligned parties
- Provides healing and resurrection services (for free or token donation)
- Can be patron for holy quests
- His two Divine Interventions are legendary—third one is major campaign moment
- Use him to teach moral lessons without being preachy
- Good counterpoint to more pragmatic or ruthless NPCs
- His death would be emotionally impactful—use sparingly
- Can provide sanctuary or guidance when party needs it

---

## Council Mistress Elara Silverleaf
**"Knowledge is not power—applied knowledge is power. Let me show you."**

### Basic Information
- **Race:** High Elf
- **Age:** 342 (appears mid-30s)
- **Location:** Silverpine, University of Arcane Studies
- **Role:** Head of Silverpine Council, University Rector
- **Alignment:** Neutral Good
- **Class:** Wizard 15 (School of Abjuration)

### Physical Description
Elegant and composed (5'7", 125 lbs), with the timeless beauty of high elves. Auburn hair with silver highlights, worn in complex braided style. Bright silver eyes that miss nothing. Pale skin. Always dressed in academic robes (burgundy with silver trim) indicating her rank as Rector. Wears spectacles for reading (doesn't need them, but they make her look scholarly).

### Stat Block
```
Medium Humanoid (High Elf), Neutral Good

Armor Class: 19 (Robe of the Archmagi, shield spell, ring of protection)
Hit Points: 112 (15d6 + 60)
Speed: 30 ft.

STR: 8 (-1)  DEX: 14 (+2)  CON: 18 (+4)
INT: 20 (+5)  WIS: 16 (+3)  CHA: 14 (+2)

Saving Throws: Int +11, Wis +9
Skills: Arcana +17 (expertise), History +11, Investigation +11, Insight +9, Perception +9
Damage Resistances: Damage from spells
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft., Passive Perception 19
Languages: Common, Elvish, Draconic, Dwarvish, Celestial, Abyssal, Infernal, Sylvan
Challenge Rating: 15 (13,000 XP)

ABILITIES:
Spellcasting: 15th-level wizard. Spell save DC 19, +11 to hit with spell attacks.

Spells Prepared (Daily):
Cantrips (at will): Fire Bolt, Mage Hand, Message, Prestidigitation, Ray of Frost
1st level (4 slots): Alarm, Detect Magic, Mage Armor*, Shield
2nd level (3 slots): Arcane Lock, Mirror Image, Misty Step
3rd level (3 slots): Counterspell, Dispel Magic, Fireball
4th level (3 slots): Banishment, Greater Invisibility, Otiluke's Resilient Sphere
5th level (2 slots): Cone of Cold, Wall of Force
6th level (1 slot): Globe of Invulnerability, Disintegrate
7th level (1 slot): Forcecage, Teleport
8th level (1 slot): Antimagic Field, Mind Blank*

*Usually active

ABJURATION SCHOOL FEATURES:
Arcane Ward: Has a magical ward with 45 hit points (2 × wizard level + Int modifier). When she takes damage, ward takes damage first. Regains 15 hit points when she casts an abjuration spell of 1st level or higher.

Projected Ward: When a creature within 30 feet takes damage, can use reaction to have ward take damage instead.

Improved Abjuration: When casting abjuration spell that requires check (like Dispel Magic), adds proficiency bonus (+6) to check.

Spell Resistance: Has advantage on saving throws against spells and resistance to spell damage.

SPECIAL FEATURES:
Fey Ancestry: Advantage against being charmed, immune to magical sleep.
Trance: Meditates for 4 hours instead of sleeping.
Academic Authority: Has advantage on Charisma checks when dealing with scholars, students, or in academic settings.
Master of Protection: Can cast Shield as a reaction without expending a spell slot 3 times per day.

ACTIONS:
Multiattack: Casts two cantrips or one spell and one cantrip.

Staff of Power: Melee Weapon Attack: +8 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d6+2 bludgeoning damage, plus 1d8 force damage.
Special: Functions as Staff of Power (has multiple charges for spells and abilities).

Spellcasting: Casts a wizard spell.

REACTIONS:
Shield: +5 AC until start of next turn when targeted by attack or Magic Missile.
Counterspell: Automatically counters spells of 5th level or lower, or makes check for higher.
Projected Ward: Uses Arcane Ward to protect ally within 30 feet.

LEGENDARY ACTIONS (3/Turn):
- Cantrip: Casts a cantrip.
- Move: Moves up to her speed.
- Spell (Costs 2): Casts a spell of 3rd level or lower.
- Arcane Ward (Costs 2): Restores 15 hit points to her Arcane Ward by casting an abjuration spell.
```

### Equipment
- **Robe:** Robe of the Archmagi (burgundy, AC 15 + Dex, advantage on saves vs. spells, resistance to spell damage)
- **Staff:** Staff of Power (can cast multiple spells, stores spell slots, can be used as weapon)
- **Ring:** Ring of Protection +1
- **Spellbook:** The Compendium of Wards (contains all wizard spells up to 6th level, specializing in abjuration)
- **Spectacles:** Glasses of Reading (magical, allow reading any language, worth 500 gp)
- **Other:** Component pouch, spell scrolls (Shield x3, Counterspell x2, Dispel Magic x2), potions of greater healing (2)

### Personality
**Traits:**
- Precise and organized—everything in its place
- Listens carefully before speaking, then speaks with authority
- Uses hand gestures when explaining complex concepts
- Corrects people politely when they're wrong (which annoys some)

**Ideals:**
- **Knowledge:** "An educated populace is a free populace."
- **Protection:** "Magic should be used to protect, not destroy."
- **Excellence:** "Good enough is the enemy of great."

**Bonds:**
- The University and its students are her life's work
- The city of Silverpine must remain safe haven for learning
- Her most promising students—she tracks their careers with pride
- The great library—repository of centuries of knowledge

**Flaws:**
- Perfectionist—can be harsh on self and others
- Somewhat elitist—believes educated opinions matter more
- Underestimates non-magical solutions to problems
- Workaholic—hasn't taken vacation in 50 years

### Background & History
Born in 905 CR in Aethermere. Showed magical talent young. Sent to Silverpine University at age 40 (young for an elf). Proved to be prodigy in abjuration magic—by age 80, was full professor.

Appointed Rector of the University at age 250 (1155 CR). Youngest Rector in university history. Under her leadership, the University has grown to be premier magical institution in western Tirvandor.

Also leads the Silverpine Council (city government). Silverpine is unique—governed by council of academics, merchants, and artisans. Elara chairs it. She's good administrator but sometimes frustrated by politics.

Never married. Devoted entirely to her work. Considers her students her children. Has trained hundreds of wizards over the centuries.

### Connections
- **Colleague:** Archmage Veridian Starweaver (fellow faculty, friendly rivalry)
- **Protégé:** Professor Elara Moonwhisper (former student, now faculty)
- **Ally:** High Queen Aelindra Aethermere (mutual respect, occasional consultation)
- **Concern:** The Syndicate (they've tried to infiltrate the University)
- **Student:** Has many former students in positions of power across Tirvandor
- **Rival:** Some faculty members think she's too controlling

### Secrets
1. **The Forbidden Vault:** University has vault of dangerous magical knowledge. Only she has access. Contains things that shouldn't exist—necromancy tomes, demon summoning, reality-breaking spells. She's studied them all (to know how to counter them, she tells herself).
2. **The Failed Student:** One of her most promising students turned to dark magic. She tried to stop him. He died in the confrontation. She's never fully forgiven herself.
3. **The True Power:** Her Staff of Power contains fragment of an ancient artifact. If reassembled with other fragments, it would create world-shattering weapon. She guards it carefully.
4. **The Secret Research:** Privately researching way to prevent another Worldrend. Has theory that requires massive magical energy. Hasn't told anyone—sounds too much like what caused first Worldrend.
5. **The Personal Ward:** Created a permanent personal ward on herself years ago. It's why she has such high Constitution. But it's slowly draining her life force. In 50-100 years, it will kill her. She's trying to fix it without removing the protection.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Library Theft:** Dangerous book stolen from restricted section. Party must recover it before it's used.
2. **The Failing Wards:** City's protective wards are failing. Party must investigate why and help restore them.
3. **The Dark Student:** Elara's former student is using dark magic for terrible purposes. She wants party to stop them—but alive if possible, for her sake.
4. **The Research Mission:** Needs rare magical components for research. Hires party to retrieve them from dangerous location.
5. **The Infiltration:** Suspects Syndicate spy in University. Party must identify them without causing panic.
6. **The Artifact Fragments:** Party discovers fragment of the same artifact as in her staff. She wants to secure it. Others want to assemble complete artifact.
7. **The Final Exam:** Needs party to test new magical defense system. What could go wrong? (Everything.)

### Roleplaying Notes
**Voice:** Clear, precise, academic. Uses technical terms. Speaks in complete paragraphs.
**Mannerisms:**
- Adjusts spectacles when thinking
- Conjures small illusions to illustrate points
- Casts minor protective spells unconsciously (like someone cracking knuckles)
- Walks with hands clasped behind back

**In Combat:** Fights defensively. Protects allies with wards. Uses Counterspell liberally. Prefers control and protection over damage. Will Teleport to safety if seriously threatened.

**Social Situations:** Professional but kind. Patient with students, less patient with incompetence. Enjoys intellectual discussions. Will lecture if given opportunity.

**Goals:**
- Short-term: Expand University, increase enrollment
- Medium-term: Establish satellite campuses in other cities
- Long-term: Make magical education accessible to all who show aptitude

### Notes for DMs
- Excellent quest-giver for magical research missions
- Can provide magical item identification, spell research, etc.
- University can be campaign location—intrigue among faculty, student problems
- Her protective magic makes her hard to kill—use as safe ally
- Good mentor figure for wizard PCs
- Her forbidden knowledge can seed dark magic plots
- The Failing Ward secret can be tragic end to her story
- Use her to represent institutional magic vs. wild magic

---

*Continued with Part 3: Major City Leaders...*

# Regional Leaders - Coastal
---

## Lord Commander Thrain Ironoak
*"Steel fears no fire. Neither do we."*

**Race:** Mountain Dwarf | **Age:** 198 | **Alignment:** Lawful Good  
**Class:** Fighter 13 (Champion) | **Location:** Kaer Thandros Military Command

### Stat Block
```
Medium Humanoid (Dwarf), Lawful Good

Armor Class: 21 (plate +2, shield, defense)
Hit Points: 156 (13d10 + 78)
Speed: 25 ft.

STR: 20 (+5)  DEX: 10 (+0)  CON: 22 (+6)
INT: 12 (+1)  WIS: 14 (+2)  CHA: 13 (+1)

Saving Throws: Str +10, Con +11
Skills: Athletics +10, Intimidation +6, Perception +7
Senses: darkvision 60 ft., passive Perception 12
Languages: Common, Dwarvish
Challenge: 13 (10,000 XP)

TRAITS:
**Dwarven Resilience.** Has advantage on saving throws against poison, and resistance to poison damage.
**Action Surge (2/rest).** Extra action
**Second Wind.** 1d10+13 HP as bonus action
**Improved Critical.** Crits on 19-20
**Remarkable Athlete.** Add half proficiency to Str/Dex/Con checks

ACTIONS:
**Battleaxe +3.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +13 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. *Hit:* 1d8+8 slashing (1d10+8 versatile) + 1d6 fire
**Warhammer +2.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +12 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. *Hit:* 1d8+7 bludgeoning (1d10+7 versatile)
**Extra Attack (3).** Attacks three times per turn
```

### Personality & Background
Gruff, honorable, old soldier. Commands with respect, not fear. Has served under three kings. Trusted advisor to King Aldric IV. Lost an eye in the Dragon Wars but refused magical healing ("Good dwarves earn their scars"). Values loyalty, hates cowardice.

**Secret:** Arranged the "Northern Pact" with frost giants on King's behalf. Only three people know.

### Background & History
Born in the deep halls of Kaer Thandros to the Ironoak clan, one of the oldest dwarven families in the Ironspine Holds. Joined the mountain guard at age 45, served in the Border Wars against orc incursions (1180s CR). Rose through ranks during the Post-Dragon Reconstruction, when his tactical brilliance defending supply caravans caught King Aldric III's attention.

Fought alongside humans during the Ashfall Uprising (1210 CR) when volcanic creatures threatened Emberforge. Lost his right eye to a fire giant's thrown boulder but refused to retreat until civilians evacuated. The injury became his badge of honor. Promoted to Lord Commander in 1225 CR, making him the first dwarf to hold the position in 200 years.

Has served three Thandris kings—the late Aldric III, briefly the infant-king Marcus (who died of fever), and now Aldric IV. This continuity makes him one of the most trusted advisors in the realm. Lives in the Military Command tower, hasn't visited his family hold in fifteen years.

### Connections
- **Reports to:** King Aldric IV Thandris (mutual respect, nearly father-son)
- **Commands:** 5,000 Royal Army soldiers, 3,000 City Watch
- **Allies:** General Marthos Thandris (king's brother), Thane Durin Ironforge (old friend)
- **Rivals:** Trade Prince Lucian Goldfingers (distrusts military spending)
- **Secret Contact:** Frost Giant Jarl Hrothgar (Northern Pact partner)

### Secrets
1. **The Northern Pact:** Negotiated a secret non-aggression treaty with frost giants. Giants get tribute of ale and metal; Thaldros gets safe northern borders. Only King Aldric IV and High Diplomat Erenna know.
2. **The Blackwood Sympathy:** His grandmother sheltered Blackwood refugees after the rebellion. He's quietly investigated their claims—and found troubling evidence the crown's version isn't complete.
3. **The Dragon Deal:** Witnessed the moment the red dragon Infernalix departed in 1156 CR. Saw someone speaking to it from the walls. Has never told anyone, not even the king.
4. **Failing Health:** The fire giant's boulder damaged more than his eye. Has recurring seizures he hides with medication from a discrete healer.
5. **The Lost Company:** His first command was massacred because he trusted bad intelligence. Survivors were told it was enemy action. It was actually friendly fire from panicking human troops.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Northern Pact Renewal:** Giants demand renegotiation. Thrain needs discrete agents to carry tribute and negotiate—official envoys would expose the secret.
2. **The Traitor Hunt:** Evidence suggests a high-ranking officer is selling military secrets to the Shadow Syndicate. Thrain needs outsiders to investigate without alerting the mole.
3. **The Lost Standard:** His first company's battle standard was taken by orcs and now sits in a warlord's trophy hall. He'll pay handsomely for its recovery—and silence about what really happened.
4. **The Blackwood Papers:** He's obtained documents suggesting House Blackwood was framed. Needs someone to verify them without his involvement being known.
5. **Dragon Witness:** After decades of silence, he's ready to tell someone what he saw during the Dragon Crisis—but only adventurers who've proven themselves trustworthy.
6. **The Kidnapped Son:** His estranged son Borin (not the Captain) was taken by giants who didn't get the Northern Pact message. Rescue required—but quietly, or the pact is exposed.
7. **The Sealed Levels:** Something is stirring in the forbidden deep levels of Kaer Thandros. He needs expendable explorers who won't be missed if they don't return.

### Equipment
Plate Armor +2 (mythril, dwarf-forged), Battleaxe +3 "Kingbreaker" (returns when thrown), Shield +1, Warhammer +2, Cloak of Protection, Ring of Feather Falling

### Plot Hooks
- Needs party to investigate suspected traitor in the ranks
- Requires agents to reinforce northern outpost discretely
- Son kidnapped by giants—rescue mission needed
- Seeks heroes to recover lost company standard from dragon's hoard

---

## Master Smith Durgan Forgefire
*"Every blade I forge protects a life. That is sacred work."*

**Race:** Mountain Dwarf | **Age:** 245 | **Alignment:** Lawful Neutral  
**Class:** Artificer 11 | **Location:** Crown Forge, Kaer Thandros

### Stat Block
```
Medium Humanoid (Dwarf), Lawful Neutral

Armor Class: 16 (breastplate, shield)
Hit Points: 90 (11d8 + 33)
Speed: 25 ft.

STR: 16 (+3)  DEX: 12 (+1)  CON: 16 (+3)
INT: 20 (+5)  WIS: 14 (+2)  CHA: 10 (+0)

Saving Throws: Con +7, Int +9
Skills: Arcana +9, Investigation +9, Smith's Tools +13 (expertise)
Senses: darkvision 60 ft., passive Perception 12
Languages: Common, Dwarvish, Elvish
Challenge: 11 (7,200 XP)

TRAITS:
**Dwarven Resilience.** Has advantage on saving throws against poison, and resistance to poison damage.
**Spellcasting.** Artificer spells (DC 17), specializes in metal/fire magic
**Can create.** +1 weapons (1 day), +2 weapons (1 week), rare magic items (1 month)
**Infusions.** Has 6 infusions active (various enhanced items)
**Right Tool for the Job.** Can create any artisan's tools

ACTIONS:
**Infused Warhammer +2.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +9 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. *Hit:* 1d8+5 bludgeoning + can cast Heat Metal through it
```

### Personality & Background
Perfectionist obsessed with craft. Speaks more to metal than people. Runs Crown Forge—makes weapons for royal guard and special commissions. Creates each piece personally. Refuses to mass-produce. Waiting list is 2-3 years. Charges fortune but worth it.

**Secret:** Can forge mythril. Only three smiths in world can. Doesn't advertise this.

### Background & History
Fourth generation Crown Forge smith, born into the craft. His great-grandfather helped build the original Crown Forge in 650 CR under King Thorin I. The Forgefire clan has passed down techniques for three centuries—secrets whispered from father to son, never written.

Durgan showed talent early, forging his first blade at age 30 (young for dwarves). Apprenticed under his father until 1050 CR, then journeyed to study other techniques. Spent twenty years in Emberforge learning volcanic smithing, ten years in the Sundaran Expanse studying desert-forged steel, and allegedly visited eastern Aethoria (he won't confirm this).

Returned to Kaer Thandros in 1120 CR and assumed his father's position after his death during the Dragon Crisis. The dragon Infernalix specifically targeted the Forge District—Durgan believes it was seeking something. He's spent 90 years trying to understand what.

Now the undisputed master of the Crown Forge, he's created weapons for three generations of royalty. His masterwork, the blade "Thrandil's Edge" carried by King Aldric IV, took seven years to complete.

### Connections
- **Patron:** King Aldric IV Thandris (primary client, respects his work)
- **Peers:** High Forge Master Borin Ironmark (only dwarf who might rival him)
- **Rivals:** Forge-Master Rurik Ironanvil of the Forgebound Guild (bitter professional dispute)
- **Apprentice:** Young Greta Ironhand (talented but impatient, reminds him of himself)
- **Secret Contact:** A mysterious Aetheian elf who provides rare materials (identity unknown)

### Secrets
1. **Mythril Mastery:** One of only three living smiths who can forge true mythril. The others are Rurik Ironanvil (his rival) and someone in Aethoria he's never met. The technique is dying.
2. **The Dragon's Purpose:** Found slag in the Forge District that shouldn't exist—dragon fire alone couldn't create it. Something else burned here. Something magical.
3. **The Incomplete Blade:** His father died mid-forge on a commissioned blade. Durgan has kept the unfinished weapon for 90 years, unable to complete it or destroy it. It whispers to him sometimes.
4. **The Eastern Journey:** He did visit Aethoria—specifically House Crystalborn. They showed him crystal-infusion techniques. He's never used them, afraid of what he might create.
5. **The Royal Request:** King Aldric IV has asked him to forge something unprecedented—a weapon that could kill an ancient dragon. He's not sure it's possible. Or ethical.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Rare Materials:** Needs adamantine from a specific crashed meteor in orc territory. Hiring adventurers for extraction.
2. **The Stolen Techniques:** His former apprentice fled to the Shadow Syndicate with forging secrets. They're making inferior but mass-produced magic weapons. Needs the apprentice stopped.
3. **The Ancient Forge:** Explorers discovered a pre-Worldrend dwarven forge in the Sealed Levels. Durgan needs it secured and studied—the techniques there might be lost to time.
4. **The Dragon Scale Commission:** A wealthy patron wants dragon-scale armor. Durgan needs fresh scales from a living dragon—and someone to get them.
5. **The Incomplete Blade:** Finally ready to complete his father's last work. But the blade requires a specific component: the tear of a dying king. He hopes King Aldric IV will volunteer a tear before his natural death, decades hence.
6. **The Rival's Challenge:** Rurik Ironanvil has challenged him to a forge-off. The prize: recognition as Thaldros's greatest smith. Durgan needs rare materials to win.
7. **The Whispering Steel:** The incomplete blade has started speaking clearly. It wants to be finished. It's telling him how. He's not sure he should listen.

### Equipment
Breastplate +1, Shield +1, Warhammer +2 (his own creation), Belt of Dwarvenkind, Bag of Holding (full of materials), masterwork smith's tools, adamantine ingots (worth 5,000 gp)

### Plot Hooks
- Will craft legendary item if party retrieves specific rare materials
- His apprentice stole secrets, fled to rival—needs recovery
- Ancient dwarven forge discovered, needs explorers to secure it
- Dragon destroyed his brother's forge, wants revenge/scales for armor

---

## Captain Borin Stoneshield
*"Every traveler is a potential threat until proven otherwise."*

**Race:** Mountain Dwarf | **Age:** 156 | **Alignment:** Lawful Neutral  
**Class:** Fighter 9 / Paladin 3 (Devotion) | **Location:** Outer Gates, Kaer Thandros

### Stat Block
```
Medium Humanoid (Dwarf), Lawful Neutral

Armor Class: 20 (plate, shield, defense)
Hit Points: 130 (9d10 + 3d10 + 48)
Speed: 25 ft.

STR: 18 (+4)  DEX: 10 (+0)  CON: 18 (+4)
INT: 10 (+0)  WIS: 14 (+2)  CHA: 14 (+2)

Saving Throws: Str +8, Con +8, Wis +6, Cha +6
Skills: None
Senses: darkvision 60 ft., passive Perception 12
Languages: Common, Dwarvish
Challenge: 10 (5,900 XP)

TRAITS:
**Dwarven Resilience.** Has advantage on saving throws against poison, and resistance to poison damage.
**Divine Smite.** Adds 2d8 radiant to hits (1st level slot)
**Lay on Hands.** 15 HP pool for healing
**Divine Sense.** Detect celestial/fiend/undead
**Sacred Weapon.** Bonus action, weapon deals radiant damage

ACTIONS:
**Longsword +2.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +10 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. *Hit:* 1d8+6 slashing + 1d8 radiant (smite)
**Extra Attack (2).** Attacks twice
```

### Personality & Background
Professional, suspicious, thorough. Questions everyone entering city. Has uncanny ability to spot lies and forged documents. Prevented three assassination attempts by catching infiltrators at gates. Never off duty. Sleeps at gatehouse. Entire life is the defense of Kaer Thandros.

**Secret:** Found evidence of traitor in royal court. Investigating quietly. Doesn't know who to trust.

### Background & History
Born in a minor clan in the Ironspine Holds, not the prestigious halls of Kaer Thandros. Came to the capital as a young dwarf seeking opportunity. Joined the City Watch at age 50, worked the Outer City beat during the worst post-Dragon reconstruction years.

Earned his reputation during the Merchant Riot of 1185 CR when grain prices spiked and hungry citizens stormed the Trade Quarter. Borin held the gates with twelve guardsmen against hundreds, never drawing blood—just talking them down while reinforcements arrived. The king himself commended him.

Took holy oaths to the Lightbringers after a near-death experience (poisoned blade from an assassin he stopped). The divine healing changed something in him. Now combines military discipline with religious conviction. Promoted to Captain of the Outer Gates in 1210 CR.

Has personally stopped three assassination attempts against the crown. The first earned him his posting; the second got him the enchanted longsword; the third made him paranoid. He knows there are more enemies inside the walls than outside.

### Connections
- **Commander:** Lord Commander Thrain Ironoak (respects his judgment)
- **Religious Superior:** Lord Commander Gareth Lightbane of the Lightbringers
- **Partner:** Watch Commander Gregor Ironhand (human, trusts with his life)
- **Informant:** Silas the Fence (criminal who provides intelligence for immunity)
- **Suspicious Of:** Multiple nobles who've requested "special entry procedures"

### Secrets
1. **The Court Traitor:** Intercepted coded messages proving someone in the Royal Quarter is selling information. The code is unbroken, but the drop point is a noble's estate. Which noble?
2. **The Third Assassin:** The third assassin he stopped wasn't aiming for the king—they were aiming for Prince Aldric. Why target the heir specifically?
3. **The Gate Records:** Keeps secret logs of everyone entering the city. Has noticed patterns—certain people arrive before certain "accidents" happen.
4. **The Bribe Offers:** Has been offered enormous bribes to "not notice" certain visitors. He's declined, but he's recorded every offer and who made it.
5. **The Divine Vision:** During his healing, he saw something—a moment of darkness swallowing Kaer Thandros. He believes it's prophetic. He doesn't know how to stop it.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Coded Messages:** Needs someone outside the guard to decode intercepted messages—can't trust internal cryptographers.
2. **The Suspicious Travelers:** Had to admit a diplomatic party he's certain contains infiltrators. Needs them watched without official involvement.
3. **The Gate Sabotage:** Someone is weakening the outer gate mechanisms. Needs investigation before the next assault.
4. **The Assassin's Employer:** The third assassin was a professional from the Shadow Syndicate. Who hired them to kill Prince Aldric?
5. **The Underground Entrance:** Discovered evidence of a tunnel bypassing his gates entirely. Needs explorers to find and seal it.
6. **The Briber's Identity:** Ready to spring a trap on whoever's offering bribes. Needs trustworthy witnesses who can testify in royal court.
7. **The Vision Quest:** A Lightbringer superior suggested his vision might be clarified through a sacred quest. He can't leave his post—but could sponsor others.

### Plot Hooks
- Needs party to investigate suspicious travelers he had to let pass
- Wants agents to test gate security (hired to infiltrate)
- Has information about incoming threat, needs it delivered to king
- Falsely accused of letting assassin through—party must clear his name

---

## Sage Thelmar Runescribe
*"The old magic remembers. We must remember with it."*

**Race:** Human | **Age:** 67 | **Alignment:** Neutral Good  
**Class:** Wizard 12 (School of Divination) | **Location:** Royal Tower, Kaer Thandros

### Stat Block
```
Medium Humanoid (Human), Neutral Good

Armor Class: 15 (mage armor, ring)
Hit Points: 66 (12d6 + 24)
Speed: 30 ft.

STR: 8 (-1)  DEX: 12 (+1)  CON: 14 (+2)
INT: 20 (+5)  WIS: 16 (+3)  CHA: 12 (+1)

Saving Throws: Int +9, Wis +7
Skills: Arcana +13, History +13, Insight +7
Senses: passive Perception 13
Languages: Common, Elvish
Challenge: 11 (7,200 XP)

TRAITS:
**Spellcasting.** 12th-level wizard, DC 17
**Portent (2/day).** Roll 2d20, replace any roll with these
**Expert Divination.** Regains spell slot when casting divination
**Specializes in.** Scrying, Divination, Identify, Legend Lore, Contact Other Plane
ACTIONS:
**Quarterstaff.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +3 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. *Hit:* 2 (1d6 - 1) bludgeoning damage.

**Spellcasting.** Thelmar is a 12th-level spellcaster. His spellcasting ability is Intelligence (spell save DC 17, +9 to hit with spell attacks). He has the following wizard spells prepared:

Cantrips (at will): *light, mage hand, message, prestidigitation*
1st level (4 slots): *detect magic, identify, shield, sleep*
2nd level (3 slots): *detect thoughts, locate object, see invisibility*
3rd level (3 slots): *clairvoyance, counterspell, dispel magic*
4th level (3 slots): *arcane eye, divination, locate creature*
5th level (2 slots): *contact other plane, legend lore, scrying*
6th level (1 slot): *true seeing*

**Portent (2/Day).** When Thelmar finishes a long rest, he rolls two d20s and records the numbers. He can replace any attack roll, saving throw, or ability check made by him or a creature he can see with one of these rolls.
```

### Personality & Background
Elderly royal advisor. Scholarly, absent-minded, brilliant. Has advised three generations of kings. More interested in ancient texts than politics but understands both. Believes current political tensions are tied to pre-Worldrend events. Researching constantly.

**Secret:** Has discovered evidence that third bloodline exists. Hasn't told King yet—trying to verify first.

### Background & History
Born in a small Heartlands village to a family of scribes. Showed magical aptitude early and was sent to the Arcanum in Silverpine at age 14. Excelled in divination studies under Archmage Veridian Starweaver, becoming one of his finest students.

Recruited to Kaer Thandros in 1202 CR when King Aldric III needed a royal diviner. Has served the crown for 45 years across three reigns. His predictions about the Merchant Riot of 1185 CR (before his official posting) brought him to royal attention—he warned of unrest six months before it occurred.

Survived the Dragon Crisis of 1156 CR as a young apprentice in Silverpine, but the experience haunted him. Has spent decades researching why the dragon departed. His divinations suggest something negotiated with it—but his visions of that moment are always obscured.

Now elderly and knowing his time is limited, he works frantically to complete his life's research: understanding the pre-Worldrend royal succession and why both House Thandris and House Aethermere believe they're the legitimate heirs.

### Connections
- **Serves:** King Aldric IV Thandris (trusts his counsel completely)
- **Mentor:** Archmage Veridian Starweaver (still corresponds, old friends)
- **Rival:** High Diviner Celestia Starborn of Silverpine (academic disagreement)
- **Apprentice:** Young Erenna (promising but impatient)
- **Secret Correspondent:** An anonymous contact in Aethoria who shares research

### Secrets
1. **The Third Bloodline:** His research suggests a third royal line exists—neither Thandris nor Aethermere, but descendants of a sibling history forgot. If true, the entire succession dispute is moot.
2. **The Dragon's Deal:** His divinations show King Aldric III's father made some kind of bargain with Infernalix. He can't see the terms, but the dragon's departure wasn't random.
3. **The Prophecy Suppression:** He's had a vision of Kaer Thandros burning that he's hidden from the king. Showing it might cause the very panic that makes it come true.
4. **The Aetheian Contact:** His anonymous correspondent claims to be from House Starweaver. They're sharing information that contradicts both continental histories.
5. **The Approaching Death:** He's divined his own death—within the year. He's racing to complete his research and find someone worthy to continue it.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Lost Archive:** Pre-Worldrend texts exist in a ruin beneath the Sundering Sea. Needs adventurers to retrieve them before they're lost forever.
2. **The Third Heir:** Has a lead on the third bloodline's descendants. Needs discrete investigation—if true, this could reshape continental politics.
3. **The Vision Verification:** Needs heroes to travel to the site of his disaster vision to see if it can be prevented.
4. **The Successor Search:** Looking for someone with divination talent to inherit his research. Will test promising candidates.
5. **The Correspondent Meeting:** His Aetheian contact wants to meet in person. Needs protection for the dangerous journey to neutral Port Myrthen.
6. **The Dragon Research:** Needs someone to investigate the Ashfall Barrens where Infernalix was last seen—to understand what the dragon wanted.
7. **The Royal Revelation:** Has finally gathered enough evidence to present to King Aldric IV. Needs witnesses he trusts in case something goes wrong.

### Plot Hooks
- Needs ancient text recovered from dangerous location
- Vision shows party's importance to realm's future—wants to help
- Possessed artifact needs identification, only he can do it
- Research leads to discovery that requires adventurers

---

## Brother Tormund
*"Thoran protects all who stand firm. Stand firm."*

**Race:** Human | **Age:** 42 | **Alignment:** Lawful Good  
**Class:** Cleric 10 (War Domain) | **Location:** Temple of Thoran, Kaer Thandros

### Stat Block
```
Medium Humanoid (Human), Lawful Good

Armor Class: 19 (plate, shield)
Hit Points: 85 (10d8 + 30)
Speed: 30 ft.

STR: 16 (+3)  DEX: 10 (+0)  CON: 16 (+3)
INT: 11 (+0)  WIS: 18 (+4)  CHA: 14 (+2)

Saving Throws: Wis +8, Cha +6
Skills: None
Senses: passive Perception 14
Languages: Common
Challenge: 9 (5,000 XP)

TRAITS:
**Spells.** Cleric spells (DC 16), War Domain spells
**War Priest (3/day).** Bonus action attack
**Divine Strike.** Extra 1d8 to weapon damage

ACTIONS:
**Warhammer +2.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +9 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. *Hit:* 1d8+5 bludgeoning + 1d8 radiant
**Channel Divinity.** Guided Strike (+10 to hit) or Turn Undead
```

### Personality & Background
Former soldier turned priest. Runs temple dedicated to Thoran (god of protection). Provides blessings to guards and soldiers. Counsels warriors about duty and sacrifice. Still trains with weapons daily. Believes strength and faith are inseparable.

**Secret:** Had vision of massive battle coming. Preparing temple to serve as field hospital.

### Background & History  
Born Marcus Tormund in Crossvale to a farming family. Joined the Royal Army at 18, served in the Northern Border Campaigns against orc raiders throughout his twenties. Witnessed countless deaths and grew disillusioned with violence without purpose.

The turning point came during the Battle of Iron Pass (1223 CR) when his company was ambushed and nearly wiped out. Tormund held a defensive line for six hours, protecting wounded soldiers, until reinforcements arrived. He was the only one of the rear guard still standing. During that stand, he prayed to every god he could name—and Thoran answered.

After recovering from his wounds, he left the military and took holy orders. Trained at the Temple of Thoran in Ironhold, then transferred to Kaer Thandros in 1230 CR. Built the temple's warrior-priest program from scratch, training soldier-clerics who protect without seeking conquest.

Now serves as the temple's head priest and chief counselor to soldiers struggling with the weight of their duties. His practical approach—combining military discipline with spiritual guidance—has made him beloved by the City Watch and Royal Army alike.

### Connections
- **Superior:** Archbishop Morven (respects but sometimes disagrees on doctrine)
- **Military Contacts:** Lord Commander Thrain Ironoak (former comrade), Captain Borin Stoneshield (provides spiritual counsel)
- **Allies:** Father Aldric Tidekeeper of Goldreach (fellow war-cleric)
- **Congregants:** Hundreds of soldiers, guards, and veterans who attend his services
- **Rival:** Brother Marcus of the Lightbringers (doctrinal disputes about the role of warfare)

### Secrets
1. **The Vision:** Saw a massive battle coming to Kaer Thandros—worse than the Dragon Crisis. Siege weapons, dark magic, armies beyond counting. He's quietly stockpiling supplies and training healers.
2. **The Survivor's Guilt:** Still dreams of the men who died at Iron Pass. Sometimes questions whether he truly heard Thoran, or just his own desperate will to survive.
3. **The Deserter Sanctuary:** Secretly shelters soldiers who've deserted due to trauma rather than cowardice. Helps them find peace before turning themselves in or starting new lives.
4. **The Forbidden Ritual:** Knows a prayer that can bind a dying soldier's soul to his weapon, creating a guardian spirit. It's not heresy, but the church leadership would disapprove. He's done it twice.
5. **The Traitor's Confession:** A dying soldier confessed to selling information to enemies. Tormund is bound by confession's sanctity but knows the name of someone who should be investigated.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Battle Preparation:** Needs help preparing the temple for mass casualties. Supplies, cots, healers, escape routes—all without causing panic.
2. **The Haunted Soldier:** A veteran is possessed by something from the battlefield. Needs both combat skill and spiritual knowledge to help.
3. **The Deserter Crisis:** One of his sheltered deserters was actually a spy. Now Tormund needs help finding him before the spy sells what he's learned.
4. **The Sacred Weapon:** A legendary warrior's blade needs to be recovered from a battlefield. The soldier's ghost won't rest until it's returned to his family.
5. **The Confession Dilemma:** The traitor from confession is about to be promoted to a sensitive position. Tormund can't break the seal but needs someone to find evidence independently.
6. **The Iron Pass Pilgrimage:** Finally ready to return to where his faith was born. Needs escort through dangerous territory—and witnesses for what he might find there.
7. **The Vision Quest:** A prophecy suggests someone can prevent his vision of destruction. He's looking for that person among adventurers who pass through.
