## Miller Tobias Waterwheel
**"The mill turns day and night, just like the world. We feed the wheel, the wheel feeds us."**

**Status:** ALIVE - Master Miller, Waterwheel Engineer  
**CR:** 4 (Expert miller with mechanical expertise)  
**Race:** Human (Heartland born)  
**Age:** 48  

### Stat Block
```


### Background & History
The Waterwheel mill has ground grain for the village of Millbrook for two hundred years. Tobias is the fifth generation to run it, and possibly the last—his sons have left for city trades, and his daughter shows no interest in flour-dusted labor.

He's content with his life: steady work, respected position, enough coin to be comfortable. He knows every farmer within ten miles, their crops, their troubles, their secrets. The mill is where people talk while waiting for their grain, and Tobias listens more than he speaks.

But lately, something is wrong with the river. Fish are dying, the water tastes strange, and the wheel has been harder to turn. Tobias has been investigating quietly, and what he's found frightens him.

### Connections
- **Community:** Millbrook village (300 residents)
- **Customers:** Every farm within ten miles
- **Daughter:** Sarah Waterwheel (herbalist, lives in town)
- **Friend:** Forester Galen Sustainharvest (shares concerns about the land)
- **Worry:** Whatever is poisoning the river

### Secrets
1. **The Upstream Source:** Has traced the river pollution to an abandoned mine. Something is leaking from it.
2. **The Listening Ear:** Knows secrets about half the valley from mill conversations. Never tells.
3. **The Hidden Fortune:** Has more saved than anyone suspects. Waiting to see if his daughter needs it.
4. **The Old Tunnels:** The mill basement connects to tunnels that lead... somewhere. Never explored far.
5. **The War Past:** Served as a soldier in his youth. Killed people. Became a miller partly to atone.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The River Investigation:** Needs help investigating the abandoned mine safely.
2. **The Tunnel Mystery:** Strange sounds from the basement tunnels. Needs someone to explore.
3. **The Secret Keeper:** Has information the party needs. Might share if asked right.
4. **The Daughter's Trouble:** Sarah is in some kind of difficulty. Needs discrete help.
5. **The Mill Defense:** Something is threatening the mill. Needs capable fighters.

---
Medium Humanoid (Human), Neutral Good

Armor Class: 13 (padded armor)
Hit Points: 52 (7d8 + 21)
Speed: 30 ft.

STR: 14 (+2)  DEX: 12 (+1)  CON: 16 (+3)
INT: 16 (+3)  WIS: 14 (+2)  CHA: 13 (+1)

Saving Throws: Con +5, Int +5
Skills: Investigation +5, Nature +4, Perception +4, Tinker's Tools +7 (expertise), Engineer's Tools +7 (expertise), Insight +4
Senses: Passive Perception 14
Languages: Common, Dwarvish (engineering terms)
Challenge Rating: 4 (1,100 XP)

SPECIAL ABILITIES:
Master Engineer: Has advantage on all checks related to mechanical devices, water systems, mills, or engineering problems. Can identify mechanical issues by sound or vibration.

Hydraulic Expertise: Understands water flow, pressure, and mechanical advantage. Can calculate optimal wheel designs, water speeds, and power outputs.

Jury Rigger: Given basic tools and materials, can temporarily repair almost any mechanical device. Repairs last 24 hours before needing proper maintenance.

Powder Knowledge: Has extensive experience with grain dust explosions and fire prevention. Knows how to prevent or cause explosive conditions.

Precise Calculations: Can mentally calculate weights, volumes, ratios, and mechanical advantages with perfect accuracy. Never makes math errors.

Tinkerer's Eye: Can assess the quality and value of any mechanical device at a glance. Knows if something is well-made, defective, or sabotaged.

ACTIONS:
Multiattack: Makes two attacks with his Heavy Wrench or Grain Sack.

Heavy Wrench: Melee Weapon Attack: +4 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d8+2 bludgeoning damage.
Special: On hit, can attempt to disarm target if they're wielding a mechanical or metal weapon (contested Athletics check).

Grain Sack: Improvised Weapon: +4 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d6+2 bludgeoning damage.
Special: On hit, target must succeed DC 13 Strength save or be knocked prone (40 lbs of grain is heavy).

Mechanical Trap (Preparation Required): Given 10 minutes, can rig a mechanical trap using mill equipment. Examples:
- Swinging beam (DC 13 Dex save, 2d10 bludgeoning)
- Grain avalanche (20-ft cone, DC 13 Str save, 3d6 bludgeoning + buried)
- Millstone drop (30-ft area, DC 14 Dex save, 4d10 bludgeoning + prone)

Sabotage Detection (1/Day): Examines mechanical device and instantly knows if it's been tampered with, how, and approximately when.

REACTIONS:
Deflect Machinery: When a mechanical device attacks him or an ally within 5 ft., can use reaction to jam it with a tool. Device malfunctions and misses its attack.

Practical Knowledge: When an ally within 30 ft. makes an Intelligence check related to mechanics or engineering, can provide guidance granting advantage on the check.
```

### Equipment
- **Armor:** Padded Leather Apron (AC 11, protects against flour dust, sparks)
- **Primary Tool:** Heavy Wrench (2 ft. long, masterwork, doubles as weapon)
- **Tools:** Tinker's tools, engineer's tools (both masterwork quality)
- **Belt:** Tool belt with hammers, pliers, oil can, measuring tape
- **Knife:** Utility knife (1d4 damage, for cutting rope/sacks)
- **Lantern:** Hooded lantern (essential in mill work, oil flask)
- **Other:** Chalk for marking, leather gloves, safety goggles (dwarven made)
- **Emergency:** Length of rope, pulleys, spare gears

### Physical Description
Average height (5'10", 180 lbs) but powerfully built from years of hauling grain sacks and working machinery. Flour dust permanently stains his clothes and hair white, making him look older. Practical brown work clothes always covered in flour. Strong hands with blacksmith-like grip strength. Brown eyes that constantly assess mechanical workings. Short practical hair usually white with flour. Clean-shaven face dusted with flour. Smells of fresh flour, water, and machine oil. Moves with efficiency of someone used to dangerous machinery.

### Personality Traits
- Constantly wipes flour off clothes (futile habit)
- Explains things using mill and water metaphors
- Listens to machine sounds to diagnose problems
- Practical and direct in speech
- Takes pride in the quality of ground flour
- Patient with questions, impatient with incompetence
- Always knows what time it is by mill wheel rotations

**Ideals:**
- **Precision:** "Flour quality depends on perfect millstone gaps. Life's the same—precision matters."
- **Service:** "Every loaf of bread starts here. That's responsibility."
- **Innovation:** "There's always a better wheel design. Always room to improve."
- **Reliability:** "The mill runs 24 hours because people rely on it. So do I."

**Bonds:**
- His watermill (built it himself 20 years ago)
- The town of Willowbrook (feeds them all)
- His apprentice Jonas (teaching him the trade)
- The river (source of his power and livelihood)
- His late wife's memory (she designed the wheel)
- The mechanical innovation he's working on

**Flaws:**
- Obsessive about mill maintenance (checks it hourly)
- Fears fire above all else (grain dust explosions)
- Guilty about profiting when grain prices rise during famine
- Distrusts magic (prefers mechanical solutions)
- Sometimes ignores family for mill work
- Paranoid about sabotage after previous incident

### Roleplaying Notes
- Constantly wipes flour from hands
- Checks pocket watch obsessively
- Taps rhythm of mill wheel on tables
- Explains everything with water flow analogies
- Offers fresh bread to visitors
- Mutters calculations under breath
- Always coated in fine white flour dust

**Key Details:**
- Owns and operates Willowbrook's primary grain mill
- Processes grain for 20 miles around
- Designed revolutionary waterwheel that's 30% more efficient
- Dwarven engineers study his wheel design
- Supplies flour to both kingdoms
- Maintains strategic grain reserves during harvest
- His mill is local news center (everyone visits)

### Secrets
1. **Hidden Reserves:** Maintains secret flour stockpile for famine (illegal but moral)
2. **Sabotage Incident:** Mill was sabotaged 5 years ago during grain shortage; he knows who did it
3. **Wife's Death:** She died in mill accident he blames himself for; her design still powers the wheel
4. **Mechanical Discovery:** Accidentally discovered something while repairing wheel—a pre-Worldrend gear system
5. **Spy Network:** Because everyone visits the mill, he hears everything—unofficial information broker
6. **The Black Flour:** During night shifts, he mills special grain for mysterious client
7. **Water Rights Conflict:** Upstream noble wants to divert river; would destroy his mill

### Plot Hooks
1. **Sabotage Mystery:** Mill malfunctions dangerously; evidence points to deliberate tampering
2. **Water Rights War:** Upstream nobleman damming river; mill will fail; party must negotiate/intimidate
3. **Ancient Mechanism:** Pre-Worldrend gears found in riverbed; he needs help investigating
4. **Grain Theft:** Large quantities of grain disappearing from mill at night; supernatural involvement?
5. **Fire Crisis:** Grain dust explosion risk during dry season; party must help fireproof the mill
6. **Apprentice Trouble:** His apprentice Jonas is being recruited by criminals; Tobias needs intervention
7. **Engineering Competition:** Dwarven engineers challenge his wheel design; contest has stakes
8. **Flood Warning:** Upstream dam failing; party must evacuate town and save the mill
9. **Merchant Pressure:** Wealthy merchant wants to buy mill for cheap; using intimidation tactics
10. **The Secret Flour:** His mysterious night client revealed as Unbound operative; he's unknowingly involved

### Connections
- **Lady Seraphina Riverbrook:** She owns land upstream; tension over water rights
- **Master Carpenter Aldric Woodwise:** Built waterwheel housing; good friends
- **Merchant-Prince Kael Icewind:** Major grain buyer; business relationship
- **Captain Blacksail:** Unknown to Tobias, pirates buying his "special" night flour
- **Druid Thornwood:** Consults about river health and water flow
- **Forge-Master Thordak Lavaheart:** Traded gear-making techniques
- **The Unbound:** Unknowingly grinding grain for their operations

## Lady Seraphina Riverbrook
**"Land ownership is a sacred trust. We do not own the earth; we are merely its temporary stewards."**

**Status:** ALIVE - Noble Landowner, River Rights Mediator  
**CR:** 6 (Aristocrat with diplomatic and combat training)  
**Race:** Human (Noble bloodline)  
**Age:** 39  

### Stat Block
```


### Background & History
Seraphina was born to wealth and privilege, the only daughter of Lord Riverbrook. She was expected to marry well and manage a noble household. Instead, she discovered a passion for governance, studying law and administration while her father prepared her for a political marriage.

When her father died unexpectedly, she had to fight to inherit—the law was unclear, and cousins contested her claim. She won through a combination of legal brilliance and strategic marriage to a lower noble who was content to let her rule. She's been Lady of Riverbrook for fifteen years.

She's transformed her domain into a model of efficient governance: roads maintained, justice fair, taxes reasonable. Other nobles either admire or resent her success. She's ambitious but patient, building alliances for a long-term goal she rarely discusses.

### Connections
- **Domain:** Riverbrook territory (12,000 residents)
- **Husband:** Lord Gareth Riverbrook (supportive, handles military)
- **Rival:** Lord Aldris Goldshore (political opponent)
- **Ally:** Various reform-minded nobles
- **Goal:** The High Council seat

### Secrets
1. **The Council Ambition:** Working toward a seat on the High Council. Would be the first woman in three generations.
2. **The Marriage Arrangement:** Her marriage is purely political. Gareth prefers men; they're friends, not lovers.
3. **The Cousin Problem:** The cousin who contested her inheritance hasn't given up. She's watching him.
4. **The Adopted Heir:** Secretly looking to adopt an heir since she and Gareth will have no children.
5. **The Information Network:** Has built an intelligence network to rival any spy master's.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Political Alliance:** Offers the party patronage in exchange for services.
2. **The Cousin Crisis:** The cousin is making moves. Needs investigation or counteraction.
3. **The Heir Search:** Looking for the right person to adopt. Might test party members.
4. **The Reform Proposal:** Working on major governance reform. Needs allies to push it through.
5. **The Intelligence Trade:** Has information the party needs. Willing to trade.

---
Medium Humanoid (Human), Lawful Neutral

Armor Class: 16 (studded leather + Dex)
Hit Points: 72 (11d8 + 22)
Speed: 30 ft.

STR: 12 (+1)  DEX: 16 (+3)  CON: 14 (+2)
INT: 16 (+3)  WIS: 14 (+2)  CHA: 18 (+4)

Saving Throws: Dex +6, Wis +5, Cha +7
Skills: Deception +7, History +6, Insight +8 (expertise), Intimidation +7, Perception +5, Persuasion +10 (expertise), Rapier +6
Senses: Passive Perception 15
Languages: Common, Elvish, Dwarvish, Infernal (business contracts), Sylvan
Challenge Rating: 6 (2,300 XP)

SPECIAL ABILITIES:
Noble Authority: Has advantage on Charisma checks when dealing with commoners, merchants, or lower nobility. Can invoke noble privilege to access restricted areas or demand audience with officials.

Diplomatic Immunity: In civilized areas, attacking her openly brings serious legal consequences. She can parley even with hostile forces (though this doesn't guarantee safety).

Resource Management: Has extensive knowledge of land management, water rights, taxation, agriculture, and resource allocation. Can assess land value, crop yields, and economic viability at a glance.

Legal Expert: Knows noble law, land rights, contract law, and water rights extensively. Can craft ironclad contracts or find loopholes in existing ones.

Dueling Training: Trained in noble fencing arts. Has advantage on Initiative and attack rolls when fighting one-on-one honorable duels.

Political Network: Maintains relationships with nobility across both kingdoms. Can send messages and gather information through her network (takes 1-3 days depending on distance).

ACTIONS:
Multiattack: Makes two attacks with her Rapier or one rapier attack and uses Commanding Presence.

Riverbrook Rapier +1: Melee Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d8+4 piercing damage.
Special: Family heirloom blade. On critical hit, target must succeed DC 15 Constitution save or be poisoned for 1 minute (blade is enchanted with subtle venom coating that replenishes daily).

Elegant Riposte (Recharge 5-6): When a creature misses her with a melee attack, she immediately counterattacks. +7 to hit, 2d8+4 piercing damage.

Main Gauche: Melee Weapon Attack: +6 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d4+3 piercing damage.
Special: Used for parrying. See reactions.

Commanding Presence: Target one creature within 30 ft. that can hear and understand her. Target must succeed DC 15 Wisdom save or be charmed or frightened (her choice) for 1 minute. On successful save, immune for 24 hours.

Demand Negotiation (1/Day): Forces a pause in combat if at least one enemy can be reasoned with. All combatants must succeed DC 15 Wisdom save or be compelled to hear her out for 1 minute. Attacking her during this time breaks the effect.

REACTIONS:
Parry: When attacked with a melee weapon, adds +3 AC against that attack using her main gauche. If this causes the attack to miss, she can immediately riposte (no action cost, +6 to hit, 1d8+3 damage).

Political Leverage: When threatened, can invoke her noble connections. Attackers must succeed DC 15 Wisdom save or hesitate (disadvantage on their next attack). Only works once per encounter per enemy.
```

### Equipment
- **Armor:** Fine Studded Leather (AC 14, disguised as fashionable clothing)
- **Primary Weapon:** Riverbrook Rapier +1 (family heirloom, magically keen)
- **Secondary:** Main Gauche (parrying dagger, masterwork)
- **Clothing:** Noble's traveling outfit (worth 50 gp, reinforced silk)
- **Jewelry:** Signet ring (family crest, proves identity), pearl necklace (worth 500 gp)
- **Documents:** Leather portfolio with land deeds, contracts, maps
- **Tools:** Wax seal, noble stationery, ledger books
- **Emergency:** Hidden lockbox key (opens vault in Kaer Thandros)
- **Potions:** 2 potions of healing, 1 potion of water breathing (insurance)
- **Mount:** Well-bred riding horse (outside), saddle and tack

### Physical Description
Elegant and commanding presence (5'8", 145 lbs) with the poise of generations of nobility. Auburn hair worn in practical noble style, sometimes covered with silk scarf. Striking green eyes that assess people instantly. Fair skin despite outdoor work managing estates. Wears practical but expensive clothing—reinforced silk that looks decorative but allows movement. Always carries rapier at hip, though she makes it look decorative. Moves with fencer's grace. Smells of rose water and parchment. Hands show evidence of both sword practice and ledger work.

### Personality Traits
- Speaks with clear authority, expects to be obeyed
- Listens intently to all sides before deciding
- Uses legal terminology in casual conversation
- Taps fingers when calculating costs/benefits
- Maintains perfect posture always
- Treats commoners with respect (unusual for nobility)
- Quick to correct contract errors or unfair deals

**Ideals:**
- **Justice:** "Law must protect both the powerful and the powerless, or it protects no one."
- **Stewardship:** "This land will outlast me. I must leave it better than I found it."
- **Honor:** "My word is my bond. Once given, I do not break it."
- **Balance:** "The river must flow for the miller and the farmer both."

**Bonds:**
- Her family estate (Riverbrook Manor, 500 acres)
- The people living on her lands (300+ tenants)
- Her deceased father's legacy (trying to honor)
- The Riverbrook family name (ancient lineage)
- Her younger brother Marcus (captain in the army)
- The river itself (family named for it)

**Flaws:**
- Stubborn about family honor and tradition
- Struggles to trust after betrayal by former steward
- Sometimes prioritizes law over people's immediate needs
- Guilty about living in wealth while tenants struggle
- Fears becoming cruel like other nobles
- Duty-bound to arranged marriage she doesn't want

### Roleplaying Notes
- Stands straight, shoulders back, even when tired
- Makes eye contact that forces honesty
- Uses "we" when speaking about estate matters
- Quotes father: "Father always said..."
- Signs documents with elaborate flourish
- Touches rapier hilt when threatened
- Speaks firmly but never shouts

**Key Details:**
- Controls water rights for 50-mile section of river
- Manages 500-acre estate with 300+ tenant farmers
- Mediates land disputes between nobles and commoners
- Trained in swordplay since childhood (family tradition)
- Opposed to her family's arranged marriage plan
- Advocates for tenant farmers' rights (controversial)
- Secretly funding irrigation projects from personal wealth
- Has veto power over water use decisions

### Secrets
1. **The Arranged Marriage:** Family pressuring her to marry Lord Crimson (who's secretly Unbound)
2. **Father's Death:** Suspects he was murdered over water rights; has no proof
3. **Hidden Heir:** Her brother Marcus is legitimate heir but enlisted to avoid responsibility
4. **Tenant Relief:** Using personal fortune to forgive tenant debts during hard times (family doesn't know)
5. **The Betrayal:** Former steward embezzled 10,000 gold; she paid it back quietly to protect family name
6. **Illegal Charity:** Redirects taxes to feed poor families (technically illegal but morally right)
7. **Romantic Secret:** In love with Captain Marcus Frontiersman (the werewolf), doesn't know his curse
8. **Political Target:** Lord Crimson (Unbound) wants her land and has tried to intimidate her
9. **Water Scheme:** Discovered that upstream nobles plan to dam the river illegally
10. **The Vault:** Her family vault contains pre-Worldrend artifact that grants water control

### Plot Hooks
1. **Water Rights War:** Upstream nobles damming river; devastating downstream farmers; she needs force
2. **The Forced Marriage:** Family pressuring marriage to Lord Crimson; she needs escape plan or exposure of him
3. **Murder Investigation:** Her father's death ruled accident; she believes murder; wants truth
4. **Tenant Uprising:** Some tenants plan rebellion over taxes; she wants peaceful resolution
5. **Assassination Attempt:** Lord Crimson hiring assassins; party must provide security
6. **Legal Battle:** Corrupt judge ruling against her in water rights case; needs evidence or intimidation
7. **The Vault:** Family vault flooding; must recover artifact before water destroys it
8. **Brother's Trouble:** Marcus Frontiersman (her werewolf love interest) needs help with curse
9. **Irrigation Project:** Ambitious canal project needs protection from saboteurs
10. **Noble Conspiracy:** Multiple nobles conspiring to steal her land; must expose them

### Connections
- **Captain Marcus Frontiersman:** Secret romantic interest (doesn't know he's a werewolf)
- **Miller Tobias Waterwheel:** Business relationship over water rights; mutual respect
- **Master Carpenter Aldric Woodwise:** Commissioned manor renovations; good relationship
- **Lord Crimson:** Arranged marriage target; she despises him (unknowingly Unbound)
- **Lady Elara Swiftwind:** Fellow noblewoman and ally against corrupt nobles
- **Merchant-Prince Kael Icewind:** Business rival over trade routes
- **Archmage Veridian Starweaver:** Corresponded about irrigation magic
- **Druid Thornwood:** Consults about river ecosystem health
- **The Unbound:** Targeted by them due to her land and water control

## Captain Marcus Frontiersman (Werewolf)
**"I protect this frontier from monsters. The irony isn't lost on me."**

**Status:** ALIVE - Frontier Captain, Cursed Werewolf  
**CR:** 8 (Veteran fighter with lycanthropy)  
**Race:** Human (cursed with werewolf lycanthropy)  
**Age:** 36  

### Stat Block
```


### Background & History
Marcus was a promising young captain in the border guard when the werewolf pack attacked. Most of his patrol died; he was bitten and left for dead. He survived, changed, and faced a choice: surrender to the beast or master it.

Twenty years later, he's done the impossible—maintained his humanity while using his lycanthropy to protect the frontier. The wild lands are full of creatures that normal soldiers can't fight; Marcus can. He operates alone, reporting to commanders who officially don't know what he is.

He's not cured—there's no cure. But he's found equilibrium: running wild during full moons in unpopulated areas, taking wolfsbane to maintain control, and channeling the predator inside toward protecting the helpless. It costs him everything else. He has no family, few friends, and no hope of a normal life.

### Connections
- **Chain of Command:** Reports to Commander Kael Stormwatcher (knows the truth)
- **Pack:** The Silver Wolf (complicated)
- **Ally:** Hermit Sage Morganna Whisperwind (provides wolfsbane)
- **Enemy:** The werewolf pack that turned him (still hunting them)
- **Self:** The beast within

### Secrets
1. **The Pack Hunt:** Has been systematically hunting the werewolves who turned him. Three left.
2. **The Control Secret:** His control isn't natural—it's a ritual Morganna developed. Requires monthly renewal.
3. **The Bite Risk:** Has accidentally bitten two people. Found them and ensured they received help.
4. **The Retirement Dream:** Wants to find a cure and live normally. Knows it probably doesn't exist.
5. **The Silver Wolf Connection:** The Silver Wolf is his turned mentor. They're linked but on opposite paths.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Hunt Continues:** Has located another werewolf from the original pack. Needs help taking it down.
2. **The Control Crisis:** Something is interfering with his control ritual. Needs investigation.
3. **The New Victim:** Someone has been bitten. He needs help getting them to Morganna.
4. **The Silver Wolf Conflict:** The confrontation with his mentor is coming. Needs allies.
5. **The Cure Rumor:** Heard of a possible cure. Needs someone to investigate while he stays hidden.

---
Medium Humanoid (Human, Shapechanger), Chaotic Good

Armor Class: 17 (half-plate)
Hit Points: 112 (14d10 + 42)
Speed: 30 ft. (40 ft. in hybrid or wolf form)

STR: 18 (+4)  DEX: 14 (+2)  CON: 16 (+3)
INT: 12 (+1)  WIS: 14 (+2)  CHA: 15 (+2)

Saving Throws: Str +7, Con +6, Wis +5
Skills: Athletics +7, Insight +5, Intimidation +5, Perception +5, Survival +8 (expertise)
Damage Immunities: Bludgeoning, Piercing, and Slashing from nonmagical attacks not made with silvered weapons (in hybrid or wolf form)
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft. (in wolf or hybrid form), Passive Perception 15
Languages: Common, Frontier dialect
Challenge Rating: 8 (3,900 XP)

SPECIAL ABILITIES:
Shapechanger: Can use an action to polymorph into a wolf-humanoid hybrid or into a Large wolf, or back into human form. Statistics are the same in each form, except as noted. Equipment melds into new form. Reverts to human if reduced to 0 HP.

Keen Hearing and Smell: Has advantage on Wisdom (Perception) checks that rely on hearing or smell (in wolf or hybrid form).

Pack Tactics: Has advantage on attack rolls against a creature if at least one ally is within 5 ft. of the creature and isn't incapacitated.

Lycanthropy Control (Partial): Can resist transformation during normal full moons with DC 15 Wisdom save. On failure, transforms and retains vague awareness but is aggressive. Always transforms during blood moons (no save).

Silver Vulnerability: Takes normal damage from silvered weapons (bypasses immunity).

Military Tactician: Grants +2 to initiative rolls for all allies within 30 ft. Can use bonus action to grant ally advantage on their next attack.

Frontier Survival Expert: Has advantage on Survival checks in wilderness. Cannot become lost in natural terrain.

ACTIONS (Human Form):
Multiattack: Makes three attacks with longsword or two with longbow.

Longsword +1: Melee Weapon Attack: +8 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d8+5 slashing damage (1d10+5 versatile).

Longbow: Ranged Weapon Attack: +5 to hit, range 150/600 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d8+2 piercing damage.

Leadership (Recharge 5-6): For 1 minute, all allies within 30 ft. gain +1 to attack rolls and saving throws.

ACTIONS (Hybrid Form):
Multiattack: Makes one bite attack and two claw attacks, or three claw attacks.

Bite: Melee Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d8+4 piercing damage. Target must succeed DC 14 Constitution save or be cursed with werewolf lycanthropy.

Claw: Melee Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 2d4+4 slashing damage.

Longsword +1 (Two-Handed): Melee Weapon Attack: +8 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d10+5 slashing damage. (Can wield weapons in hybrid form with difficulty)

Howl of the Hunt (1/Day): Releases a terrifying howl. All creatures within 60 ft. that can hear must succeed DC 14 Wisdom save or be frightened for 1 minute. Allies gain advantage on their next attack.

ACTIONS (Wolf Form):
Bite: Melee Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 2d6+4 piercing damage. Target must succeed DC 14 Constitution save or be cursed with werewolf lycanthropy.

Pounce: If the wolf moves at least 20 ft. straight toward a creature and hits with bite, target must succeed DC 14 Strength save or be knocked prone. If prone, wolf can make another bite attack as bonus action.

REACTIONS:
Protective Transformation: When ally within 10 ft. is attacked by creature that would kill them, Marcus can transform into hybrid form as reaction and intercept the attack (becomes new target).

Silver Sensitivity: If hit by silvered weapon, must succeed DC 15 Wisdom save or revert to human form immediately.
```

### Equipment (Human Form)
- **Armor:** Half-Plate +1 (custom-fitted, reinforced)
- **Primary Weapon:** Longsword +1 "Frontier's Edge" (silvered, ironically)
- **Secondary:** Silvered Dagger (keeps it as test of control)
- **Ranged:** Longbow with 40 arrows (20 normal, 20 silvered)
- **Shield:** Heater Shield (+2 AC when used)
- **Cloak:** Frontier Captain's Cloak (marks authority, grants +1 to Charisma checks with frontier folk)
- **Amulet:** Moonstone Pendant (helps resist transformations, grants +2 to Wisdom saves vs. lycanthropy)
- **Belt:** Utility belt with rope, signal horn, rations, waterskin
- **Potions:** 3 potions of healing, 1 potion of heroism
- **Special:** Silver chain (last resort restraint if he loses control)
- **Documents:** Captain's commission, frontier maps, wanted posters

### Physical Description (Human Form)
Rugged and battle-hardened (6'1", 200 lbs) with the weathered look of frontier life. Dark brown hair kept military short. Intense gray eyes that sometimes flash amber in moonlight. Strong jawline with short beard showing early gray. Multiple scars across face and arms from frontier combat. Moves with controlled power, like a caged wolf. Wears half-plate that's seen heavy use but is meticulously maintained. Smells of leather, steel, and wild places. Carries himself with authority but growing weariness.

**(Hybrid Form):** Gains wolf-like features—elongated snout, fangs, claws, fur covering body, digitigrade legs, tail. Height increases to 7 feet. Eyes glow amber. Still recognizable but terrifying. Retains ability to speak (with difficulty).

**(Wolf Form):** Large black wolf with gray eyes. Indistinguishable from dire wolf except for amber eye-flash in moonlight.

### Personality Traits
- Constantly aware of moon phases
- Checks silver weapons compulsively
- Keeps distance from people he cares about
- Patrols alone whenever possible
- Drinks wolfsbane tea nightly (bitter, helps control)
- Watches his hands for signs of transformation
- Protective of others to extreme degree

**Ideals:**
- **Protection:** "These people need a guardian, even if that guardian is cursed."
- **Control:** "I will master this curse or die trying. I will not endanger innocents."
- **Duty:** "I swore an oath to protect this frontier. The curse doesn't change that."
- **Redemption:** "Maybe by protecting others, I can atone for what I've become."

**Bonds:**
- His frontier militia (30 volunteers he commands)
- Westmarch settlement (200 people relying on his protection)
- Lady Seraphina Riverbrook (secret love, fears revealing curse)
- His late mentor Captain Aldric (infected him while dying)
- The memory of his first kill as a werewolf (still haunts him)
- His younger sister in Silverpine (hasn't seen her in 2 years)

**Flaws:**
- Increasingly isolated, pushes people away
- Guilty about curse transmission (has accidentally infected two people)
- Suicidal thoughts during full moons (considers silver to the heart)
- Drinks heavily to cope with curse
- Refuses magical help (fears making it worse)
- Doesn't sleep well (nightmares of transformation kills)
- Secret meetings with The Silver Wolf (who understands)

### Roleplaying Notes
- Touches moonstone amulet when stressed
- Checks moon phase calendar constantly
- Refuses to eat rare meat (reminds him of curse)
- Volunteers for dangerous missions (death wish)
- Growls unconsciously when angry
- Sniffs air when suspicious (hybrid sense memory)
- Keeps silver dagger visible (warning to himself)

**Key Details:**
- Commands Westmarch frontier garrison (30 militia)
- Infected with lycanthropy 3 years ago
- Has partial control during most full moons
- Secretly meets Silver Wolf for advice/support
- In love with Lady Seraphina Riverbrook (terrified to tell her)
- Has infected 2 people accidentally (deep guilt)
- Considers suicide regularly but duty prevents it
- Knows Elder Thalindra suspects his curse

### Secrets
1. **The Infection Origin:** His dying mentor Captain Aldric was a werewolf and bit him while delirious
2. **Two Accidents:** Has accidentally infected two people during transformations; both became werewolves
3. **The Silver Wolf Connection:** Secretly meets with Aldren Moonrunner, a full werewolf who taught him control
4. **Seraphina's Love:** Loves Lady Seraphina but can't tell her; she loves him too; both are oblivious
5. **Suicide Plans:** Has detailed plans to end himself if he ever kills an innocent
6. **The Blood Moon:** During blood moons he has zero control; chains himself in secret basement
7. **Hunting the Infected:** Tracking the two he accidentally infected; hasn't found them yet
8. **Druid Contact:** Elder Thalindra knows and is researching cure; he doesn't know she's helping
9. **The Unbound:** Lord Shadows knows about his curse and plans to use it against him
10. **Pack Dreams:** Sometimes dreams of running with a wolf pack; fears he's losing humanity

### Plot Hooks
1. **Frontier Attack:** Monster assault on Westmarch during full moon; must defend while managing curse
2. **The Infected:** One of his accidentally infected victims is in nearby town; party must help capture
3. **Blood Moon Rising:** Rare blood moon approaching; he'll lose complete control; needs secure location
4. **Romance Complication:** Seraphina discovers his curse at worst possible moment
5. **Werewolf Hunter:** Silver-armed hunter arrives hunting "the Westmarch beast"; party must intervene
6. **The Cure Quest:** Elder Thalindra found cure ingredients; party must retrieve from dangerous locations
7. **Unbound Blackmail:** Lord Shadows threatens to expose curse unless Marcus betrays friends
8. **Transformation Accident:** Transforms during diplomatic meeting; must prove he's not murderous beast
9. **Pack Calling:** Wild werewolf pack wants him to join; Silver Wolf urges him to resist
10. **Final Choice:** Can take cure but it requires sacrificing someone else to the curse

### Connections
- **Lady Seraphina Riverbrook:** Secret love interest (mutual but unspoken); terrified to reveal curse
- **The Silver Wolf / Aldren Moonrunner:** Mentor in curse control; secret ally
- **Elder Thalindra Oakheart:** She knows his curse; researching cure without his knowledge
- **Hermit Sage Morganna:** Consults about lycanthropy lore
- **Druid Thornwood:** Provides wolfsbane and control herbs
- **Lord Shadows Blackwood:** Knows about curse; plans to exploit it
- **Captain Aldric (deceased):** His infected mentor whose dying wish was Marcus's survival
- **Master Hunter Kael Dragonsbane:** Suspicious of Marcus; may investigate

## The Silver Wolf
/ ALDREN MOONRUNNER
**"The curse is not evil. The man makes that choice, not the beast."**

**Status:** ALIVE - Mysterious Protector, Controlled Werewolf  
**CR:** 10 (Master werewolf with complete control)  
**Race:** Human (fully embraced lycanthropy)  
**Age:** Unknown (appears 40s, likely much older)  

### Stat Block
```


### Background & History
Before the curse, she was Captain Helena Silverbane, the most decorated officer in the frontier guard. She was Marcus's mentor, the one who trained him, the one who led the patrol into the werewolf ambush. She was the first bitten, and the first to turn.

Unlike Marcus, she didn't fight the beast—she embraced it. The Wolf offered freedom from human frailty, from pain, from the slow decline of aging. She disappeared into the wilderness and built a pack of werewolves who live as she does: hunting, running, wild and free.

She's not evil in any simple sense. Her pack doesn't attack innocents unprovoked. But they are predators, and they claim hunting territories that sometimes conflict with human settlements. She believes lycanthropy is a gift and seeks to share it—willing or not—with those she deems worthy.

### Connections
- **Pack:** Twelve werewolves loyal to her
- **Former Protégé:** Captain Marcus Frontiersman (love and hate intertwined)
- **Enemy:** Werewolf hunters across the region
- **Ally:** Some fey creatures who appreciate her wildness
- **Target:** Soldiers and warriors she deems "worthy" of the gift

### Secrets
1. **The Original Guilt:** She led the patrol into the ambush deliberately. Had already made a deal with the pack.
2. **The Marcus Obsession:** Wants Marcus to join her willingly. Has been slowly manipulating circumstances.
3. **The Fey Alliance:** Made deals with unseelie fey for territorial protection.
4. **The Pack Instability:** Some pack members are growing too wild. She's losing control.
5. **The Cure Fear:** Knows a cure exists. Terrified that if Marcus finds it, she'll want it too.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Pack Contact:** Reaches out to the party as neutral intermediaries.
2. **The Territory Dispute:** Her pack is encroaching on human lands. Negotiate or fight.
3. **The Cure Information:** Has information about a cure. Might trade it—for the right price.
4. **The Marcus Trap:** Has set a trap for Marcus. The party might be able to intervene.
5. **The Pack Rebellion:** Some werewolves have gone feral. She needs help stopping them before hunters blame her pack.

Medium Humanoid (Human, Shapechanger), Chaotic Neutral

Armor Class: 18 (natural armor in hybrid form)
Hit Points: 142 (17d10 + 51)
Speed: 40 ft. (50 ft. in hybrid or wolf form)

STR: 20 (+5)  DEX: 16 (+3)  CON: 18 (+4)
INT: 14 (+2)  WIS: 16 (+3)  CHA: 12 (+1)

Saving Throws: Str +9, Dex +7, Con +8, Wis +7
Skills: Acrobatics +7, Athletics +9, Intimidation +5, Perception +11 (expertise), Stealth +11 (expertise), Survival +11 (expertise)
Damage Immunities: Bludgeoning, Piercing, and Slashing from nonmagical attacks not made with silvered weapons
Senses: Darkvision 120 ft., Blindsight 30 ft. (hearing/smell based), Passive Perception 21
Languages: Common, Sylvan, understands Druidic
Challenge Rating: 10 (5,900 XP)

SPECIAL ABILITIES:
Shapechanger (Master): Can transform between human, hybrid, and wolf forms as a bonus action. Can maintain hybrid form indefinitely. Has complete control during all moon phases.

Perfect Control: Immune to forced transformations. Never loses control to beast instincts. Can voluntarily fail saves to resist transformation if desired.

Keen Senses (All Forms): Advantage on Perception checks using hearing or smell. Can track by scent alone, identifying individual scents up to 24 hours old.

Pack Lord: Other lycanthropes view him with respect/fear. Has advantage on Charisma checks with lycanthropes. Can sense other lycanthropes within 100 ft.

Regeneration: Regains 10 HP at start of his turn if he has at least 1 HP. Doesn't regenerate damage from silvered weapons.

Legendary Resistance (2/Day): If fails saving throw, can choose to succeed instead.

Moon-Blessed: During full moons, gains +2 to all ability scores and his regeneration increases to 15 HP per turn.

Pack Tactics: Advantage on attack rolls against creatures if at least one ally is within 5 ft.

Ambush Predator: Has advantage on attack rolls against creatures that haven't taken a turn in combat yet.

Trackless: Leaves no trail in wilderness. Can't be tracked by normal means.

ACTIONS (Human Form - Rare):
Multiattack: Makes three unarmed strikes or weapon attacks.

Unarmed Strike: Melee Weapon Attack: +9 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d6+5 bludgeoning damage.

ACTIONS (Hybrid Form - Preferred):
Multiattack: Makes one bite attack and three claw attacks.

Bite: Melee Weapon Attack: +9 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 2d8+5 piercing damage. Target must succeed DC 16 Constitution save or be cursed with werewolf lycanthropy (but only if Aldren wishes it).

Claw: Melee Weapon Attack: +9 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 2d6+5 slashing damage.

Rending Claws: If both claw attacks hit same target, deal extra 3d6 slashing damage.

Alpha's Howl (Recharge 5-6): Releases a primal howl. Effects depend on target:
- Allied lycanthropes: Gain 20 temp HP, advantage on attacks for 1 minute
- Enemies: DC 16 Wisdom save or frightened for 1 minute
- Range: 300 ft.

Pounce: If moves at least 20 ft. toward target and hits with claw, target must succeed DC 17 Strength save or be knocked prone. Can make bite attack as bonus action against prone targets.

Savage Maul (Recharge 6): Focuses all attacks on single target. Makes four claw attacks. If two or more hit, also makes bite attack. If bite hits, deals double damage.

ACTIONS (Wolf Form - Large):
Bite: Melee Weapon Attack: +9 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 3d8+5 piercing damage. Target must succeed DC 16 Constitution save or be cursed with werewolf lycanthropy (only if Aldren wishes).

Pounce: If moves 30 ft. toward target and hits with bite, target must succeed DC 17 Strength save or be knocked prone. Can make another bite as bonus action.

Pack Leader's Call (1/Day): Summons 2d4 wolves (CR 1/4 each) that arrive in 1d4 rounds and obey his commands for 1 hour.

REACTIONS:
Uncanny Dodge: When attacker he can see hits him with attack, can halve the damage.

Savage Riposte: When creature misses him with melee attack, can immediately make claw attack against them.

Protective Pounce: When ally within 30 ft. is attacked, can move up to half speed and impose disadvantage on attack roll.

LEGENDARY ACTIONS (3 per round):
- Move: Moves up to half speed without provoking opportunity attacks.
- Claw Attack: Makes one claw attack.
- Detect (Costs 1): Makes Perception check or senses all lycanthropes within 100 ft.
- Howl (Costs 2): Uses Alpha's Howl if available.
- Transform (Costs 1): Changes between forms.
```

### Equipment (Rarely Carries)
- **Clothing:** Simple traveler's clothes (human form), shreds when transforming
- **Amulet:** Silver moon pendant (proof he's mastered the curse, doesn't harm him)
- **Cloak:** Weather-worn gray cloak (wolf form can wear it like a cape)
- **Pouch:** Small leather pouch with herbs, wolfsbane antidote, emergency rations
- **No Weapons:** Relies entirely on natural weapons
- **No Armor:** Natural armor in hybrid form superior to any worn armor

### Physical Description

**(Human Form - Rarely Seen):**
Rugged and weathered (6'0", 190 lbs) with the look of someone who lives in wilderness. Prematurely gray hair worn long and wild. Piercing gray eyes that sometimes flash silver. Multiple scars across exposed skin. Strong build from years of hunting. Wears simple travel-worn clothes. Moves with predator's grace even in human form.

**(Hybrid Form - His Preferred State):**
Towering werewolf (7'5", 320 lbs) with silver-gray fur that seems to shimmer in moonlight. Powerful build with visible muscle definition. Elongated wolf snout with intelligent gray eyes. Large pointed ears constantly swiveling. Massive claws (6 inches long) and fangs. Digitigrade legs with powerful haunches. Long bushy tail. Wears the gray cloak like a badge. Despite terrifying appearance, moves with controlled grace.

**(Wolf Form - For Travel):**
Large silver-gray wolf (size of a small horse). Appears as a dire wolf but with distinctive silver sheen to fur. Gray eyes remain intelligent and aware. Faster than normal wolves. Often mistaken for spirit or fey wolf.

### Personality Traits
- Speaks little, observes much
- Comfortable in prolonged silences
- Refers to himself as "we" (human and beast are one)
- Watches moon phases but isn't controlled by them
- Protective of innocent lycanthropes struggling with curse
- Hunts those who abuse lycanthropy
- Smells everyone upon meeting (habit)

**Ideals:**
- **Balance:** "Man and beast can coexist in one soul. The struggle creates strength."
- **Choice:** "The curse doesn't make monsters. People choose to be monsters."
- **Protection:** "Those who cannot control the beast need guidance, not execution."
- **Nature:** "The wild is not evil. Civilization fears what it doesn't understand."

**Bonds:**
- Lycanthropes struggling with control (mentors them)
- The forest and wild places (his true home)
- Captain Marcus Frontiersman (teaching him control)
- The memory of his pack (all dead now)
- An oath made long ago (won't speak of it)
- The balance between civilization and wilderness

**Flaws:**
- Increasingly isolated from humanity
- Sometimes forgets human social norms
- Violent toward anyone who abuses lycanthropy
- Guilty about past (killed people before gaining control)
- Fears complete loss of humanity despite control
- Refuses to fully commit to either beast or man
- Hunted by silver-armed hunters (constant vigilance)

### Roleplaying Notes
- Sniffs air constantly
- Tilts head like a wolf when confused
- Growls low when threatened
- Uses minimal words, maximum meaning
- Makes eye contact that feels predatory
- Comfortable on all fours in hybrid form
- Howls at the moon (celebration, not compulsion)

**Speech Patterns:**
- "We smell fear on you. Unnecessary."
- "The moon calls. We answer freely."
- "Control comes from acceptance, not resistance."
- "Your beast and you are not enemies. Learn this."

### Key Details
- **Master of Lycanthropy:** Has complete control, even during blood moons
- **Unknown Age:** Appears 40s but may be ancient (lycanthropy slows aging)
- **Mysterious Past:** Refuses to discuss how he gained control
- **Mentor Role:** Teaches other lycanthropes control
- **The Silver Wolf:** Local legend; people don't realize he's real
- **Territory:** Claims western forest as territory (doesn't allow evil lycanthropes)
- **The Test:** Carries silver amulet—proof he's mastered the curse
- **Pack Memory:** Last survivor of his original pack (all died fighting something)

### Secrets
1. **Ancient Origin:** Is actually 200+ years old; lycanthropy stopped aging
2. **The Oath:** Swore oath to moon goddess to never sire new lycanthropes without consent
3. **Pack Massacre:** His entire pack was wiped out by Unbound 50 years ago; he survived
4. **Druid Connection:** Is actually a former druid who chose lycanthropy to gain power
5. **Lord Shadows:** Knows Lord Shadows personally from decades ago; has history
6. **The Cure:** Knows how to cure lycanthropy but won't share (believes curse is gift)
7. **Moonstone Source:** Mines moonstones from secret cave; gives them to struggling lycanthropes
8. **Marcus's Future:** Sees great potential in Marcus but fears he lacks will to continue
9. **Hunter's Target:** Multiple silver-armed hunters seek his head (worth 5,000 gold)
10. **The Prophecy:** Believes lycanthropes will play role in coming "Second Worldrend"

### Plot Hooks
1. **Lycanthrope Mentorship:** Marcus needs advanced training; sends party to fetch Aldren
2. **The Rogue Werewolf:** Evil werewolf terrorizing region; Aldren asks party's help hunting it
3. **Hunter Assault:** Silver-armed hunters found his den; needs protection during healing
4. **The Moon Temple:** Ancient temple to moon goddess discovered; Aldren needs escort to investigate
5. **Pack Reformation:** Gathering good-aligned lycanthropes to form new pack; needs party's help recruiting
6. **Unbound Revenge:** Learns Unbound killed his pack; wants revenge; needs party to infiltrate
7. **The Cure Theft:** Someone stole his notes on lycanthropy control; must recover before misused
8. **Moonstone Mine:** His secret moonstone mine under attack by kobolds; party must help defend
9. **Blood Moon Ritual:** Rare blood moon allows ritual to grant perfect control; needs components
10. **The Alpha Challenge:** Ancient alpha werewolf challenges him for territory; ritual combat requires witnesses

### Connections
- **Captain Marcus Frontiersman:** Student/mentee; teaching him curse control
- **Elder Thalindra Oakheart:** Aware of each other; mutual respect; she protects his territory
- **Druid Thornwood:** Former druid colleague from decades ago
- **Hermit Sage Morganna:** Trades information about lycanthropy lore
- **Lord Shadows Blackwood:** Ancient enemy; knows secrets from Aldren's past
- **The Unbound:** Killed his pack 50 years ago; sworn enemy
- **Master Hunter Kael Dragonsbane:** Uneasy truce; respects Aldren's control
- **Seraphina Riverbrook:** Occasionally protects her lands; she doesn't know why
- **The Frost Seer:** She has visions of him in future conflict

## Forester Galen Sustainharvest
**"Cut three, plant ten. That's how the forest survives, and so do we."**

**Status:** ALIVE - Sustainable Forestry Expert, Druid Liaison  
**CR:** 6 (Ranger with druidic knowledge)  
**Race:** Half-Elf (human and wood elf heritage)  
**Age:** 67 (appears 50s)  

### Stat Block
```


### Background & History
Galen's family has managed this section of forest for twelve generations, carefully harvesting timber while maintaining the woodland's health. He learned the craft from his father, who learned from his father, an unbroken chain of knowledge stretching back centuries.

He's developed sustainable harvesting to a science: which trees to cut, which to preserve, how to encourage regrowth, when to let areas lie fallow. His forest produces steady timber while remaining healthy. Other foresters study his methods; lumber companies resent his restrictions.

Recently, he's noticed troubling changes. Trees are growing strangely, animals behaving oddly, and the forest's... feeling has shifted. Something is wrong at a level he can't quite identify, and it frightens him.

### Connections
- **Territory:** Three thousand acres of managed forest
- **Ally:** Miller Tobias Waterwheel (shares concerns)
- **Enemy:** Quickcut Lumber Company (wants his land)
- **Contact:** Druid Thornwood (magical advisor)
- **Family:** Wife and three children, all learning forestry

### Secrets
1. **The Blight Signs:** Has seen early signs of magical blight. Not sure what to do about it.
2. **The Buried Thing:** Found something buried in a clearing. Ancient, magical, and getting warmer.
3. **The Lumber Company:** They've tried bribing, threatening, and sabotaging him. He has evidence.
4. **The Family Gift:** His family has minor forest magic. Nothing dramatic, just an affinity.
5. **The Evacuation Plan:** If things get bad enough, he knows how to get his family out fast.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Blight Investigation:** Needs magical help understanding what's happening to the forest.
2. **The Buried Discovery:** The thing in the clearing is definitely waking up. Needs excavation.
3. **The Lumber Fight:** Ready to move against Quickcut. Needs allies and legal help.
4. **The Forest Defense:** Something is coming. Needs help preparing.
5. **The Knowledge Share:** Willing to teach sustainable forestry to those who'll use it.

---
Medium Humanoid (Half-Elf), Neutral Good

Armor Class: 16 (studded leather + Dex)
Hit Points: 78 (12d8 + 24)
Speed: 30 ft., climb 30 ft.

STR: 14 (+2)  DEX: 16 (+3)  CON: 14 (+2)
INT: 14 (+2)  WIS: 18 (+4)  CHA: 13 (+1)

Saving Throws: Str +5, Dex +6, Wis +7
Skills: Animal Handling +7, Athletics +5, Nature +8 (expertise), Perception +10 (expertise), Stealth +6, Survival +10 (expertise), Woodcarver's Tools +5
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft., Passive Perception 20
Languages: Common, Elvish, Sylvan, Druidic (honorary), can speak with animals and plants
Challenge Rating: 6 (2,300 XP)

RACIAL ABILITIES:
Fey Ancestry: Advantage against being charmed, immune to magic sleep.
Trance: Meditates 4 hours instead of sleeping.

SPECIAL ABILITIES:
Favored Enemy (Aberrations, Undead): +2 damage against these creature types. Advantage on tracking them and Intelligence checks to recall information about them.

Natural Explorer (Forest): In forest terrain:
- Difficult terrain doesn't slow party's travel
- Can't become lost except by magical means
- Remains alert to danger even during other activities
- Can move stealthily at normal pace alone
- Finds twice as much food when foraging
- Learns exact number, sizes, and how long ago creatures passed

Spellcasting: 8th-level ranger. Spell save DC 15, +7 to hit with spell attacks.

Spells Prepared:
1st level (4 slots): Cure Wounds, Entangle, Goodberry, Speak with Animals
2nd level (3 slots): Pass without Trace, Spike Growth, Locate Plants or Animals

Sustainable Forestry Expert: Can assess forest health, tree ages, and sustainable harvest rates with perfect accuracy. Knows exactly which trees can be safely harvested without damaging ecosystem.

Tree Speaker: Can communicate with trees (as *speak with plants* spell) without expending spell slot. Trees willingly share information about recent events with him.

Forest Network: Maintains relationships with druids, rangers, and forest spirits across 100-mile radius. Can send messages through the trees (takes 24 hours).

Animal Companion - Moss the Bear: Always accompanied by an old brown bear (CR 1) that trusts him completely.

ACTIONS:
Multiattack: Makes two attacks with Longbow or Handaxe, or three with Hunting Knife (melee).

Forestkeeper's Longbow +1: Ranged Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, range 150/600 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d8+4 piercing damage plus 1d6 poison damage (arrows tipped with natural toxins).
Special: Can choose nonlethal damage. Poisoned creatures have disadvantage on Perception checks (toxin affects senses).

Hunting Knife: Melee Weapon Attack: +6 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d6+3 piercing damage.

Handaxe +1: Melee or Ranged Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, reach 5 ft. or range 20/60 ft.
Hit: 1d6+4 slashing damage.

Entangling Roots (Recharge 5-6, replaces spell slot): Causes roots to erupt from ground in 20-foot radius centered on point within 60 ft. Creatures in area must succeed DC 15 Strength save or be restrained. Lasts 1 minute or until destroyed (AC 10, 20 HP per 10-foot square).

Call Animal Ally (1/Day): Summons 1d4 forest animals (wolves, bears, boars, or elk) that arrive in 1d4 rounds and obey commands for 1 hour.

Mark the Violator (1/Day): Marks creature that has harmed the forest unnecessarily. Marked creature:
- Has disadvantage on Stealth checks in forests
- Animals are hostile toward them
- Druids and rangers can sense the mark
- Lasts until they atone for the damage

REACTIONS:
Forest's Warning: When ally within 30 ft. is about to trigger natural hazard (falling branch, hidden pit, dangerous plant), can shout warning granting +5 to their saving throw or check to avoid.

Defensive Retreat: When hit by attack, can immediately move up to half speed without provoking opportunity attacks (bonus action next turn)

.

BONUS ACTIONS:
Quick Assessment: Examines forest area within 60 ft. and learns:
- Number of trees and their health
- Any unnatural disturbances
- Presence of hidden creatures (DC 15 Perception)
- Best path through difficult terrain
```

### Equipment
- **Armor:** Reinforced Studded Leather +1 (forest camouflage pattern)
- **Primary Weapon:** Forestkeeper's Longbow +1 (carved with growth runes)
- **Arrows:** Quiver with 40 arrows (20 normal, 10 poisoned, 10 nonlethal blunt)
- **Secondary:** Handaxe +1 (doubles as tool and weapon)
- **Tool:** Hunting Knife (razor sharp, used for careful bark removal)
- **Tools:** Woodcarver's tools, forester's marking axe, measuring rope
- **Cloak:** Forest Green Cloak (grants advantage on Stealth in forest)
- **Boots:** Soft Leather Boots (no sound when walking, tracks minimal)
- **Pack:** Rope, climbing gear, tree-marking paint, seedling pouches
- **Book:** Comprehensive forestry journal (40 years of observations)
- **Companion:** Moss the Bear (old brown bear, best friend)
- **Seeds:** Pouches of various tree seeds (oak, pine, maple, etc.)

### Physical Description
Lean and weathered (5'11", 165 lbs) with the wiry build of someone who climbs and hikes constantly. Silver-streaked brown hair worn in practical ponytail. Kind hazel eyes that shift green in certain lights (elf heritage). Tanned, lined face marked by years of outdoor work. Moves with quiet grace through forests. Wears earth-tone clothes that blend perfectly with forest. Perpetually has leaves, moss, and bark pieces on his person. Smells of pine, earth, and leather. His hands are calloused but gentle. Usually accompanied by Moss, a large old brown bear.

### Personality Traits
- Speaks softly, rarely raises voice
- Often pauses to touch or examine trees
- Quotes forest wisdom and old sayings
- Patient to extreme degree
- Treats trees like old friends
- Gentle but firm about forest protection
- Makes decisions slowly but confidently

**Ideals:**
- **Balance:** "Take what you need, not what you want. Plant more than you harvest."
- **Wisdom:** "The forest teaches if you're patient enough to listen."
- **Stewardship:** "We don't own the forest. We serve it, and it serves us."
- **Future:** "I plant trees knowing I won't see them grown. That's the responsibility."

**Bonds:**
- The forest (considers it alive and conscious)
- His bear companion Moss (20 years together)
- Apprentice foresters he's training (12 current students)
- The druid circle (honorary member despite not being druid)
- His children and grandchildren (family of foresters)
- The memory of ancient trees he's lost

**Flaws:**
- Sometimes prioritizes trees over people
- Holds decades-long grudges against those who harmed forests
- Difficulty adapting to rapid change
- Guilty about trees felled under his authority
- Can't walk past sick tree without stopping to help
- Increasingly tired (age catching up)

### Roleplaying Notes
- Runs hand along tree bark while talking
- Moss the bear is always nearby
- Knows every tree in hundred-mile radius by sight
- Offers fresh fruit from "forest gifts"
- Refers to trees by personality ("Old Grandfather Oak")
- Stops conversations to listen to forest sounds
- Makes gifts from carved wood

**Key Details:**
- 40+ years experience in sustainable forestry
- Honorary druid circle member (respects their teachings)
- Mediates between loggers and druids
- Trained 50+ foresters across his career
- Maintains seedling nursery (thousands of saplings)
- Maps every tree in managed territory
- Personal friend of Druid Thornwood
- Moss the bear saved his life 20 years ago

### Secrets
1. **Hidden Grove:** Knows location of sacred grove with pre-Worldrend trees (Druids don't know)
2. **The Ancient Contract:** Maintains verbal contract with dryad queen; she protects his family in exchange for forest protection
3. **Illegal Operations:** Knows which merchants are illegally logging; collects evidence
4. **The Seedbank:** Hidden cache of extinct tree species seeds (from before Worldrend)
5. **Forest Spirits:** Can see and speak with minor forest spirits (gift from dryad queen)
6. **Moss's Secret:** His bear companion is actually a polymorphed druid watching over him
7. **Tree Sickness:** Several ancient trees dying from unknown magical disease; he's researching
8. **His Testament:** His will leaves his entire life's earnings to forest conservation
9. **The Warning:** Forest spirits warning him something is coming from the east
10. **Unbound Activities:** Has detected systematic logging patterns that match Unbound ritual circles

### Plot Hooks
1. **Illegal Logging:** Massive illegal deforestation operation discovered; needs party to stop it
2. **The Tree Sickness:** Ancient trees dying mysteriously; must find cause and cure
3. **Dryad Diplomacy:** Dryad queen demands audience with party; he must mediate
4. **Seedbank Theft:** His cache of extinct seeds stolen; must recover before they're destroyed
5. **Forest Fire:** Arson suspected; must find culprit before fire season starts
6. **The Ancient Grove:** Party needs rare plants from sacred grove; must earn permission
7. **Merchant Conflict:** Logging company vs. druids escalating; needs neutral arbitration
8. **Bear Trouble:** Moss the bear's true identity revealed during crisis
9. **Spirit Warning:** Forest spirits show him visions of disaster; party must investigate
10. **Final Survey:** His last great work—complete survey of the forest; needs protection from dangers

### Connections
- **Druid Thornwood:** Close colleague and friend; work together on forest health
- **Elder Thalindra Oakheart:** Consulted on Heart Oak illness; deeply concerned
- **Master Carpenter Aldric Woodwise:** Business partner in sustainable logging
- **Forester Galen Sustainharvest:** The mentor of next generation
- **Hermit Sage Morganna:** Occasionally trades forest lore
- **The Silver Wolf:** Aware of his presence; unofficial alliance protecting forest
- **Lord Shadows Blackwood:** Unknown enemy (Unbound clearing forests for rituals)
- **Dryad Queen Silvaris:** Secret ally through ancient contract

## Druid Thornwood
/ THERON OAKENSHADE
**"The forest remembers all debts—those paid and those owed."**

**Status:** ALIVE - Forest Guardian Druid  
**CR:** 11 (Powerful druid with earth/forest specialization)  
**Race:** Firbolg (forest giant-kin)  
**Age:** 127 years old  

### Stat Block
```


### Background & History
Thornwood isn't a name—it's what the forest itself calls him. He was born human, with a human name he's forgotten, in a village that no longer exists. When loggers came to clearcut his home forest, he called on power he didn't know he had. The forest responded. The loggers didn't survive.

That was sixty years ago. Since then, he's become more forest than man. Bark grows on his skin, leaves sprout from his hair, and he can be in any part of the forest simultaneously by traveling through the root network. He protects the woodland from all threats—natural and unnatural.

He's not hostile to civilization, but he's not friendly either. Loggers who harvest sustainably can pass safely; those who clear-cut wake the trees' wrath. Hunters who take only what they need are welcome; poachers are never found. He maintains balance, nothing more.

### Connections
- **Domain:** The entire old-growth forest (100 square miles)
- **Ally:** Forester Galen Sustainharvest (respects sustainable practices)
- **Circle:** Connection to other nature spirits
- **Enemy:** Quickcut Lumber Company (eternal vendetta)
- **Memory:** His human life (fading)

### Secrets
1. **The Fading Humanity:** Will be entirely tree within twenty years. Unsure how to feel about it.
2. **The Logger Massacre:** What happened sixty years ago was worse than rumors suggest. Thirty-seven died.
3. **The Forest Heart:** Protects a grove that contains the forest's spiritual center. Would die for it.
4. **The Blight Knowledge:** Knows what's causing the blight but not how to stop it.
5. **The Successor Need:** Needs to pass his role to someone before he loses the ability. Looking for candidates.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Blight Cure:** Has partial information about stopping the blight. Needs help with the rest.
2. **The Forest Heart Defense:** Something is moving toward the grove. Needs powerful allies.
3. **The Successor Test:** Tests party members as potential successors to his role.
4. **The Quickcut War:** The lumber company is escalating. Needs help ending them permanently.
5. **The Humanity Question:** Reaches out about possibly regaining his human form. Conflicted about it.

---
Medium Humanoid (Firbolg), Neutral

Armor Class: 16 (barkskin)
Hit Points: 127 (15d8 + 60)
Speed: 30 ft.

STR: 16 (+3)  DEX: 14 (+2)  CON: 18 (+4)
INT: 14 (+2)  WIS: 20 (+5)  CHA: 14 (+2)

Saving Throws: Int +6, Wis +9, Cha +6
Skills: Animal Handling +9, Arcana +6, Insight +9, Medicine +9, Nature +10 (expertise), Perception +9, Survival +9
Damage Resistances: Poison
Condition Immunities: Charmed, Frightened (while in forest)
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft., Passive Perception 19, Tremorsense 30 ft. (through roots)
Languages: Common, Elvish, Sylvan, Druidic, Giant, Primordial, can speak with beasts and plants
Challenge Rating: 11 (7,200 XP)

RACIAL ABILITIES (Firbolg):
Firbolg Magic: Can cast *detect magic* and *disguise self* (appear 3 feet shorter) once each per short rest.

Hidden Step: Can magically turn invisible until start of next turn or until attacks, casts spell, or forces saving throw. Once per short rest.

Powerful Build: Counts as Large for carrying capacity and push/drag/lift.

Speech of Beast and Leaf: Can communicate simple ideas with beasts and plants.

SPECIAL ABILITIES:
Spellcasting: 12th-level druid (Circle of the Land - Forest). Spell save DC 17, +9 to hit with spell attacks.

Spells Prepared:
Cantrips (at will): Druidcraft, Guidance, Produce Flame, Thorn Whip, Shillelagh
1st level (4 slots): Cure Wounds, Entangle, Goodberry, Speak with Animals
2nd level (3 slots): Barkskin*, Hold Person, Pass without Trace, Spike Growth
3rd level (3 slots): Call Lightning, Conjure Animals, Plant Growth, Speak with Plants
4th level (3 slots): Blight, Dominate Beast, Grasping Vine, Stone Shape
5th level (2 slots): Commune with Nature, Cone of Cold (forest feature), Tree Stride
6th level (1 slot): Transport via Plants, Wall of Thorns
*Usually active

Forest Sanctuary: When a beast or plant creature attempts to attack him, must succeed DC 17 Wisdom save. On failure, must choose different target or action wasted. On success, immune for 24 hours.

Wild Shape (2/Short Rest): Can wild shape into beasts up to CR 1 as action (swim speed at 8th level). Prefers brown bear, dire wolf, or giant eagle forms. Lasts 6 hours.

Land's Stride: Moving through difficult terrain costs no extra movement. Can pass through magical plants without being slowed or taking damage.

Nature's Ward: Immune to poison and disease. Can't be charmed or frightened by fey or plants.

Root Network: While in forest, can sense disturbances through root systems within 300 ft. radius. Knows if creatures are moving through his territory.

Thornwood Transformation (1/Day): For 10 minutes, becomes avatar of forest fury:
- AC increases to 18
- Gain temp HP equal to druid level (12)
- Melee attacks deal +2d8 piercing (thorns)
- Can cast entangle as bonus action
- Resistant to all damage except fire

ACTIONS:
Multiattack: Makes two attacks with Thornwood Staff or casts a cantrip and makes one staff attack.

Thornwood Staff (Shillelagh): Melee Weapon Attack: +9 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 2d8+5 magical bludgeoning damage plus 1d8 poison damage (thorns).
Special: Staff regrows thorns naturally. On critical hit, target is grappled by thorny vines (escape DC 17).

Thorn Whip: Ranged Spell Attack: +9 to hit, range 30 ft., one creature.
Hit: 3d6 piercing damage and pull target 10 ft. closer.

Flame Seed (Recharge 5-6): Hurls explosive acorn. Ranged Spell Attack: +9 to hit, range 60 ft.
Hit: 4d8 fire damage to target and 2d8 fire to all creatures within 5 ft. (Dex DC 17 half).

Command Forest (1/Day): In 60-foot radius, causes:
- All plants become difficult terrain for enemies
- Trees attempt to restrain enemies (DC 17 Str save or restrained)
- Party gains half cover from foliage
- Lasts 10 minutes

Summon Forest Guardian (1/Day): Summons awakened tree (CR 2) that fights for 1 hour.

REACTIONS:
Bramble Defense: When hit by melee attack, thorny brambles lash out at attacker. +9 to hit, 2d8 piercing damage.

Nature's Intervention: When ally within 30 ft. takes damage, can cause vines to absorb some impact, reducing damage by 2d10+5.

Root Trip: When creature within 10 ft. moves, can cause roots to trip them. DC 17 Dexterity save or knocked prone.

LEGENDARY ACTIONS (2 per round):
- Cantrip: Casts a cantrip.
- Move: Moves up to half speed without provoking opportunity attacks.
- Thorn Lash (Costs 2): Uses thorn whip.
- Healing Blessing (Costs 2): Touches creature and heals 3d8+5 HP.
```

### Equipment
- **Staff:** Thornwood Staff (legendary, carved from ancient oak, grows thorns, never breaks)
- **Armor:** Living Bark Armor (AC 16 with barkskin, regenerates daily)
- **Robes:** Druidic robes woven from living vines (deep green, always fresh)
- **Cloak:** Leaf Cloak (changes color with seasons, grants advantage on Stealth in forests)
- **Belt:** Rope of Entanglement (can animate as bonus action)
- **Pouch:** Component pouch with rare herbs, crystals, and seeds
- **Amulet:** Wooden Amulet (carved with druidic symbols, glows near unnatural magic)
- **Seeds:** Emergency goodberries (always has 10 fresh berries)
- **Book:** Personal journal of forest observations (50 years)
- **Tools:** Herbalism kit (expertly maintained)

### Physical Description
Towering and imposing (7'2", 280 lbs) with the gentle giant presence of firbolgs. Skin has gray-blue tone with texture resembling bark. Long hair and beard are dark brown with green moss growing naturally. Deep amber eyes that glow faintly in darkness. Face is weathered and lined with age, carved features like ancient wood. Wears robes of living vines that move slightly. The Thornwood Staff is gnarled oak that grows fresh thorns daily. Moves with slow, deliberate power. Smells of earth, moss, and ancient forests. Small plants occasionally sprout from his footprints.

### Personality Traits
- Speaks in slow, measured tones
- Often pauses mid-sentence to listen to forest
- Refers to trees and animals by name
- Patient but can be terrifyingly angry when forest is threatened
- Quotes ancient druidic wisdom
- Makes decisions based on long-term forest health
- Treats all living things with respect

**Ideals:**
- **Balance:** "Life and death, growth and decay—all part of the cycle."
- **Protection:** "The forest shelters us. We shelter the forest. This is the way."
- **Ancient Ways:** "The old ways preserved forests for millennia. Modern ways threaten them."
- **Debt:** "The forest remembers all debts—those paid and those owed."

**Bonds:**
- The entire forest (considers it a living entity)
- The druid circle (12 members under his guidance)
- Elder Thalindra Oakheart (ally in protecting nature)
- His sacred grove (contains 500-year-old trees)
- Ancient forest spirits (maintains communication with them)
- His apprentice druids (currently training 6 young druids)

**Flaws:**
- Sometimes prioritizes forest over sentient life
- Holds grudges for decades (forest memory is long)
- Struggles to forgive those who harm nature
- Can be terrifyingly violent toward forest destroyers
- Inflexible about druidic traditions
- Doesn't trust civilization or technology

### Roleplaying Notes
- Staff plants in ground during conversations (roots sprout)
- Small animals frequently around him
- Speaks to trees when alone (and they respond)
- Makes decisions agonizingly slowly
- Touches earth to sense disturbances
- Offers healing to injured animals reflexively
- Eyes glow green when angry

**Key Details:**
- Leader of western forest druid circle
- 127 years old, considered young for firbolgs
- Maintains sacred groves across 100-mile territory
- Can sense forest disturbances through root network
- Personal ally of Elder Thalindra
- Trained 30+ druids across his lifetime
- Has zero tolerance for illegal logging
- Forest spirits report to him

### Secrets
1. **The Corruption Source:** Has traced Heart Oak's illness to Unbound ritual site
2. **Ancient Pact:** Bound by oath to ancient treant (still alive, hidden)
3. **Forest Spirit Council:** Leads council of dryads, treants, and fey that meet quarterly
4. **The Blight:** Aware of spreading magical corruption from east; researching solution
5. **Violent Past:** During youth, killed 12 loggers in rage; still haunted by it
6. **True Name:** "Thornwood" is title; his true name is Theron Oakenshade (gives power if known)
7. **The Grove Heart:** His sacred grove contains portal to Feywild
8. **Dying Prophecy:** Forest spirits showed him vision of "great burning" coming
9. **Unbound Infiltration:** Suspects Unbound agent within druid circle
10. **Ultimate Defense:** If forest is threatened with destruction, will summon ancient treants (catastrophic power)

### Plot Hooks
1. **Heart Oak Crisis:** Traced illness to Unbound ritual 10 miles east; needs party to stop it
2. **Illegal Logging War:** Massive deforestation operation; druid circle preparing assault; needs mediation or alliance
3. **Blight Spread:** Magical corruption spreading; must find source and cure before forest dies
4. **Treant Awakening:** Ancient treant mentor calling him; something terrible happening
5. **Feywild Portal:** Grove's portal destabilizing; creatures emerging; must stabilize
6. **Apprentice Missing:** One of his druid students disappeared investigating corruption
7. **Spirit Council:** Forest spirits demand action against Unbound; will they go to war?
8. **The True Name:** Enemy discovered his true name; must retrieve stolen knowledge
9. **Sacred Grove Defense:** Unbound assault on his grove; final battle location
10. **Ultimate Choice:** Can save Heart Oak or his grove, not both; which does he choose?

### Connections
- **Elder Thalindra Oakheart:** Close ally; coordinate on Heart Oak crisis
- **Forester Galen Sustainharvest:** Business partner in sustainable forestry
- **Master Carpenter Aldric Woodwise:** Respect sustainable practices; tense but functional relationship
- **The Silver Wolf / Aldren Moonrunner:** Knew him as druid decades ago; complicated history
- **Captain Marcus Frontiersman:** Provides wolfsbane for curse control
- **Hermit Sage Morganna:** Fellow nature scholar; trade information
- **Lord Shadows Blackwood:** Unbound leader destroying forest; sworn enemy
- **Druid Elder Silvaris:** Elder firbolg druid; his mentor and friend
- **Dryad Queen:** Maintains ancient alliance with forest fey

## Bard Finnegan Storyteller
**"Every tale deserves to be told, every song to be sung. Even the sad ones. Especially the sad ones."**

**Status:** ALIVE - Master Bard, Chronicler, Living History  
**CR:** 7 (Master performer with enchantment magic)  
**Race:** Half-Elf (human and high elf heritage)  
**Age:** 247 years old (appears late 50s)  

### Stat Block
```


### Background & History
Finnegan has been collecting stories for forty years, traveling from village to village, tavern to tavern, gathering tales both true and legendary. He has one of the most comprehensive collections of folklore in Thaldros, and more importantly, he understands how to separate fact from fiction.

He was a soldier in his youth, then a failed merchant, before discovering his true calling: preserving oral tradition. He's not a great musician or performer—merely competent—but his knowledge of stories is encyclopedic. People invite him to perform because his tales are accurate and complete, even when the truth is uncomfortable.

Now sixty and slowing down, he's looking for a place to record his collection properly. He fears dying with his head full of stories that will be lost forever.

### Connections
- **Network:** Performers, storytellers, and archivists across the region
- **Patron:** Various nobles who fund his collection
- **Rival:** Other storytellers with less concern for accuracy
- **Friend:** Sage Elminster Runereader (scholarly collaboration)
- **Treasure:** Forty years of stories in his memory

### Secrets
1. **The True Histories:** Knows the real versions of many sanitized official histories. Dangerous knowledge.
2. **The Pattern Recognition:** Has noticed patterns in stories that suggest current events echo past catastrophes.
3. **The Hero's Secret:** Knows embarrassing truths about a famous hero's legend. Never told.
4. **The Dying Man's Confession:** Was told a deathbed confession that implicates a powerful family. Burden of proof.
5. **The Story Magic:** Some stories he tells have minor magical effects. Never examined why.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Recording Project:** Needs help establishing a proper archive before his memory fails.
2. **The Pattern Investigation:** Shares his pattern observations, hoping the party can investigate.
3. **The Dangerous Knowledge:** Has information about someone the party is investigating.
4. **The Confession Dilemma:** Wants advice on what to do with the deathbed confession.
5. **The Story Quest:** Heard of a legendary tale in a dangerous location. Needs escorts to collect it.

---
Medium Humanoid (Half-Elf), Neutral Good

Armor Class: 15 (studded leather + Dex)
Hit Points: 84 (13d8 + 26)
Speed: 30 ft.

STR: 10 (+0)  DEX: 16 (+3)  CON: 14 (+2)
INT: 16 (+3)  WIS: 14 (+2)  CHA: 20 (+5)

Saving Throws: Dex +6, Wis +5, Cha +8
Skills: Acrobatics +6, Deception +8, History +9 (expertise), Insight +5, Perception +8 (expertise), Performance +11 (expertise), Persuasion +11 (expertise), Musical Instruments +9 (expertise)
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft., Passive Perception 18
Languages: Common, Elvish, Dwarvish, Halfling, Sylvan, Draconic (sings in all)
Challenge Rating: 7 (2,900 XP)

RACIAL ABILITIES:
Fey Ancestry: Advantage against being charmed, immune to magic sleep.

SPECIAL ABILITIES:
Spellcasting: 13th-level bard (College of Lore). Spell save DC 16, +8 to hit with spell attacks.

Spells Known:
Cantrips (at will): Light, Mage Hand, Message, Vicious Mockery
1st level (4 slots): Charm Person, Comprehend Languages, Cure Wounds, Disguise Self, Heroism
2nd level (3 slots): Detect Thoughts, Hold Person, Invisibility, Suggestion
3rd level (3 slots): Dispel Magic, Hypnotic Pattern, Major Image, Sending
4th level (2 slots): Confusion, Dimension Door, Greater Invisibility
5th level (1 slot): Modify Memory, Raise Dead (rare)
6th level (1 slot): Mass Suggestion, True Seeing
7th level (1 slot): Teleport

Bardic Inspiration (d10, 5/Long Rest): As bonus action, grants ally inspiration die they can add to ability check, attack roll, or saving throw within next 10 minutes.

Jack of All Trades: Adds +2 to any ability check that doesn't already include proficiency bonus.

Song of Rest: During short rest, allies regain extra 1d10 HP when using Hit Dice.

Magical Secrets: Knows spells from other classes (included in spell list).

Cutting Words (5/Long Rest): When creature he can see within 60 ft. makes attack roll, ability check, or damage roll, can use reaction to subtract 1d10 from the roll.

Living Chronicle: Has personally witnessed and chronicled 200+ years of history. Can recall any historical event he witnessed perfectly. Has advantage on all History checks.

Master Performer: Has advantage on Performance and Persuasion checks. Can earn 10 gp per day performing in taverns minimum, 100+ gp for noble performances.

Legendary Storyteller: When telling stories, can enchant audience. Listeners must succeed DC 16 Wisdom save or be captivated, unable to take hostile actions while he performs.

Memory Keeper: Can perfectly recall any story, song, poem, or historical account he's heard. His mind is a living library.

Tongues Master: Can perform in any language he knows, translating on the fly.

ACTIONS:
Multiattack: Makes two attacks with Rapier or casts a cantrip and makes one rapier attack.

Storyteller's Rapier +1: Melee Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d8+4 piercing damage.
Special: This slender blade is covered in etched stories. On critical hit, target must succeed DC 16 Charisma save or be charmed for 1 minute.

Vicious Mockery: Target within 60 ft. that can hear him must succeed DC 16 Wisdom save or take 3d4 psychic damage and disadvantage on next attack roll.

Hand Crossbow: Ranged Weapon Attack: +6 to hit, range 30/120 ft.
Hit: 1d6+3 piercing damage.

Enthralling Performance (1/Day): Performs for at least 1 minute. At end, up to 10 creatures who watched must succeed DC 16 Wisdom save or be charmed for 1 hour. Charmed creatures regard him as friendly acquaintance.

Tale of Heroes (Recharge 5-6): Tells inspiring battle story. All allies within 30 ft. gain:
- +2 to attack rolls
- +2 to AC
- Temp HP equal to 2d10+5
- Lasts 1 minute

REACTIONS:
Countercharm: As reaction when ally within 30 ft. must make save against being frightened or charmed, can grant them advantage on save.

Cutting Words: See special abilities above.

Historical Insight: When ally within 30 ft. makes Intelligence check about history or lore, can use reaction to grant advantage.

BONUS ACTIONS:
Bardic Inspiration: Grants inspiration die to ally.

Quick Performance: Makes Performance check to maintain crowd's attention or calm situation.
```
