### Physical Description
Distinguished and charismatic (5'10", 160 lbs) with the ageless quality of half-elves. Silver-white hair worn long and theatrical. Sparkling blue eyes that dance with mischief and wisdom. Weathered face with laugh lines and a warm smile. Moves with performer's grace. Wears colorful traveling clothes that have seen a thousand performances. The legendary lute "Memoir" is always within reach. Hands show decades of instrument playing—callused but graceful. Smells of pipe smoke, old books, and campfire stories. Voice is rich, melodious, perfect for songs and tales.

### Personality Traits
- Speaks in dramatic, story-like fashion
- Makes callbacks to historical events he witnessed
- Breaks into song mid-conversation
- Collects stories like others collect coins
- Performs even mundane actions theatrically
- Remembers everyone's name and story
- Weeps openly at sad tales

**Ideals:**

- **Truth:** "Every story has truth in it, even the lies reveal character."
- **Connection:** "Through stories, we're all connected—past, present, future."

**Bonds:**
- His journals (200+ years of chronicles, irreplaceable)

- The responsibility to preserve history

**Flaws:**
- Can't resist telling a story (even when inappropriate)
- Nostalgic to the point of melancholy
- Drinks too much when remembering sad tales
- Survivor's guilt (everyone he loved is dead)
- Lonely despite crowds (immortal among mortals)
- Secretly fears being forgotten
- Sometimes confuses memories across centuries

### Roleplaying Notes
- Strums lute while thinking
- Starts every statement with "I remember when..."
- Weeps during emotional stories (unashamed)
- Makes everything dramatic (even grocery shopping)
- Calls people "dear friend" after one meeting
- Breaks into relevant songs constantly
- Quotes his own compositions

**Speech Patterns:**
- "Ah, but that reminds me of a story from the Year of Falling Stars..."
- "As I sang to Queen Elara in '98, 'The past is never dead, it lives in song'..."
- "*strums lute* Let me tell you a tale..."
- "I was there, you know. I remember it well. *distant look*"

### Key Details:**
- 247 years old, witnessed major historical events
- Performed for kings, queens, and emperors
- Chronicler of Age of Strife, Worldrend aftermath
- Living repository of oral history
- Has composed 500+ songs and ballads
- Trained 40+ bards across his lifetime
- Famous across both kingdoms
- "Memoir" lute is legendary artifact

### Secrets
1. **Worldrend Witness:** Was present at the Worldrend, saw what caused it (traumatic memory)
2. **Royal Scandal:** Knows which current nobles have illegitimate bloodlines (dangerous knowledge)
3. **Hidden Journals:** Has 20 secret journals with uncensored history (explosive if found)
4. **Lost Love:** His wife died 180 years ago; still mourns; writes songs to her
5. **True Age:** Actually 280+ years old, uses magic to appear younger; fears people knowing
6. **Memory Curse:** Sometimes can't distinguish which memories are his vs. stories he's heard
7. **Bardic College Secret:** Knows location of legendary Bardic College that vanished in Worldrend
8. **The Last Song:** Has prophecy song he must sing before Second Worldrend (knows it's coming)
9. **Unbound Knowledge:** Chronicled early Unbound formation; knows their original goals
10. **Immortality Price:** Secret deal with fey keeps him alive; price comes due soon

### Plot Hooks

2. **Memory Theft:** Someone stole three of his journals; contain damaging royal secrets
3. **The Lost Ballad:** Legendary song fragment discovered; must find remaining pieces

5. **Performance Crisis:** Must perform for hostile nobles; party provides security

## Hermit Sage Morganna Whisperwind
**"I have read every book worth reading twice. Some truths are found only in silence."**

**Status:** ALIVE - Hermit Scholar, Pre-Worldrend Expert  
**CR:** 9 (Wizard scholar with extensive knowledge)  
**Race:** Human (with fey-touched ancestry)  
**Age:** 312 years old (impossibly old for human, magical longevity)  

### Stat Block
```


### Background & History
Morganna was once a prominent healer in Silverpine, respected for her skill with both medicine and magic. Then she started hearing whispers—voices from dying patients, from the recently dead, from things that had never been alive. The voices drove her from the city, into the wilderness, where their chatter was quieter.

She's lived in her remote cottage for thirty years, visited only by those who need what she uniquely provides: healing for curses, potions that normal apothecaries can't make, and counsel from someone who hears both sides of the living and dead.

She's not mad—the whispers are real. She communes with spirits, ghosts, and stranger things. This has made her invaluable for certain problems and terrifying for most people. She's content with solitude; the living are exhausting, and the dead are usually more polite.

### Connections
- **Client:** Captain Marcus Frontiersman (provides control ritual)
- **Contact:** The Frost Seer Eirlys (fellow unusual seer)
- **Spirit Friends:** Several ghosts who provide information
- **Enemy:** A powerful ghost she bound that wants revenge
- **Worry:** The whispers are getting louder

### Secrets
1. **The Bound Ghost:** Bound a dangerous ghost years ago. It's been working to escape.
2. **The Death Knowledge:** Has learned things about what lies beyond death. It's changed her.
3. **The Living Reluctance:** Has developed abilities that could help cities. Refuses to return.
4. **The Ritual Collection:** Has developed rituals for communicating with various entities. Some are dangerous.
5. **The Coming Dead:** The whispers are telling her about a massive influx of spirits soon. Mass death approaches.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Ghost Consultation:** Can contact specific dead for information. Services available.
2. **The Bound Ghost Crisis:** The imprisoned ghost is breaking free. Needs help reinforcing the binding.
3. **The Mass Death Warning:** Shares her warning about coming death. Needs help investigating.
4. **The Ritual Teaching:** Might teach spirit communication to those who prove worthy.
5. **The Marcus Emergency:** Something's wrong with Captain Marcus's ritual. Needs urgent ingredients.

---
Medium Humanoid (Human), True Neutral

Armor Class: 13 (16 with mage armor)
Hit Points: 99 (18d8 + 18)
Speed: 25 ft. (slowed by age)

STR: 8 (-1)  DEX: 12 (+1)  CON: 13 (+1)
INT: 22 (+6)  WIS: 18 (+4)  CHA: 14 (+2)

Saving Throws: Int +11, Wis +9
Skills: Arcana +16 (expertise), History +16 (expertise), Insight +9, Investigation +11, Medicine +9, Nature +11, Perception +9, Religion +11
Damage Resistances: Psychic
Condition Immunities: None (deliberately refuses protections)
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft. (magical), Passive Perception 19, can see magic auras
Languages: Common, Elvish, Dwarvish, Draconic, Celestial, Infernal, Abyssal, Deep Speech, Primordial, Ancient Common (pre-Worldrend), Telepathy 60 ft.
Challenge Rating: 9 (5,000 XP)

SPECIAL ABILITIES:
Spellcasting: 14th-level wizard (School of Divination). Spell save DC 19, +11 to hit with spell attacks.

Spells Prepared:
Cantrips (at will): Light, Mage Hand, Message, Minor Illusion, Prestidigitation
1st level (4 slots): Comprehend Languages, Detect Magic, Identify, Mage Armor*
2nd level (3 slots): Detect Thoughts, Locate Object, See Invisibility
3rd level (3 slots): Clairvoyance, Dispel Magic, Tongues

7th level (1 slot): Etherealness, Sequester
*Usually active

Portent (2/Day): When she or creature she can see makes attack roll, ability check, or saving throw, she can replace the roll with one of two d20s she rolls at dawn. Must decide before roll is made.

Expert Divination: When casts divination spell of 2nd level or higher, regains expended spell slot of lower level.

- Darkvision 60 ft.
- See invisible creatures and objects within 10 ft.
- Read any language
- See into Ethereal Plane within 60 ft.

Magical Longevity: Extended life through careful spellcasting and fey pacts. Ages 1 year per 10 years.

Scholar's Mind: Perfect memory for anything read or studied. Can recall exact text from thousands of books.

Prophetic Dreams: Each long rest, DM rolls twice for random encounter/event. She can choose which occurs, or neither.

Forbidden Knowledge: Knows dangerous secrets about pre-Worldrend world, ancient rituals, true names, and lost magic.

Library Network: Has created scrying links to 20 major libraries. Can research in any of them remotely.

ACTIONS:
Quarterstaff: Melee Weapon Attack: +4 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d6-1 bludgeoning damage (1d8-1 versatile).

Cast a Spell: Casts a prepared spell.

Prophetic Warning (Recharge 5-6): Uses divination magic to predict enemy's next action. One creature within 60 ft. must reveal their intended action next turn. Morganna's allies gain advantage against that action.

Borrowed Knowledge (3/Day): Taps into collective knowledge of all libraries she's linked to. For 1 hour, has proficiency in any one skill, tool, or language of her choice.

Consult the Tome (1/Day): Opens her ancient grimoire and consults forgotten lore. Casts legend lore without expending spell slot. Takes 1 minute.

REACTIONS:
Shield: Casts shield to increase AC by 5 until start of next turn (spell).

Forewarned: After rolling initiative, can swap initiative with one willing creature she can see.

Prophetic Save: When ally she can see within 30 ft. fails saving throw, can use reaction to force reroll.

LEGENDARY ACTIONS (2 per round):
- Cantrip: Casts a cantrip.
- Move: Moves up to half speed.
- Consult Knowledge (Costs 2): Makes Intelligence check with advantage to recall lore.
- Scrying Glimpse (Costs 2): Uses scrying to observe a distant location for 1 minute (must have been there before).
```

### Equipment
- **Staff:** Ancient Quarterstaff (simple, but has been with her 200+ years)
- **Robes:** Sage's Robes (AC 11, dusty gray, countless pockets)
- **Ring:** Ring of Mind Shielding (protects from thought reading, holds her soul if killed)
- **Amulet:** Amulet of Proof Against Detection and Location
- **Glasses:** Spectacles of True Seeing (allows true seeing 1/day)
- **Headband:** Headband of Intellect (already included in stats)
- **Cloak:** Cloak of Elvenkind (advantage on Stealth, Perception can't see her)
- **Belt:** Belt of Many Pouches (contains spell components)
- **Books:** Personal grimoire (1,000 pages, 200+ years of notes)
- **Scrolls:** 10 scrolls of various divination spells
- **Potions:** 2 potions of longevity, 3 potions of healing
- **Library Key:** Master key that opens her hermitage library (3,000+ books)
- **Sending Stones:** 5 sending stones linked to other scholars
- **Telescope:** Astrological telescope (for star divination)

### Physical Description
Ancient and frail appearance (5'5", 110 lbs) despite magical longevity. Impossibly old for a human—312 years through magic and fey bargains. Hair is pure white, long and wild, often escapes from loose bun. Pale, paper-thin skin with age spots and wrinkles mapping centuries of study. Eyes are milky white (blind) but "see" through magical sight. Moves slowly, leaning on quarterstaff. Wears dusty gray robes covered in pockets containing scrolls, herbs, and oddities. Thick spectacles for reading (purely aesthetic, she "sees" magically). Smells of old parchment, dried lavender, and ancient dust. Trembling hands from age but mind is sharp as ever.

### Personality Traits
- Speaks in slow, whispery voice
- Frequently forgets she's speaking aloud vs. thinking
- Quotes obscure texts constantly
- Forgets to eat unless reminded
- Obsessively organizes knowledge
- Intolerant of intellectual laziness
- Values truth above all else (even painful truth)

**Ideals:**
- **Knowledge:** "All knowledge must be preserved, even dangerous knowledge."
- **Truth:** "Truth is truth, whether comfortable or devastating."
- **Memory:** "I am the keeper of what was, so others may learn what will be."
- **Neutrality:** "I observe and record, I do not judge or interfere."

**Bonds:**
- Her library (3,000+ books, some unique copies)
- The truth about the Worldrend (obsessed with discovering)
- Her apprentices (she's trained 8 scholars across centuries)
- Ancient texts she hasn't finished reading
- The fey who granted her extended life (complicated relationship)
- Memories of everyone she's known (all dead now)

**Flaws:**
- Socially inept after centuries alone
- Values knowledge over people's feelings
- Hoards dangerous information
- Refuses to share certain secrets (even if it would help)
- Fears death will erase her accumulated knowledge
- Lonely but won't admit it
- Sometimes wishes she had let herself die naturally

### Roleplaying Notes
- Touches books lovingly
- Forgets people's names but remembers obscure facts
- Falls asleep mid-conversation (advanced age)
- Speaks to herself constantly
- Quotes book titles and page numbers
- Makes tea obsessively (has 40+ varieties)
- Writes notes constantly in margins

**Speech Patterns:**
- "As stated in Volume XII of Arcturus's Compendium, page 247..."
- "*mutters* Where did I put that reference...oh, you're still here?"
- "I read about this 180 years ago. Let me think... *long pause*"
- "Interesting. *writes note* Continue speaking."

### Key Details
- 312 years old (impossible for normal human)
- Lives in hermitage 5 miles from Oakenheart
- Library contains 3,000+ books (many unique)
- Has corresponded with every major scholar for 200+ years
- Expert on pre-Worldrend era
- Extended life through fey pacts and magic
- Sees magically (physically blind)
- Trained 8 master scholars across her life

### Secrets
1. **True Age:** Actually 312, not the 280 she claims; extended by fey pact
2. **The Worldrend Answer:** Has pieced together what caused Worldrend; knowledge is dangerous
3. **Forbidden Texts:** Owns 12 books that contain world-threatening knowledge
4. **True Name Archive:** Documented true names of 40+ powerful entities (catastrophic if stolen)
5. **Fey Pact:** Bargained with fey for extended life; price was her sight and her ability to lie
6. **Second Worldrend:** Her research suggests another Worldrend is approaching
7. **The Cure:** Knows cure for lycanthropy, undeath, and several "incurable" conditions
8. **Ancient Vault:** Location of pre-Worldrend vault containing reality-warping artifacts
9. **Lord Shadows's Secret:** Discovered his true identity and goals; hasn't told anyone (waiting for right moment)
10. **Her Death Trigger:** Upon death, her library will burn automatically (fail-safe to prevent knowledge misuse)

### Plot Hooks
1. **Worldrend Research:** Needs party to retrieve ancient text from dangerous ruins
2. **Forbidden Book Theft:** One of her dangerous texts stolen; must recover before catastrophe
3. **The Apprentice:** Seeks final apprentice before she dies; party must help her search
4. **Fey Debt:** The fey demand payment; she needs party to negotiate new terms
5. **Second Worldrend:** Her research predicts date of next cataclysm; party must prevent it
6. **Ancient Vault:** She'll reveal location of vault in exchange for specific quest
7. **True Name Blackmail:** Someone discovered she has true name archive; wants to steal it
8. **Lycanthropy Cure:** She'll provide cure for Marcus if party helps with research
9. **Library Defense:** Unbound assault her hermitage for forbidden knowledge
10. **Final Confession:** She's dying; wants to pass all knowledge to worthy successor

### Connections
- **Elder Thalindra Oakheart:** Fellow ancient; trade historical knowledge; mutual respect
- **Archmage Veridian Starweaver:** Corresponded for 150+ years; intellectual equals
- **Bard Finnegan Storyteller:** He provides oral history; she provides written; collaborate
- **Professor Miranda Questseeker:** Her most recent apprentice (considers her successor)
- **The Frost Seer:** Both seers of future and past; occasionally share visions
- **Sage Cornelius the Elder:** Fellow scholar; friendly rivalry
- **Captain Marcus Frontiersman:** Researching lycanthropy cure for him
- **The Silver Wolf:** He visits occasionally; she studies his perfect control
- **Lord Shadows Blackwood:** Has discovered his true identity through research
- **Druid Elder Silvaris:** Both ancients; discuss philosophy and nature of time

## Archmage Veridian Starweaver (Expanded)
**"Magic is not power. It is responsibility. Those who forget this truth become tyrants or corpses."**

**Status:** ALIVE - Royal Archmage, Quest-Giver  
**CR:** 18 (Archmage)  
**Race:** High Elf  
**Age:** 624 years old  

### Stat Block
```
Medium Humanoid (Elf), Lawful Neutral

Armor Class: 15 (18 with mage armor)
Hit Points: 165 (22d8 + 66)
Speed: 30 ft.

STR: 10 (+0)  DEX: 16 (+3)  CON: 16 (+3)
INT: 22 (+6)  WIS: 18 (+4)  CHA: 18 (+4)

Saving Throws: Int +12, Wis +10, Cha +10
Skills: Arcana +18, History +12, Insight +10, Investigation +12, Perception +10
Damage Resistances: Damage from spells (Magic Resistance)
Senses: Darkvision 60 ft., Passive Perception 20
Languages: Common, Elvish, Draconic, Celestial, Infernal, Sylvan, Dwarvish, Deep Speech
Challenge Rating: 18 (20,000 XP)

RACIAL ABILITIES:
Fey Ancestry: Advantage against being charmed, immune to magic sleep.
Trance: Meditates 4 hours instead of sleeping.

SPECIAL ABILITIES:
Spellcasting: 18th-level wizard. Spell save DC 20, +12 to hit with spell attacks.

Spells Prepared (can cast any wizard spell, but typically has these ready):
Cantrips (at will): Fire Bolt, Light, Mage Hand, Prestidigitation, Ray of Frost
1st level (4 slots): Detect Magic, Identify, Mage Armor*, Shield
2nd level (3 slots): Detect Thoughts, Mirror Image, Misty Step
3rd level (3 slots): Counterspell, Dispel Magic, Fireball
4th level (3 slots): Arcane Eye, Banishment, Greater Invisibility
5th level (3 slots): Cone of Cold, Scrying, Wall of Force
6th level (2 slots): Disintegrate, Globe of Invulnerability, True Seeing
7th level (2 slots): Teleport, Plane Shift, Forcecage
8th level (1 slot): Mind Blank*, Maze
9th level (1 slot): Time Stop, Wish (rarely used)
*Usually active

Magic Resistance: Advantage on saving throws against spells and magical effects.

Arcane Recovery (1/Day): During a short rest, recovers expended spell slots up to 9th level combined.

Signature Spells: Can cast Counterspell and Dispel Magic without expending spell slots (each 1/short rest).

Scrying Network: Maintains 12 crystal balls across both kingdoms, can use as bonus action to switch views.

Starweaver Bloodline: Once per day, can cast any divination spell without expending a spell slot.

LEGENDARY RESISTANCE (3/Day): If he fails a saving throw, he can choose to succeed instead.

ACTIONS:
Multiattack: Casts a cantrip and uses his Starlight Staff, or casts two cantrips.

Starlight Staff (Quarterstaff +3): Melee Weapon Attack: +9 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d6+3 bludgeoning damage (1d8+3 versatile) plus 2d10 force damage.
Special: Functions as Staff of Power. Can cast wizard spells through the staff as a bonus action.

Fire Bolt: Ranged Spell Attack: +12 to hit, range 120 ft., one target.
Hit: 4d10 fire damage.

Cast a Spell: Casts a spell from prepared list.

Teleportation Circle (Special): Can teleport party to any permanent circle he knows (costs 5,000 gp in materials, usually charges 1,000 gp per person).

REACTIONS:
Shield: Casts Shield to increase AC by 5 until start of next turn.

Counterspell: Automatically counters spells of 5th level or lower, makes check for higher levels (+12 bonus).

Absorb Spell (Staff of Power, 3/Day): When targeted by a spell, absorb it into staff and regain spell slot equal to spell's level.

LEGENDARY ACTIONS (3 per round):
- Cantrip: Casts a cantrip.
- Detect Magic: Uses detect magic sense (knows presence of magic within 30 ft.).
- Teleport (Costs 2): Uses misty step without expending a spell slot.
- Cast Spell (Costs 3): Casts a spell of 3rd level or lower from prepared list.
```

### Background & History
Born over four centuries ago in the ancient elven city of Aethermere, Veridian showed prodigious magical talent before he could walk. He was formally inducted into the Arcanum at age forty (young for an elf), became a full wizard at one hundred, and achieved the rank of Archmage at two hundred and fifty—the youngest in recorded history.

His specialty is divination, but his true mastery lies in the intersection of magical schools. He developed the Starweaver Synthesis—a technique for combining spells of different schools into hybrid effects. The technique is now taught at every major magical academy, though few can replicate his fluency.

He has served as headmaster of the Silverpine Arcanum for seventy-five years, overseeing its expansion from regional school to continental institution. Under his leadership, enrollment has tripled, and the school has produced three archmages and dozens of notable wizards.

Despite his power, Veridian is approachable and patient with students. He remembers what it was like to struggle with concepts, even if it was four hundred years ago. His office door is always open, and he teaches at least one introductory class per term "to remember where magic begins."

### Connections
- **Sage Thelmar Runescribe:** His most promising former student, now serving the crown
- **Professor Elara Moonwhisper:** Faculty colleague who shares his interest in celestial phenomena
- **Archmage Eldrin Aethermere:** Secret correspondent in Aethoria, sharing research across the Sundering Sea
- **The Circle of Eight:** Rumored member, though he neither confirms nor denies
- **High Diviner Celestia Starborn:** His successor as head of Divination, though they disagree on methodology

### Secrets
1. **Circle Membership:** He is indeed one of the Circle of Eight, though the organization operates more loosely than legends suggest.
2. **The Prophecy:** Has foreseen something catastrophic approaching within the next decade, but the vision is unclear and he fears acting on incomplete information.
3. **Aetherian Contact:** His correspondence with Archmage Eldrin involves more than research—they're developing a way to safely cross the Sundering Sea.
4. **Mortality's Approach:** Despite elven longevity, he can feel his time ending within the century. He's quietly preparing for succession.
5. **The Forbidden Research:** Keeps a sealed section in the library containing knowledge too dangerous to destroy but too dangerous to share.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Prophecy:** Veridian needs help investigating his unclear vision. The party might be pieces of the puzzle.
2. **The Crossing:** The Aetherian passage project is reaching a critical phase. He needs brave souls to test it.
3. **Succession Planning:** Time to identify and test the next headmaster. The candidates are all flawed in different ways.
4. **The Sealed Section:** Something has been disturbed in the forbidden library. Investigation required.
5. **Circle Business:** The other Circle members need a favor, and Veridian is calling in markers.


### Equipment
- **Robes:** Archmage's Robes (AC 15 + Dex, advantage on saves vs. spells)
- **Staff:** Starlight Staff (Staff of Power, legendary, +3 quarterstaff, 20 charges)
- **Ring:** Ring of Spell Storing (contains Shield, Counterspell, Dispel Magic)
- **Cloak:** Cloak of Protection +1
- **Amulet:** Amulet of Proof Against Detection and Location
- **Headband:** Circlet of Intellect (already included in stats)
- **Spellbook:** "The Cosmic Codex" - contains all wizard spells up to 9th level
- **Communication Crystals:** 12 sending stones linked to allies
- **Scrying Orb:** Crystal ball with true seeing
- **Potions:** 3 potions of supreme healing, 1 potion of invulnerability
- **Teleportation Chalk:** For creating temporary circles (10 uses)

### Physical Description
Tall and slender (6'1", 145 lbs) with the timeless grace of high elves. Silver-white hair worn long and loose, often floating slightly as if in an invisible breeze. Eyes shift color with his mood - blue when calm, violet when using divination, gold when angry. Pale, ageless features marked with faint runic tattoos along his temples (warding glyphs). Wears flowing robes of deep midnight blue with silver star patterns that actually twinkle. The Starlight Staff pulses with gentle light and is never far from his hand.

### Personality Traits
- Speaks in measured, precise sentences
- Makes direct eye contact that seems to see through deception
- Often pauses mid-conversation to consult magical sensors
- Gestures create small sparkles of light
- Has a dry, understated sense of humor
- Never panics - has seen too much

**Ideals:**
- **Responsibility:** "Those with power must use it to protect the powerless."
- **Knowledge:** "Understanding magic prevents its misuse."
- **Balance:** "Neither kingdom should dominate - equilibrium preserves peace."

**Bonds:**
- King Aldric IV (advised him since he was a child)
- The Kingdom of Thaldros
- His students and apprentices
- The truth about the Worldrend (obsessed with preventing repetition)
- Tower library (contains irreplaceable texts)

**Flaws:**
- Sometimes too cautious, overthinks decisions
- Struggles to trust others with important tasks
- Secret guilt over not predicting something in the past
- Workaholic - sleeps only 4 hours per night
- Underestimates threats outside magical realm

**Expanded Role in Campaigns:**
**Primary Function:** High-level quest giver, magical expertise, investigation coordinator

**Key Details (Expanded):**
- Personal advisor to King Aldric IV
- Suspects Unbound infiltration of royal court
- Trained half the wizards in both kingdoms
- Tower in Kaer Thandros serves as adventure hub
- Possesses extensive scrying network
- Can teleport party to mission locations
- Maintains magical communication crystals

**Campaign Quest Types:**
1. **Investigation:** "Strange magical signatures detected - investigate source"
2. **Retrieval:** "Ancient artifact must be secured before Unbound finds it"
3. **Protection:** "Scholar in danger - escort them safely to my tower"
4. **Research:** "I need rare components/texts - can you acquire them?"
5. **Counter-intelligence:** "Spy among court wizards - identify them"

**Rewards Offered:**
- Spell scrolls and magical items
- Access to his personal library
- Training in advanced magic
- Teleportation services
- Introductions to other powerful allies
- Information about party's personal quests

**Relationship Progression:**
- **Suspicious** (first quest): Tests party's loyalty and competence
- **Interested** (after 2-3 quests): Offers better rewards, more trust
- **Allied** (after 5+ quests): Shares critical information, major support
- **Confidant** (late campaign): Reveals full knowledge of Unbound, recruits party for final missions

**Secrets He Can Reveal:**
- Lord Shadows Blackwood's true identity and motivations
- Location of pre-Worldrend artifacts
- Weaknesses of Unbound leadership
- Truth about Worldrend's cause
- Prophecies about Second Worldrend

**Connections:**
- Corresponds with Hermit Sage Morganna
- Knows The Frost Seer's visions are accurate
- Has met Matriarch Seraphina Silverleaf
- Studied under High Mage Arcturus (ghost) through séances
- Aware of Professor Miranda's research

## Professor Miranda Questseeker (Expanded)
**"Every mystery has a solution. We simply must ask the right questions."**

**Status:** ALIVE - Silverpine University Professor, Investigation Expert  
**CR:** 9 (Expert investigator)  
**Race:** Human  
**Age:** 42  

### Stat Block
```
Medium Humanoid (Human), Lawful Good

Armor Class: 13 (16 with mage armor)
Hit Points: 78 (12d8 + 24)
Speed: 30 ft.

STR: 10 (+0)  DEX: 14 (+2)  CON: 14 (+2)
INT: 20 (+5)  WIS: 16 (+3)  CHA: 14 (+2)

Saving Throws: Int +9, Wis +7
Skills: Arcana +13, History +13, Investigation +13, Insight +7, Perception +7, Persuasion +6
Senses: Passive Perception 17
Languages: Common, Elvish, Dwarvish, Draconic, Ancient Common (pre-Worldrend dialect)
Challenge Rating: 9 (5,000 XP)

SPECIAL ABILITIES:
Spellcasting: 9th-level wizard (Divination school). Spell save DC 17, +9 to hit with spell attacks.

Spells Prepared:
Cantrips (at will): Light, Mage Hand, Message, Prestidigitation
1st level (4 slots): Comprehend Languages, Detect Magic, Identify, Mage Armor*
2nd level (3 slots): Detect Thoughts, Locate Object, See Invisibility
3rd level (3 slots): Clairvoyance, Dispel Magic, Tongues
4th level (3 slots): Arcane Eye, Locate Creature
5th level (1 slot): Legend Lore, Scrying
*Usually active

Expert Knowledge: Has advantage on all Intelligence checks related to history, arcana, and investigation. On a failed check, can reroll once per day.

Researcher's Network: Can send messages to student assistants across both kingdoms. Within 24 hours, receives information as if casting Legend Lore (no spell slot needed, 1/day).

Quick Study: Can learn one new language by studying for 1 week, or decipher unknown writing with 1 hour of study (DC 15 Intelligence check).

Academic Authority: Has advantage on Persuasion checks when dealing with scholars, nobility, or in academic settings.

Encyclopedic Memory: Can perfectly recall any text she's read. Has access to knowledge equivalent to a library in her mind.

ACTIONS:
Multiattack: Makes two dagger attacks or casts a cantrip and uses a dagger.

Dagger +1: Melee or Ranged Weapon Attack: +7 to hit, reach 5 ft. or range 20/60 ft.
Hit: 1d4+3 piercing damage.

Light Crossbow: Ranged Weapon Attack: +6 to hit, range 80/320 ft.
Hit: 1d8+2 piercing damage.

Cast a Spell: Casts a prepared spell.

Share Knowledge (Recharge 5-6): Grants one ally advantage on their next Intelligence, Wisdom, or Charisma check as she provides relevant historical context or tactical advice.

REACTIONS:
Defensive Scholar: When hit by an attack, can impose disadvantage on the attack roll (3/day). Represents ducking behind cover or using an object as a shield.

Counterspell (3rd level): Can counter a spell of 3rd level or lower, or make a check (+9) for higher levels.

BONUS ACTIONS:
Academic Insight: After observing a creature for 1 round, learn its type, one resistance or immunity, and one special ability (if any).
```

### Background & History
Miranda earned her nickname honestly—she's never met a mystery she didn't want to solve or a question she wasn't willing to pursue across continents. Born in Crossvale to a merchant family, she rejected the family business at sixteen to attend the Arcanum, specializing in historical research and artifact identification.

Her breakthrough came at thirty-five when she correctly identified a "worthless" brooch in a museum collection as a pre-Worldrend communication device. The discovery made her reputation and funded her next twenty years of research.

Now fifty-eight, she holds the Chair of Ancient Studies at the Arcanum and has authored twelve books on pre-Worldrend civilizations. Her field expeditions are legendary—equal parts brilliant archaeological work and barely-survived disasters. Students compete fiercely for spots on her research teams.

Her methodology is controversial in academic circles. She believes in getting her hands dirty, taking calculated risks, and following hunches. "You can't understand history from a library chair," she's fond of saying. "You have to dig it up."

### Connections
- **Merchant Princess Yasmin:** Rival and occasional collaborator in artifact acquisition
- **Archmage Veridian Starweaver:** Mentor who indulges her unconventional methods
- **Caravan Master Hassan:** Has provided transport for several expeditions
- **Tomb Raiders Guild:** Complicated relationship—she buys from them while publicly condemning them
- **Research Assistants:** A rotating cast of graduate students who emerge from her expeditions either traumatized or transformed

### Secrets
1. **The Forbidden Dig:** Found a pre-Worldrend site five years ago that she's kept secret because what's there is too dangerous to excavate.
2. **The Tomb Raiders:** More than just a buyer—she founded the guild thirty years ago to fund her research, then "left" while keeping a controlling interest.
3. **Personal Tragedy:** Lost her husband and daughter on an expedition fifteen years ago. Threw herself into work to avoid dealing with grief she's never processed.
4. **The Artifact Collection:** Has a private collection of artifacts too dangerous or valuable to document publicly.
5. **Worldrend Knowledge:** Believes she knows what caused the Worldrend, but the implications are so disturbing she's never published her findings.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Forbidden Site:** She's finally ready to excavate, but needs a capable team to handle what's down there.
2. **The Guild Problem:** Someone is using her Tomb Raiders for something she didn't authorize. Time to investigate.
3. **Family Ghosts:** Evidence suggests her family might have survived the expedition. Or something wearing their faces has.
4. **The Publication:** She's decided to publish her Worldrend theory. Multiple parties want to stop her.
5. **Rival's Revenge:** Yasmin has discovered something Miranda wants desperately and is making her work for it.


### Equipment
- **Armor:** Bracers of Defense (AC 13 + Dex)
- **Weapons:** Dagger +1 (silver-inlaid, inscribed with runes), light crossbow
- **Ring:** Ring of Mind Shielding (thoughts can't be read, immune to detect thoughts)
- **Cloak:** Cloak of Elvenkind (advantage on Stealth checks)
- **Spectacles:** Glasses of Seeing (advantage on Investigation and Perception checks involving sight)
- **Bag:** Bag of Holding (contains research materials, books, maps, artifacts)
- **Spellbook:** "The Investigator's Compendium" - Contains all her prepared spells plus 20+ utility spells
- **Research Materials:** Notebooks (12), quills, ink, chalk, measuring tools
- **Artifacts:** 3 minor pre-Worldrend artifacts she's studying
- **Potions:** 2 potions of healing, 1 potion of invisibility
- **Communication:** Sending stone linked to Archmage Veridian

### Physical Description
Average height (5'6", 135 lbs) with an energetic, purposeful demeanor. Brown hair usually tied back in a practical bun, often with a quill stuck through it. Sharp hazel eyes behind round spectacles that seem to analyze everything. Wears practical scholar's robes in university colors (deep green and gold) with many pockets for note-taking supplies. Always has ink stains on her fingers. Carries a worn leather satchel full of books and papers. Moves with nervous energy, often gesturing enthusiastically when explaining discoveries.

### Personality Traits
- Speaks rapidly when excited about research
- Constantly takes notes (even mid-conversation)
- Asks dozens of follow-up questions
- Gets distracted by interesting tangents
- Extremely organized despite appearing scattered
- Enthusiastic about mysteries

**Ideals:**
- **Truth:** "Knowledge must be preserved and shared, not hidden or destroyed."
- **Discovery:** "Every question answered reveals ten more questions. That's the joy of research."
- **Preservation:** "History forgotten is doomed to repeat."

**Bonds:**
- Silverpine University and its archives
- Her students (protective of them)
- The truth about House Blackwood
- Historical accuracy and record-keeping
- Hermit Sage Morganna (mentor figure)

**Flaws:**
- Sometimes ignores danger when focused on research
- Naive about political dangers
- Trusts written sources too readily
- Workaholic who forgets to eat or sleep
- Uncomfortable in combat situations

### Roleplaying Notes
- Constantly adjusts her spectacles
- Mutters to herself when thinking
- Pulls out notebooks to reference previous findings
- Gets excited and talks faster
- Apologizes for going off on tangents
- Makes connections others miss

**Expanded Role in Campaigns:**
**Primary Function:** Investigation coordinator, research quest-giver, mystery solver

**Key Details (Expanded):**
- Leading expert on pre-Worldrend history
- Secretly investigating House Blackwood's fall
- Knows more about Unbound than she should
- Employs network of student researchers
- Has contacts in both kingdoms
- Often in danger due to discoveries
- Enthusiastic about hiring adventurers for field work

**Campaign Quest Types:**
1. **Archaeological:** "Ruins discovered - need exploration team"
2. **Historical:** "Interview survivors of [event] - record testimonies"
3. **Retrieval:** "Specific text/artifact needed for research"
4. **Protection:** "My research threatened - need guards"
5. **Investigation:** "Follow these leads - report findings"

**Research Topics (Quest Hooks):**
- House Blackwood's true fate and heir survival
- Pre-Worldrend civilization and technology
- Magical anomalies across both continents
- Dragon treaties and their violations
- Unbound faction activities (dangerous)
- Ancient prophecies about reunification

**Rewards Offered:**
- Historical knowledge and context
- Academic credentials (advantage on social interactions)
- Access to university restricted archives
- Letters of recommendation to nobility
- Payment in gold (university funded)
- Credit in published papers (fame)

**Character Development:**
- Starts as detached academic
- Becomes personally invested in stopping Unbound
- Eventually joins party as support NPC if convinced
- Can provide crucial breakthrough at key moment
- May be targeted for assassination (rescue mission)

**Secrets She Knows:**
1. Lord Shadows is legitimate Blackwood heir
2. Unbound seeking specific pre-Worldrend artifact
3. Location of House Blackwood's hidden vault
4. Truth about royal succession dispute
5. Pattern in magical disturbances (Second Worldrend signs)

**Connections:**
- Former colleague of Hermit Sage Morganna
- Corresponds with Archmage Veridian
- Knows Sage Elminster's research
- Has interviewed Captain Marcus about werewolves
- Student of historical figures through texts

## Master Hunter Kael Dragonsbane (Expanded)
**"Dragons aren't evil. They're territorial, predatory, and incredibly dangerous. Rather like humans, honestly."**

**Status:** ALIVE - Elite Monster Hunter, Dragon Expert  
**CR:** 13 (Legendary monster hunter)  
**Race:** Human  
**Age:** 47  

### Stat Block
```
Medium Humanoid (Human), Neutral Good

Armor Class: 18 (dragon scale mail)
Hit Points: 180 (19d10 + 76)
Speed: 40 ft.

STR: 18 (+4)  DEX: 20 (+5)  CON: 18 (+4)
INT: 14 (+2)  WIS: 18 (+4)  CHA: 12 (+1)

Saving Throws: Str +9, Dex +10, Con +9, Wis +9
Skills: Athletics +9, Insight +9, Nature +7, Perception +14, Stealth +10, Survival +14
Damage Resistances: Fire (from dragon scale armor)
Senses: Passive Perception 24, Darkvision 60 ft. (goggles)
Languages: Common, Draconic, Giant, Sylvan, limited Abyssal
Challenge Rating: 13 (10,000 XP)

SPECIAL ABILITIES:
Legendary Monster Hunter: Has advantage on Wisdom (Survival) checks to track creatures and Intelligence checks to recall information about creatures.

Favored Enemy (Dragons): Has advantage on all checks related to dragons. Deals an extra 2d6 damage to dragons with weapon attacks.

Additional Favored Enemies: Giants, undead, aberrations (extra 1d6 damage to each)

Natural Explorer: Ignores difficult terrain, can't be tracked against his will, advantage on initiative rolls.

Multiattack: Makes three attacks with weapons or two attacks and uses a special ability.

Extra Attack (2): Can attack three times when taking the Attack action.

Hunter's Mark (At Will): Can mark a creature he can see within 90 ft. as bonus action. Deals extra 1d8 damage to marked target, has advantage on tracking it. Lasts until target drops to 0 HP or Kael dismisses it.

Slayer's Counter (3/Day): When a Large or larger creature misses him with an attack, can use reaction to make an attack against that creature.

Dragon Slayer: Critical hits on dragons. When he scores a critical hit against a dragon, the dragon must make DC 17 Constitution save or be stunned until end of Kael's next turn.

Uncanny Dodge: When an attacker he can see hits him, can use reaction to halve the damage.

Evasion: When subjected to effect that allows Dex save for half damage, takes no damage on success and half on failure.

ACTIONS:
Multiattack: Makes three attacks with Dragonpiercer or longbow, or two attacks and uses Hunter's Mark or Tactical Command.

Dragonpiercer (Longsword +2): Melee Weapon Attack: +11 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d8+7 slashing damage (1d10+7 versatile) plus 2d6 force damage.
Special: This weapon was forged from an ancient dragon's fang. Deals double damage to dragons and ignores dragon damage resistances.

Longbow +1 (Dragonbone Bow): Ranged Weapon Attack: +11 to hit, range 150/600 ft.
Hit: 1d8+6 piercing damage plus 1d8 fire damage.
Special: Arrows burst into flame mid-flight. Can cast Hunter's Mark as part of this attack.

Silvered Shortsword: Melee Weapon Attack: +10 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d6+5 piercing damage. Counts as silvered and magical for overcoming resistances.

Net (Specialty): Ranged Weapon Attack: +10 to hit, range 5/15 ft.
Hit: Target is restrained. DC 17 Strength check to escape. Kael's nets are reinforced adamantine (AC 15, 20 HP).

Tactical Command (Recharge 5-6): Kael barks orders to allies. All allies within 60 ft. who can hear him gain advantage on their next attack roll or saving throw, and their movement doesn't provoke opportunity attacks until start of their next turn.

REACTIONS:
Slayer's Counter: When a Large or larger creature misses him, make one weapon attack against it.

Uncanny Dodge: Halve damage from one attack he can see.

Protective Throw (3/Day): When an ally within 5 ft. is hit by an attack, Kael can push them out of harm's way (they move 5 ft. without provoking opportunity attacks) and take the hit himself.

LEGENDARY ACTIONS (3 per round):
- Move: Moves up to his speed without provoking opportunity attacks.
- Attack: Makes one weapon attack.
- Hunter's Mark (Costs 2): Uses Hunter's Mark on a new target.
- Exploit Weakness (Costs 2): One ally gains advantage on their next attack against Kael's marked target.
```

### Background & History
Kael earned his epithet the hard way—by killing dragons. Not through luck or ambush, but through decades of study, preparation, and countless near-death experiences. He's survived encounters with fourteen dragons and killed eight of them (with significant help).

Born in a frontier village constantly threatened by a young red dragon, Kael lost half his family before he turned twelve. He dedicated his life to ensuring other families wouldn't suffer the same fate. He joined the Silver Wardens at fifteen, studied under their best monster hunters, and eventually specialized in the most dangerous game.

His approach combines scholarly research with practical hunting. He knows dragon anatomy, behavior patterns, territorial instincts, and weaknesses. He's written the definitive guide to dragon hunting (circulation restricted by the Wardens—they don't want amateurs trying).

At sixty-four, his body is failing faster than his spirit. Old injuries accumulate, and he knows he has perhaps five more years of field work. He's focused now on passing his knowledge to the next generation, though finding students capable of surviving the training is challenging.

### Connections
- **Warden Commander Thalia Moonbow:** His commanding officer and one of the few people he considers a peer
- **Scout Captain Finn Quickfoot:** The halfling has discovered something Kael needs to investigate
- **Master Smith Durgan Forgefire:** Creates his specialized dragon-hunting equipment
- **The Dragon Infernalix:** The great wyrm that threatened Kaer Thandros—Kael has studied him for decades
- **Surviving Students:** Only three of the twelve hunters he's trained are still alive

### Secrets
1. **Infernalix's Deal:** Knows about the old king's bargain with the dragon. Suspects it's coming due soon.
2. **The Ninth Dragon:** There's one he's never spoken about—a dragon he befriended rather than killed, who shares information about dragonkind.
3. **Failing Body:** His injuries are worse than he lets on. Some days he can barely grip a sword.
4. **The Survivor's Guilt:** Three of his students died because of his decisions. He replays those moments constantly.
5. **Dragon Blood:** During one fight, he was bathed in dragon blood. It changed him subtly—better senses, resistance to fire, and dreams he doesn't understand.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Final Hunt:** One last dragon needs killing before Kael retires. The most dangerous one yet.
2. **Finn's Discovery:** The halfling scout has found tracks that suggest something ancient is awakening.
3. **Dragon Friend:** His dragon contact has sent a warning—others of its kind are planning something.
4. **Student's Legacy:** One of his dead students had a child who's now old enough to demand answers about how their parent died.
5. **The Blood's Call:** His dragon-blood changes are intensifying. He needs to understand what's happening before it's too late.


### Equipment
- **Armor:** Dragon Scale Mail (AC 14 + Dex, max +2, fire resistance) - Made from black dragon scales
- **Primary Weapon:** Dragonpiercer (Longsword +2, legendary, dragon fang hilt, glows near dragons)
- **Ranged Weapon:** Dragonbone Bow (Longbow +1, fires flaming arrows, 20 arrows)
- **Secondary:** Silvered Shortsword (magical, silvered)
- **Utility:** 3 adamantine nets, hunter's trap kit, climbing gear
- **Eye Patch:** Goggles of Night (darkvision 60 ft.) - covers missing left eye
- **Cloak:** Cloak of Elvenkind (advantage on Stealth)
- **Boots:** Boots of Speed (double speed as bonus action, 10 rounds/day)
- **Pouch:** Bag of dragon parts (scales, claws, teeth for crafting)
- **Potions:** 3 potions of superior healing, 1 potion of fire resistance, 1 potion of invulnerability
- **Tools:** Hunting traps, caltrops, manacles (masterwork)
- **Trophy:** Preserved ancient dragon claw (proof of his legend)

### Physical Description
Weathered and scarred (6'2", 210 lbs of muscle), every inch the veteran monster hunter. Left eye covered by dark leather eye patch with brass fittings, lost to dragon acid. Face marked with three parallel scars across right cheek (dragon claw). Short brown hair going gray at temples, kept practical. Wears dragon scale armor that's clearly seen heavy use, polished but dented. Moves with economy of motion - no wasted movement. His one remaining eye is steel-gray and misses nothing. Dragonpiercer sword always at his hip, dragonbone bow across his back. Smells faintly of dragon musk and woodsmoke.

### Personality Traits
- Speaks in short, efficient sentences
- Constantly assesses threats in any room
- Respectful to worthy opponents (including monsters)
- Patient and observant
- Dry, dark humor about injuries
- Never boasts - his scars speak for him

**Ideals:**
- **Balance:** "Nature needs predators. We're one of them."
- **Respect:** "Killing should be for protection or survival, never sport."
- **Mentorship:** "Knowledge dies with us unless we pass it on."

**Bonds:**
- The wilds and natural world
- His students and apprentices
- The memory of his original hunting party (all dead)
- Captain Marcus (friend, lycanthropy cases)
- The people threatened by monsters

**Flaws:**
- Survivor's guilt over lost companions
- Sometimes treats people like prey to be studied
- Underestimates non-physical threats
- Haunted by the dragon that took his eye
- Drinks heavily after difficult hunts

### Roleplaying Notes
- Touches his eye patch when thinking
- Checks escape routes instinctively
- Speaks about dragons with mixture of respect and hatred
- Offers tactical advice mid-combat
- Tells hunting stories with lessons embedded

**Expanded Role in Campaigns:**
**Primary Function:** Monster hunting quests, dangerous creature expert, combat mentor

**Key Details (Expanded):**
- Survived encounter with ancient dragon
- Trains aspiring monster hunters
- Travels between both continents
- Knows weaknesses of all major monster types
- Can be hired for specific hunts
- Respects worthy prey (won't hunt unnecessarily)
- Missing eye, scarred extensively, still formidable

**Campaign Quest Types:**
1. **Hunting:** "Dangerous creature threatening settlement - eliminate it"
2. **Capture:** "Rare specimen needed alive for study"
3. **Training:** "Learn proper techniques for hunting [monster type]"
4. **Investigation:** "Unusual monster behavior - determine cause"
5. **Escort:** "Transporting dangerous cargo - need protection"

**Specialization by Monster Type:**
- **Dragons:** Knows habits, lairs, weaknesses (signature)
- **Giants:** Diplomacy and combat tactics
- **Aberrations:** Identification and elimination
- **Undead:** Tracking and destruction methods
- **Fey:** Negotiation and counter-magic
- **Lycanthropes:** Non-lethal containment (works with Captain Marcus)

**Training Services:**
- Combat technique improvements (+1 to attack rolls vs. specific creature type)
- Monster lore (advantage on knowledge checks)
- Tracking skills (advantage on survival checks)
- Tactical planning (bonus to initiative vs. large creatures)
- Survival in hostile terrain

**Rewards Offered:**
- Gold payment (standard rates)
- Monster parts and crafting materials
- Magical weapons from his collection
- Training and skill improvement
- Reputation among hunter guilds
- Connections to wealthy clients

**Character Arc:**
- Initially just doing job
- Recognizes party's potential
- Becomes mentor figure
- May sacrifice himself protecting party from dragon
- Or aids in final confrontation with ancient threat

**Secrets He Knows:**
1. Morveth Shadowmane's approximate location
2. Dragon Infernalix may still be alive
3. Unbound using monsters as weapons
4. Location of several dragon hoards
5. Ritual to summon/communicate with dragons

**Connections:**
- Works with Captain Marcus (lycanthropy expert)
- Hired by both royal courts
- Knows Silver Wolf's identity (respects the choice)
- Has treaties with some intelligent monsters
- Former student of Ranger-Lord Silvanus's techniques

## Captain Thalia Lightbringer
**"Justice without mercy is tyranny. Mercy without justice is weakness. We must be both."**

**Status:** ALIVE - Paladin, Iron Council Representative  
**CR:** 11 (Oath of Devotion Paladin)  
**Race:** Human  
**Age:** 34  

### Stat Block
```
Medium Humanoid (Human), Lawful Good

Armor Class: 20 (plate armor +1, shield +1, Defense fighting style)
Hit Points: 136 (16d10 + 48)
Speed: 30 ft.

STR: 18 (+4)  DEX: 12 (+1)  CON: 16 (+3)
INT: 12 (+1)  WIS: 16 (+3)  CHA: 20 (+5)

Saving Throws: Wis +7, Cha +9
Skills: Athletics +8, Insight +7, Intimidation +9, Medicine +7, Persuasion +9, Religion +5
Damage Resistances: Radiant (divine blessing)
Condition Immunities: Frightened (Aura of Courage)
Senses: Passive Perception 13, Divine Sense 60 ft.
Languages: Common, Celestial
Challenge Rating: 11 (7,200 XP)

PALADIN ABILITIES:
Divine Sense (5/Day): As action, detect celestials, fiends, undead within 60 ft. Can also sense Unbound corruption (unique).

Lay on Hands (80 HP/Day): Can heal 80 HP total or cure diseases/poisons (5 HP per condition).

Fighting Style: Defense (+1 AC while wearing armor, already included).

Divine Smite: When she hits with melee weapon, can expend spell slot to deal extra radiant damage (2d8 for 1st level, +1d8 per slot level, +1d8 vs undead/fiends, max 5d8).

Extra Attack: Attacks twice when taking Attack action.

Aura of Protection (10 ft.): She and allies within 10 ft. gain +5 to all saving throws.

Aura of Courage (10 ft.): She and allies within 10 ft. are immune to being frightened.

Aura of Devotion (10 ft.): She and allies within 10 ft. can't be charmed.

Divine Health: Immune to disease.

SPELLCASTING:
Spellcasting: 11th-level paladin. Spell save DC 17, +9 to hit with spell attacks.

Spells Prepared (Oath of Devotion):
1st level (4 slots): Bless, Command, Cure Wounds, Detect Evil and Good, Protection from Evil and Good*, Sanctuary
2nd level (3 slots): Aid, Lesser Restoration, Zone of Truth* (at will, special)
3rd level (3 slots): Beacon of Hope, Dispel Magic, Revivify
*Oath spells, always prepared

SPECIAL ABILITIES:
Sacred Weapon (1/Day): As action, Dawnbreaker emits bright light (20 ft. radius), adds +5 to attack rolls for 1 minute. Can end early to cast Dispel Magic.

Turn the Unholy (1/Day): As action, each fiend or undead within 30 ft. must make DC 17 Wisdom save or be turned for 1 minute.

Radiant Presence: She glows faintly with golden light (dim light 5 ft.). Increases to bright light 20 ft. when using divine abilities.

Champion of the Iron Council: Advantage on Persuasion checks with lawful good creatures and disadvantage on Deception checks (can't lie convincingly - too honest).

LEGENDARY ACTIONS (3 per round, CR 11+):
- Move: Moves up to her speed.
- Attack: Makes one melee attack.
- Healing Touch (Costs 2): Uses Lay on Hands to heal an ally within touch range (up to 20 HP).
- Divine Command (Costs 2): Casts Command without expending a spell slot.
- Inspire (Costs 3): All allies within 30 ft. gain temporary HP equal to her Charisma modifier + paladin level (10 temp HP) and advantage on their next attack roll or saving throw.

ACTIONS:
Multiattack: Makes two attacks with Dawnbreaker.

Dawnbreaker (Longsword +2): Melee Weapon Attack: +10 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d8+6 slashing damage (1d10+6 versatile) plus 2d6 radiant damage.
Special: This legendary holy sword (formerly Paladin Radiant's) glows near betrayers and oathbreakers. Once per day can cast Daylight. Deals extra 2d6 radiant damage to undead and fiends (total 4d6).

Shield Bash: Melee Weapon Attack: +8 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d4+4 bludgeoning damage, target must succeed DC 16 Strength save or be knocked prone.

Javelin: Ranged Weapon Attack: +8 to hit, range 30/120 ft.
Hit: 1d6+4 piercing damage.

Cast a Spell: Casts a prepared paladin spell.

REACTIONS:
Shield of Faith: When an ally within 5 ft. is hit, can use reaction to impose disadvantage on attack roll or grant +2 AC against that attack (3/day).

Divine Retribution: When hit by a melee attack, attacker takes 2d8 radiant damage (Charisma modifier/day, 5 uses).
```

### Background & History
Born to a minor noble family in Silverpine, Thalia was raised with privilege but felt called to service. She joined the Lightbringers at eighteen, one of the few women in the order at the time, and proved herself through sheer determination and undeniable faith.

Her defining moment came during the Tomb of Shadows expedition—a disaster that killed twenty-three Lightbringers and nearly released an imprisoned lich. Thalia was one of seven survivors and the one who ultimately sealed the tomb, though it cost her left arm below the elbow.

She now wears a blessed prosthetic forged by dwarven artificers and enchanted by the order's chaplains. It functions nearly as well as flesh and serves as a symbol of sacrifice in the line of duty. She's been promoted to Captain, commanding a company of sixty Lightbringers.

At forty-two, she's considered a rising star in the order—young enough to have decades of service ahead, experienced enough to have earned respect. Some whisper she might eventually challenge for the Iron Council, though she claims no such ambition.

### Connections
- **Lord Commander Gareth Lightbane:** Her superior, who she respects but sometimes questions
- **Brother Tormund:** Spiritual advisor who helped her through recovery after losing her arm
- **The Tomb Survivors:** Six others who share a bond forged in horror
- **Sister Elena:** Fellow captain and closest friend, stationed in a distant chapter house
- **Captain Borin Stoneshield:** Colleague in Kaer Thandros, fellow pragmatist

### Secrets
1. **The Tomb's Voice:** Something from the Tomb of Shadows still whispers to her sometimes. She's told no one, fearing they'll think her corrupted.
2. **Doubts About Gareth:** Questions some of the Lord Commander's decisions but lacks evidence of actual wrongdoing.
3. **The Survivor's Secret:** The seven survivors made a pact to never speak of exactly what they saw in the tomb's deepest chambers.
4. **Prosthetic Limitations:** The arm malfunctions occasionally, especially near strong undead. She hides this.
5. **Personal Vow:** Swore to eventually return and destroy what's in the tomb, when she's powerful enough.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Whispers Return:** The voice from the tomb is getting louder, saying something important.
2. **Survivor's Reunion:** One of the other survivors has been acting strangely. Investigation needed.
3. **The Return:** She's finally ready to go back to the Tomb of Shadows. She needs a capable team.
4. **Gareth's Orders:** She's been given orders she finds troubling. Obey or investigate?
5. **Arm's Secret:** The prosthetic has started glowing near certain locations. What is it detecting?


### Equipment
- **Armor:** Plate Armor +1 (gleaming silver with sun symbol, blessed by Saint Celestine)
- **Shield:** Shield +1 (steel, emblazoned with Iron Council sigil)
- **Weapon:** Dawnbreaker (Legendary longsword +2, see above, formerly Paladin Radiant's blade)
- **Secondary:** 3 javelins (silvered)
- **Holy Symbol:** Silver sun pendant (acts as spell focus)
- **Ring:** Ring of Protection +1 (already included in AC)
- **Cloak:** Cloak of Protection (white with gold trim, advantage vs. effects)
- **Gauntlets:** Gauntlets of Ogre Power (Str 18, already included)
- **Belt:** Belt of Dwarvenkind (Con +2, darkvision 60 ft., poison resistance)
- **Potions:** 3 potions of greater healing, 1 potion of heroism
- **Documents:** Iron Council authorization papers, letters of introduction
- **Other:** Prayer book, healer's kit, tent, rations

### Physical Description
Tall and athletic (5'10", 165 lbs) with a commanding presence. Long auburn hair usually worn in a practical braid. Bright green eyes that shine with conviction. Wears gleaming silvered plate armor that's clearly well-maintained. A faint golden radiance surrounds her, especially noticeable in dim light. Dawnbreaker sword is always at her side, the blade catching light even in shadow. Moves with grace despite heavy armor. Has a small scar on her chin from training accident. Stands straight with natural authority - clearly someone used to being obeyed.

### Personality Traits
- Speaks with conviction and passion
- Makes direct eye contact, hard to look away
- Touches her holy symbol when praying (often)
- Radiates warmth and hope
- Quick to defend the innocent
- Struggles visibly with moral gray areas

**Ideals:**
- **Justice:** "The law must protect all equally, from peasant to king."
- **Redemption:** "Even the fallen can rise again if they choose to."
- **Duty:** "I serve something greater than myself - that's what gives life meaning."

**Bonds:**
- The Iron Council and its ideals
- Dawnbreaker (Paladin Radiant's legacy)
- Her paladin order
- The innocent and downtrodden
- Her secret love (complicated political situation)

**Flaws:**
- Sometimes too idealistic
- Struggles with moral complexity
- Can be manipulated through her compassion
- Overworks herself
- Secretly doubts her worthiness of Dawnbreaker

### Roleplaying Notes
- Glows brighter when emotional
- Grips sword hilt when uncertain
- Kneels to pray before major decisions
- Speaks in inspirational phrases
- Can't tell convincing lies

**Campaign Role:**
**Primary Function:** Righteous quest-giver, divine support, moral compass

**Quest Types:**
1. **Justice:** "Corrupt officials must be exposed and tried"
2. **Protection:** "Innocents threatened - provide sanctuary"
3. **Redemption:** "Fallen paladin seeks to make amends - supervise"
4. **Purification:** "Unholy site must be consecrated"
5. **Investigation:** "Evil hidden among nobility - unmask it"

**Special Abilities:**
- Can cast *zone of truth* at will
- Divine sense detects Unbound corruption
- Aura grants immunity to fear (30 ft. radius)
- Can resurrect fallen allies (once per week)
- Dawnbreaker glows near betrayers

**Rewards & Support:**
- Healing and resurrection services
- Divine blessings and consecrations
- Safe havens in Iron Council temples
- Letters of authority (legal backing)
- Training in paladin techniques
- Spiritual guidance

**Character Arc:**
- Starts believing in absolute good vs evil
- Learns about moral complexity (Lord Shadows's legitimate grievances)
- Struggles with whether redemption possible for Unbound
- Eventually finds balance between justice and mercy
- Key ally in final confrontation
- May offer redemption path to Lord Shadows

**Secrets & Knowledge:**
1. Iron Council has corruption too
2. Paladin Radiant's spirit guides her sometimes
3. She's destined to face Lich of Raven's Keep
4. Secretly dating someone from "wrong" faction
5. Questions whether reunification is justice or conquest

**Connections:**
- Wields Paladin Radiant Dawnbringer's sword
- Coordinates with Archmage Veridian
- Reports to Iron Council leadership
- Knows Saint Celestine can manifest through her
- Works with Admiral Marcus Truewind

## Sage Cornelius the Elder
**"History doesn't repeat, but it certainly rhymes. And these verses sound familiar."**

**Status:** ALIVE - Ancient Historian, Worldrend Expert  
**CR:** 10 (Scholar with vast knowledge and magical protections)  
**Race:** Human (magically extended life)  
**Age:** 189 years old  

### Stat Block
```
Medium Humanoid (Human), Neutral Good

Armor Class: 14 (17 with mage armor and ring)
Hit Points: 99 (18d8 + 18)
Speed: 25 ft. (reduced by age)

STR: 8 (-1)  DEX: 12 (+1)  CON: 12 (+1)
INT: 22 (+6)  WIS: 20 (+5)  CHA: 14 (+2)

Saving Throws: Int +10, Wis +9
Skills: Arcana +14, History +18, Insight +9, Investigation +14, Perception +9, Religion +10
Damage Resistances: Psychic (from years of study)
Senses: Passive Perception 19
Languages: Common, Elvish, Dwarvish, Draconic, Ancient Common, Celestial, Infernal, Primordial
Challenge Rating: 10 (5,900 XP)

SPECIAL ABILITIES:
Spellcasting: 10th-level wizard (Divination school). Spell save DC 18, +10 to hit with spell attacks.

Spells Prepared:
Cantrips (at will): Guidance (special), Light, Mage Hand, Message
1st level (4 slots): Comprehend Languages, Detect Magic, Identify, Mage Armor*
2nd level (3 slots): Augury, Locate Object, See Invisibility
3rd level (3 slots): Clairvoyance, Counterspell, Tongues
4th level (3 slots): Arcane Eye, Divination
5th level (2 slots): Legend Lore, Scrying
*Always active

Living Library: Has perfect memory of every text he's read (over 20,000 books). Can recall any historical fact with perfect accuracy. Advantage on all Intelligence checks related to history.

Pattern Recognition: After observing an event or situation for 1 minute, can predict likely outcomes with uncanny accuracy. DM should provide hints about consequences.

Prophetic Insight: Once per day, can ask DM one yes/no question about the future. DM must answer truthfully based on current trajectory (though actions can change outcome).

Extended Life: Through magical means, has lived far beyond natural lifespan. Ages at 1/10 normal rate. Fragile but mentally sharp.

Protective Wards: His tower has permanent Alarm, Glyph of Warding, and Magic Circle spells protecting it.

ACTIONS:
Walking Staff: Melee Weapon Attack: +3 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
Hit: 1d6-1 bludgeoning damage. (He's not a combatant)

Cast a Spell: Casts a prepared spell.

Share Knowledge (Special): Can spend 10 minutes teaching an ally. That ally gains advantage on one specific type of check (chosen when teaching) for 24 hours.

REACTIONS:
Scholarly Insight: When an ally within 60 ft. makes an Intelligence, Wisdom, or Charisma check, Cornelius can use reaction to add +5 to their roll (3/day).

Counterspell: Attempts to counter a spell being cast.

LEGENDARY ACTIONS (3 per round, represents his vast knowledge):
- Recall: Makes an Intelligence check to remember a crucial fact.
- Advise: Grants one ally within 60 ft. advantage on their next ability check.
- Prophesy (Costs 2): Makes a prediction. DM provides hint about immediate danger or opportunity.
- Cast Spell (Costs 3): Casts a spell of 3rd level or lower.
```

### Background & History
Cornelius has been ancient for as long as anyone can remember. Records from a hundred years ago describe him as "the elderly sage Cornelius," and records from two hundred years ago say the same thing. Either he's found a way to extend his life considerably, or there have been multiple people using the name. He claims the former.

His specialty is ancient civilizations—not the recent ancient, but the truly old. Pre-Worldrend cultures, the Primordials, the First Age. He reads languages no one else can identify, recognizes artifacts others dismiss as rocks, and occasionally references events from millennia ago as if he'd witnessed them.

He holds no official position but is consulted by every major institution. The Arcanum keeps a permanent guest chamber for him. The Free Cities Alliance seeks his advice on archaeological policy. Noble houses hire him to authenticate relics. He charges nothing for his services but accepts donations to fund further research.

His current residence is a cluttered tower on the outskirts of Silverpine, filled with artifacts, scrolls, and things that move when you're not looking directly at them.

### Connections
- **Professor Miranda Questseeker:** Occasional collaborator, though they disagree on methodology
- **Archmage Veridian Starweaver:** Old friend—how old, neither will say
- **Merchant Princess Yasmin:** She brings him artifacts; he tells her their histories
- **The Circle of Eight:** Denies any connection but seems suspiciously well-informed about their activities
- **Nobody knows his family:** He deflects all personal questions with practiced ease

### Secrets
1. **True Age:** He is over eight hundred years old, sustained by a combination of elven blood (he's one-quarter elf), alchemical treatments, and a binding to a genius loci that anchors his life force.
2. **The Worldrend Witness:** He was alive during the Worldrend. He knows what caused it—and who.
3. **The Burden:** His knowledge of history includes things that must remain secret for civilization's safety. This burden weighs heavily.
4. **Multiple Identities:** Has lived under dozens of names throughout history, each with its own documented life and death.
5. **The Anchor's Price:** His life-sustaining connection requires a yearly ritual that he finds increasingly distasteful.

### Plot Hooks
1. **The Critical History:** Something from his knowledge is suddenly relevant. He needs help acting on information he's kept secret for centuries.
2. **The Ritual:** His yearly ritual has been disrupted. Without it, he'll begin aging rapidly.
3. **Identity Exposed:** Someone has connected his various historical identities. What do they want?
4. **Succession:** He's finally contemplating death. Time to pass on his knowledge—but to whom?
5. **The Worldrend Truth:** Events are unfolding that relate to what caused the original catastrophe.


### Equipment
- **Robes:** Simple scholar's robes (worn, ink-stained)
- **Staff:** Ancient walking staff (mundane, needed for mobility)
- **Ring:** Ring of Protection +2
- **Amulet:** Amulet of Proof Against Detection and Location
- **Spectacles:** Special reading glasses (can read in any lighting)
- **Spellbook:** "Chronicles of the Worldrend" - His life's work, contains all his spells plus extensive historical notes
- **Maps:** Detailed maps of both continents (including pre-Worldrend versions)
- **Documents:** Partial World-Splitter schematics, Worldrend trigger points map
- **Library:** Personal collection of 20,000+ books in his tower
- **Potions:** 2 potions of longevity, 3 potions of healing
- **Communication:** Crystal ball for remote consultations

### Physical Description
Extremely old and frail (5'8", 120 lbs), appears ancient but eyes are sharp and clear. Long white hair and beard, both neatly trimmed. Deeply wrinkled face marked by decades of study. Wears simple brown robes covered in ink stains and aged parchment dust. Thick spectacles magnify intelligent hazel eyes. Moves slowly with walking staff, but mind is lightning-quick. Hands shake slightly but writing is still precise. Smells of old books, candle wax, and parchment.

### Personality Traits
- Speaks urgently, as if time is running out (it might be)
- References historical parallels constantly
- Patient teacher despite internal panic
- Frustrated when ignored or dismissed
- Treats mistakes as learning opportunities
- Touches forehead when concentrating

**Ideals:**
- **Knowledge:** "History must be preserved so mistakes aren't repeated."
- **Warning:** "Those who ignore the past are condemned to repeat it."
- **Legacy:** "My knowledge must outlive me."

**Bonds:**
- His library (life's work)
- Professor Miranda (favorite student)
- Preventing Second Worldrend (obsession)
- The truth about history
- Future generations

**Flaws:**
- Sometimes seems paranoid (but he's usually right)
- Fragile health limits mobility
- Frustrated by political inaction
- Workaholic despite age
- Fears dying before sharing crucial knowledge

### Roleplaying Notes
- Constantly references historical events
- Makes prophetic statements that seem odd until later
- Taps staff when impatient
- Adjusts spectacles habitually
- Mutters dates and names under breath

**Campaign Role:**
**Primary Function:** Lore expert, prophecy interpreter, warning system

**Quest Types:**
1. **Research:** "Verify this historical account's accuracy"
2. **Retrieval:** "Specific text confirms my theory - find it"
3. **Investigation:** "Event matches Worldrend precursor - investigate"
4. **Warning:** "Settlement in danger based on patterns - evacuate them"
5. **Protection:** "Unbound assassin targeting me - I must survive to share knowledge"

**Critical Knowledge:**
- Detailed timeline of First Worldrend
- Warning signs appearing now
- Unbound's true ultimate goal
- How original Worldrend was triggered
- Potential ways to prevent Second Worldrend
- Location of World-Splitter weapon

**Information He Provides:**
**Early Campaign:** Fragmented warnings, seems paranoid
**Mid Campaign:** Patterns become clear, proves accuracy
**Late Campaign:** Precise predictions, prevention methods
**Climax:** Crucial knowledge for stopping Second Worldrend

**Rewards:**
- Historical context for party's discoveries
- Advance warning of dangers
- Interpretation of prophecies and omens
- Letters of introduction to other scholars
- Access to his library (20,000 volumes)
- Eventually: location of game-changing artifact

**Character Arc:**
- Dismissed as paranoid old scholar
- Predictions start coming true
- Becomes crucial ally
- May sacrifice himself to delay/prevent Worldrend
- Or survives to document party's heroism

**Secrets:**
1. Witnessed precursor event as child (trauma)
2. Has map showing Worldrend's trigger points
3. Knows Unbound's ritual requirements
4. Possesses partial World-Splitter schematics
5. Has been warning royalty for decades (ignored)

**Connections:**
- Former mentor to Professor Miranda
- Corresponds with Hermit Sage Morganna
- Knows Archmage Veridian (mutual respect)
- Has read Sage Elminster's research
- Aware of Frost Seer's prophecies (confirms them)
